I the Feaderes ant i the Sunes ant i the Hali Gastes nome her biginneth Ancrene Wisse 
Al thet gode religiuse doth other werieth efter the uttre riwle al 
togedere is hervore al nis bute ase tole to timbrin hertowart Al nis bute as thuften to 
servi the leafdi to riwlin the heorte 
This an boc is todealet in eahte leasse bokes 
Nu mine leove sustren this boc ich todeale on eahte destinctiuns thet ye cleopieth 
 dalen Ant euch withute monglunge speketh al bi himseolf of sunderliche thinges ant 
thah euchan riht falleth efter other ant is the leatere eaver iteiet to the earre 
 The earste dale speketh al of ower servise 
 The other is hu ye schulen thurh ower fif wittes witen ower heorte thet ordre ant 
religiun ant sawle lif is inne I this destinctiun aren chapitres five as fif stuchen efter fif 
wittes the witeth the heorte as wakemen hwerse ha beoth treowe ant speketh of 
euch wit sunderlepes o rawe 
 The thridde dale is of anes cunnes fuheles the Davith i the Sawter eveneth himseolf 
to as he were ancre ant hu the cunde of the ilke fuheles beoth ancren iliche 
 The feorthe dale is of fleschliche fondunges ant gasteliche bathe ant confort ayeines 
ham ant of hare salven 
The fifte dale is of schrift 
The seste dale is of penitence 
The seovethe of schir heorte hwi me ah ant hwi me schal Jesu Crist luvien ant 
hwet binimeth us his luve ant let us him to luvien 
The eahtuthe dale is al of the uttre riwle earst of mete ant of drunch ant of othre 
thinges thet falleth therabuten th refter of the thinges the ye mahen undervon ant hwet 
thinges ye mahen witen other habben th refter of ower clathes ant of swucche thinges 
as therabuten falleth th refter of ower werkes of doddunge ant of blodletunge of 
ower meidnes riwle aleast hu ye ham schulen leofliche learen 

Her biginneþ þe earste boc of ures ant ureisuns þe gode beoþ to seggen 
Hwen ye earst ariseþ blesciþ ow ant seggeþ Ant biginneþ anan 
wiþ up ahevene ehnen ant honden toward heovene buhinde o cneon forþ
ward upo þe bedde ant seggeþ swa al þe ymne ut wiþ þe verset ant te ureisun Herefter scheoiende ow ant claþinde 
ow seggeþ ant þis word seggeþ eaver aþet ye beon 
al greiþe þis word habbeþ muchel on us ant i muþ ofte euch time þet ye mahen 
sitten ye oþer stonden 
Hwen ye beoþ al greiþe sprengeþ ow wiþ haliweater þet ye schulen eaver 
habben ant þenchen o Godes flesch ant on his deorewurþe blod þet is abuve þe 
hehe weoved ant falleþ adun þertowart wiþ þeose gretunges 
Alswa ye schule don hwen þe preost halt hit up ed te measse ant bivore þe 
hwen ye schule beon ihuslet Efter þis falleþ o cneon to ower crucifix wiþ þeose fif 
gretunges ine munegunge of Godes fif wunden 
Ant wiþ þis word beateþ on ower breoste 
Hwase ne con þeos five segge þe earste cneolinde fif siþen ant 
blesciþ ow wiþ euchan of þeose gretunges Ant wiþ þeose wordes beateþ ower heorte ant cusseþ þe eorþe icruchet 
wiþ þe þume þe refter wendeþ ow to ure Leafdi onlicnesse ant cneoliþ wiþ fif aleast to þe oþre ymagnes ant to ower relikes luteþ oþer cneoliþ nomeliche 
to þe halhen þe ye habbeþ to þurh luve iturnd ower weofdes swa muche þe reaþere 
yef ei is ihalhet 
þerefter ananriht ure Leafdi uhtsong ant seggeþ o þis wise yef hit is werc
dei falleþ to þer eorþe yef hit is halidei buhinde sumdeal duneward seggeþ ant ba stille Rihteþ ow up þe refter ant seggeþ Makieþ on ower muþ a creoiz wiþ þe þume Ed a 
large creoiz wiþ þe þume ant wiþ þe twa fingres from buve þe forheaved dun to 
þe breoste ant falleþ to þe eorþe yef hit is wercdei wiþ oþer 
buheþ duneward yef hit is halidei aþet þus ed euch ant 
ed te biginnunge of þe ant i þe ed ant ed te ant hwerse ye eaver hereþ Maries nome inempnet ant ed euch 
þet falle to ower ures ant to þe ant to þe collecte ed eavereuch tide ant ed te 
leatemeste vers of eavereuch ymne ant ed te leaste vers wiþuten an of þe salm Ed alle þes ilke yef hit is halidei buheþ 
sumdel dunewart Yef hit is wercdei falleþ to þer eorþe Ed te biginnunge of eaver 
euch tide wiþ makieþ rodetaken as ich ear tahte Ed buheþ oþer cneoliþ efter þet te dei is Wiþ 
falleþ eaver adun ant ed tis word cusseþ þe eorþe 
ant alswa i þe ed tis word ant 
ed te messe i þe muchele ed ant 
Euchan segge hire ures as ha haveþ iwriten ham ant euch tide sunderliche ase 
forþ as ye mahen seggeþ in his time ear to sone þen to leate yef ye ne mahen eaver 
halde þe time Uhtsong bi niht i winter i sumer i þe dahunge þis winter schal 
biginnen ed te HaliRode Dei ine hervest ant leasten aþet Easter Prime in winter earliche 
i sumer bi forþmarhen þe refter Yef ye habbeþ neode for eani hihþe to 
speoken ye muhe seggen hit bivoren ant efter uhtsong anan yef hit swa neodeþ Non 
eaver efter mete ant hwen ye slepeþ efter slep hwil þet sumer leasteþ bute 
hwen ye feasteþ i winter bivore mete hwen ye al veasteþ þe Sunnedei þah efter 
mete for ye eoteþ twien Ed te an salm ye schulen stonden yef ye beoþ eise ant ed te 
oþer sitten ant eaver wiþ rungen up ant buhen Hwase mei stonden al 
on ure Leafdi wurþschipe stonde o Godes halve Ed alle þe seove tiden singeþ ant ba bivoren ant efter efter euch tide bivore þe Ed þreo tiden seggeþ wiþ bivoren uhtsong ant 
efter prime ant efter complie from ower complie aþet efter haldeþ silence 
Efter evensong anan ower euche niht seggeþ hwen ye beoþ eise bute hit 
beo hali niht for feaste of nihe lesceuns þe cume ine marhen bivore cumplie oþer efter 
uhtsong wiþ þreo salmes ant wiþ þreo lesceuns euche niht sundri In 
aniversaries of ower leoveste freond seggeþ alle nihene I stude of ed euch 
psalmes ende Ed sitteþ aþet alswa ed bute ed te lesceuns ant ed te 
ant from al ut i stude of seggeþ on 
ende Ine marhen oþer i niht efter þe suffragies of uhtsong seggeþ commendaciun 
sittinde þe salmes cneolinde þe ureisuns oþer stondinde Yef ye þus doþ euche niht 
bute ane Sunneniht ye doþ muche betere In ameldei we seggeþ ba ant efter þe metegraces I twimeldei efter non ant ye alswa mote don 
Seove psalmes seggeþ sittinde oþer cneolinde wiþ þe letanie Fiftene psalmes 
seggeþ o þis wise þe earste five for owseolf ant for alle þe ow god doþ oþer 
unnen þe oþre five for þe peis of al Hali Chirche þe þridde five for alle Cristene 
sawles Efter þe forme five Efter þe oþre five alswa Efter þe þridde five þe ye schulen seggen wiþuten Seove salmes ant þus 
þeose fiftene seggeþ abuten under for abute swuch time as me singeþ measse in alle 
religiuns ant ure Laverd þolede pine upo þe rode ye ahen to beo nomeliche i beoden 
ant i bonen ant alswa from prime aþet midmarhen hwen preostes of þe worlt singeþ 
hare meassen Ye mahen yef ye wulleþ seggen ower þis wise 
 Almihti Godd Feader Sune Hali Gast as ye beoþ þreo an Godd alswa ye beoþ 
an mihte an wisdom ant an luve ant þah is mihte iturnd to þe in Hali Writ nomeliche 
þu deorewurþe Feader to þe wisdom seli Sune to þe luve Hali Gast Yef me an 
almihti Godd þrile i þreo hades þes ilke þreo þinges mihte forte servi þe wisdom 
forte cweme þe luve ant wil to don hit mihte þet ich mahe don wisdom þet ich 
cunne don luve þet ich wulle don aa þet te is leovest As þu art ful of euch god 
alswa nis na god wone þeras þeose þreo beoþ mihte ant wisdom ant luve iveiet 
togederes þet tu yetti me ham Hali þrumnesse i þe wurþschipe of þe þreo hwase hit haveþ oþer sum oþer of þe hali

 A Jesu þin are Jesu for mine sunnen ahonget o rode for þe ilke fif wunden þe þu 
on hire bleddest heal mi blodi sawle of alle þe sunnen þet ha is wiþ iwundet þurh mine 
fif wittes I þe munegunge of ham þet hit swa mote beon deorewurþe Laverd Fif yef þu const oþer of þe creoiz sum oþer þis is an of 
þe beste 
 For þe seove yiftes of þe Hali Gast þet ich ham mote habben ant for þe seove tiden 
þet Hali Chirche singeþ þet ich deale in ham slepe ich oþer wakie ant for þe seove 
bonen i þe ayein þe seoven heaved ant deadliche sunnen þet tu wite me 
wiþ ham ant alle hare brokes ant yeove me þe seovene selie eadinesses þe þu havest 
Laverd bihaten þine icorene i þin eadi nome Seove 
 For þe ten heastes þe ich ibroken habbe summe oþer alle ant meseolven 
towart te hwetse beo of oþerhwet untreoweliche iteoheþet i bote of þeose bruchen 
forte sahtni me wiþ þe deorewurþe Laverd Ten I þe wurþgunge Jesu Crist of þine tweof apostles þet 
ich mote overal folhin hare lare þet ich mote habben þurh hare bonen þe tweolf 
bohes þe bloweþ of chearite as Seinte Pawel writeþ blisfule Laverd Tweolf

 Leafdi Seinte Marie for þe ilke muchele blisse þet tu hefdest inwiþ þe i þet ilke 
time þet Jesu Godd Godes sune efter þe engles gretunge nom flesch ant blod in þe 
ant of þe underfeng mi gretunge wiþ þe ilke ant make me telle lutel of euch blisse 
utewiþ ah frovre me inwiþ ant ernde me þeo of heovene Ant ase wis as i þe ilke 
flesch þet he toc of þe nes neaver sunne ne i þin as me leveþ efter þe ilke 
tacunge hwetse bivore were clense mi sawle of fleschliche sunnen Biginne þe aþet as me biginneþ antefne ant tenne þe salm ant efter þe 
salm al ut fif siþen ant þus to euch salm al ut fif siþen

 Leafdi Seinte Marie for þe ilke muchele blisse þet tu hefdest þa þu sehe þi deore 
deorewurþe sune efter his derve deaþ arisen to blisful lif his bodi sevevalt brihtre

libben dealen in his pinen feolahliche in eorþe forte beon i blisse his feolahe in

muchele sorhe efter mi sorhe þet ich am in her lead me to þi blisse fif siþen

Her biginneþ þe oþer dale of þe heorte warde þurh þe fif wittes 
 Wiþ alles cunnes 
warde dohter seiþ Salomon wite wel þin heorte for sawle lif is in hire 
 yef ha is wel iloket þe heorte wardeins beoþ þe fif wittes sihþe ant 
herunge smechunge ant smeallunge ant euch limes felunge Ant we schulen speoken 
of alle for hwase wit þeose wel he deþ Salomones bode he wit wel his heorte ant his 
sawle heale þe heorte is a ful wilde beast ant makeþ moni liht lupe As Seint Gregoire 
seiþ Na þing ne etfliþ mon sonre þen his ahne heorte 
Daviþ Godes prophete meande i sum time þet ha wes etsteart him þet is min heorte is edflohe me Ant eft he blisseþ him ant seiþ þet 
ha wes icumen ham Laverd he seiþ min heorte 
is icumen ayein eft Ich hire habbe ifunden Hwense hali mon ant se wis ant se war 
lette hire edstearten sare mei anoþer of hire fluht carien Ant hwer edbrec ha ut from 
Daviþ þe hali king Godes prophete Hwer Godd wat ed his ehþurl þurh a sihþe 
þet he seh þurh a bihaldunge as ye schulen efter iheren 
Forþi mine leove sustren þe leaste þet ye eaver mahen luvieþ ower þurles Alle 
beon ha lutle þe parlurs least ant nearewest þe claþ in ham beo twafald blac þet 
claþ þe cros hwit wiþinnen ant wiþuten þet blake claþ bitacneþ þet ye beoþ 
blake ant unwurþ to þe world wiþuten þet te soþe sunne haveþ utewiþ forculet 
ow ant swa wiþuten as ye beoþ unseowlich imaket ow þurh gleames of his grace 
þe hwite cros limpeþ to ow for þreo crosses beoþ read ant blac ant hwit þe reade 
limpeþ to þeo þe beoþ for Godes luve wiþ hare blodschedunge irudet ant ireadet 
as þe martirs weren þe blake cros limpeþ to þeo þe makieþ i þe worlt hare peni
tence for ladliche sunnen þe hwite limpeþ ariht to hwit meidenhad ant to cleannesse 
þet is muche pine wel forte halden Pine is ihwer þurh cros idon to understonden 
þus bitacneþ hwit cros þe warde of hwit chastete þet is muche pine wel to biwitene 
þe blake claþ alswa teke þe bitacnunge deþ leasse eil to þe ehnen ant is þiccre 
ayein þe wind ant wurse to seon þurh ant halt his heow betere for wind ant for oþer
hwet Lokiþ þet te parlures claþ beo on eavereuch half feaste ant wel itachet ant 
witeþ þer ower ehnen leaste þe heorte edfleo ant wende ut as of Daviþ ant ower 
sawle seccli sone se heo is ute Ich write muchel for oþre þet nawiht ne rineþ ow 
mine leove sustren for nabbe ye nawt te nome ne ne schulen habben þurh þe 
grace of Godd of totilde ancres ne of tollinde locunges ne lates þet summe oþer
hwiles weilawei uncundeliche makieþ For ayein cunde hit is ant unmeaþ sulli 
wunder þet te deade dotie ant wiþ cwike worltmen wede þurh sunne 
 Me leove sire seiþ sum ant is hit nu se overuvel forte totin utwart Ye hit 
leove suster for uvel þe þer kimeþ of hit is uvel ant overuvel to eavereuch ancre 
nomeliche to þe yunge ant to þe alde forþi þet ha to þe yungre yeoveþ uvel 
forbisne ant scheld to werien ham wiþ For yef ei edwit ham þenne seggeþ ha anan 
 Me sire þeo deþ alswa þet is betere þen ich am ant wat betere þen ich hwet ha 
haveþ to donne Leove yunge ancre ofte a ful haher smiþ smeoþeþ a ful wac cnif 
þe wise folhe i wisdom ant nawt i folie An ald ancre mei do wel þet te þu dest uvele 
Ah totin ut wiþuten uvel ne mei ower nowþer Nim nu yeme hwet uvel beo icumen of 
totunge Nawt an uvel ne twa ah al þe wa þet nu is ant eaver yete wes ant eaver 
schal iwurþen al com of sihþe þet hit beo soþ lo her preove 
Lucifer þurh þet he seh ant biheold on himseolf his ahne feiernesse leop into 
prude ant bicom of engel eatelich deovel Of Eve ure alde moder is iwriten on alre 
earst in hire sunne inyong of hire ehsihþe þet is Eve biheold o þe forboden eappel ant 
seh hine feier ant feng to delitin i þe bihaldunge ant toc hire lust þertoward ant nom 
ant et þe rof ant yef hire laverd Low hu Hali Writ spekeþ ant hu inwardliche hit teleþ 
hu sunne bigon þus eode sihþe bivoren ant makede wei to uvel lust ant com þe dede 
þ refter þet al moncun ifeleþ 
þes eappel leove suster bitacneþ alle þe þing þet lust falleþ to ant delit of sunne 
Hwen þu bihaldest te mon þu art in Eve point þu lokest o þe eappel Hwase hefde 
iseid to Eve þa ha weorp earst hire ehe þe ron A Eve Went te awei þu warpest 
ehe o þi deaþ Hwet hefde ha iondsweret Me leove sire þu havest woh Hwerof 
chalengest tu me þe eappel þet ich loki on is forbode me to eotene ant nawt to 
bihalden þus walde Eve inohreaþe habben iondsweret O mine leove sustren as 
Eve haveþ monie dehtren þe folhiþ hare moder þe ondswerieþ o þisse wise Me 
wenest tu seiþ sum þet ich wulle leapen on him þah ich loki on him Godd wat 
leove suster mare wunder ilomp Eve þi moder leop efter hire ehnen from þe ehe 
to þe eappel from þe eappel i parais dun to þer eorþe from þe eorþe to helle þer 
ha lei i prisun fowr þusent yer ant mare heo ant hire were ba ant demde al hire 
ofsprung to leapen al efter hire to deaþ wiþuten ende Biginnunge ant rote of al þis ilke 
reowþe wes a liht sihþe þus ofte as me seiþ of lutel muchel waxeþ Habbe þenne 
muche dred euch feble wummon hwen þeo þe wes riht ta iwraht wiþ Godes honden 
wes þurh a sihþe biswiken ant ibroht into brad sunne þet al þe world overspreadde A 
meiden Dyna het Jacobes dohter as hit teleþ i Genesy eode ut to bihalden uncuþe 
wummen yet ne seiþ hit nawt þet ha biheold wepmen Ant hwet come wenest tu 
of þet bihaldunge Ha leas hire meidenhad ant wes imaket hore þe refter of þet ilke 
weren trowþen tobrokene of hehe patriarches ant a muchel burh forbearnd ant te 
king ant his sune ant te burhmen islein þe wummen ilead forþ hire feader ant hire 
breþren se noble princes as ha weren utlahen imakede þus eode ut hire sihþe Al 
þullich þe Hali Gast lette writen o boc forte warni wummen of hare fol ehnen Ant 
nim þerof yeme þet tis uvel of Dyna com nawt of þet ha seh Sichen Emores 
sune þet ha sunegede wiþ ah dude of þet ha lette him leggen ehnen on hire for þet 
tet he dude hire wes i þe frumþe sare hire unþonkes 
Alswa Bersabee þurh þet ha unwreah hire i Daviþes sihþe ha dude him sunegin 
on hire se hali king as he wes ant Godes prophete Nu kimeþ forþ a feble mon halt 
him þah ahelich yef he haveþ a wid hod ant a loke cape ant wule iseon yunge ancres 
ant loki nede ase stan hu hire wlite him liki þe naveþ nawt hire leor forbearnd i þe 
sunne ant seiþ ha mei baldeliche iseon hali men ye swucche as he is for his wide 
sleven Me surquide sire ne herest tu þet Daviþ Godes ahne deorling bi hwam he 
seolf seide Ich habbe ifunden quoþ he 
 mon efter min heorte þes þe Godd seolf seide bi þis deorewurþe sahe king ant 
prophete icuret of alle þes þurh an ehewurp to a wummon as ha wesch hire lette ut 
his heorte ant foryet himseolven swa þet he dude þreo utnume heaved ant deadliche 
sunnen o Bersabees spusbruche þe leafdi þet he lokede on treisun ant monslaht on 
his treowe cniht Urie hire laverd Ant tu a sunful mon art se swiþe hardi to keasten 
cang ehnen upo yung wummon Ye mine leove sustren yef ei is anewil to seon ow 
ne wene ye þer neaver god ah leveþ him þe leasse Nulle ich þet nan iseo ow bute 
he habbe of ower meistre spetiale leave For alle þe þreo sunnen þet ich spec of least 
ant al þet uvel of Dina þet ich spec of herre al com nawt forþi þet te wummen 
lokeden cangliche o wepmen ah for heo unwriyen heom in monnes echsiþþe ant 
duden hwarþurch ha machten fallen in sunne 
Forþi wes ihaten on Godes laye þet put were iwriyen eaver ant yef ani were 
unwriyen ant beast feolle þerin he þe unwreah þe put hit schulde yelden þis is a 
swiþe dredful word to wummon þet schaweþ hire to wepmones echne Heo is bitacned 
bi þeo þet unwriþ þe put þe put is hire feire neb hire hwite swire hire lichte 
echnen hond yef ha halt forþ in his echyesihþe Yet beoþ hire word put bute ha 
beon þe bet iset Al yet þe feayeþ hire hwetse hit eaver beo þurch hwat machte 
sonre fol luve awacnin al ure Laverd put cleopeþ þis put he hat þet beo ilided 
þet beast þe rin ne falle ant druncni in sunne 
Best is þe beastlich mon þet ne þenchet naut on God ne ne noteþ naut his wit as 
mon ach to donne ach secheþ for to fallen in þis put þet ich spec of yef he hit open 
fint Ach þe dom is ful strong to þeo þe þe put unlideþ For heo schal yelde þe best 
þet þe rin biþ ifallen ha is witi of his deaþ biforen ure Laverd ant schal for his saule 
ondsweren an Domesdei ant yelde þe bestes lure hwenne ha navet oþer yeld þenne 
hireseolven Strong yeld is her mid alle Ant Godes dom is ant his heste þet heo hit 
yelde allegate for heo unlidede þe put þet hit adrong inne 
þu þet unwrisd þis put þu þet dest ani þing þurch hwet mon is of þe fleschliche 
ifonded þach þu hit nute naut dred þis dom swiþe Ant yef he is ifonded swa 
þet he sunege deadliche on ani wise þach hit ne beo naut wiþ þe bute wiþ wil 
toward þe oþer yef he secheþ to fullen ed sum oþer þe fondunge þet of þe þurch 
þi dede awacnede beo al siker of þe dom þu schalt yelde þe best for þe puttes 
openunge ant buten þu beo iscrive þerof acorien his sunne Hund wule in bluþelich 
hwarse he fint open þet þe muþ ne mei 
for scheome þe licht echye spekeþ hit ant is as erendebeorere of þe lichte heorte 
Ach nu is sum wummon þe nalde for nan þing wilni fulþe to mon ant þach ne rochte 
ha neaver þach he þochte toward hire ant were of hire ifondet Ant nu deþ Sein 
Austin ba twa þeos in a cuple wilnin ant habbe wil forto beon iwilned Yirni mon oþer habbe wil forto 
beon iyirned of mon ba is haved sunne þe echnen 
beoþ þe forme arewen of lecheries prickes Alswa ase men worreþ mid þreo cunes 
wepnes wiþ scheotung ant wiþ speres ord ant wiþ sweordes egge al richt wiþ þilke 
wepnen þet is wiþ schute of eche wiþ spere of wundinde word wiþ sweord of 
deadlich hond werreþ lecherie þe stinkinde hore upon þe lavedi chastete þet is 
Godes spuse Earest scheot þe arewen of þe licht echnen þe fleoþ lichtliche forþ ase 
flaa þet is iviþered ant stikeþ i þere heorte þerefter schakeþ hire spere ant neolachet 
upon hire ant mid schakinde word yeveþ speres wunde 
Sweordes dunt is dunricht þet is þe hondlunge for sweord smit of nech ant 
yeveþ deaþes dunt ant hit is weilawei nech ido wiþ ham þe cumeþ swa nech 
togederes þet ouþer hondli oþer oþer ifele oþer Hwase is wis ant seli wiþ þe 
schute wite hire þet is wite hire echnen For al þet uvel þerefter kimeþ of þe echne 
arewen Ant nis ha muche chang oþer to folhardi þe hald hire heved baltliche ut of 
þe opene carnel hwil me wiþ quarreus utewiþ assailleþ þe castel Sikerliche ure fa 
þe werreur of helle he scheot as ich wene ma quarreus to an ancre þenne to seovene 
ant fifti lavedis i þe worlde þe carneus of þe castel beoþ hire husþurles 
 As deþ com seiþ Sein Bernard into þe world þorch sunne asswa 
deaþ þurch þeos echþurles haveþ inyong to þe saule Laverd Crist as men walden 
steoke feste uh þurl of hire hus for hwon þet heo machten bisteoken deaþ þe rute 
ant an ancre nule naut tunen hire eilþurl ayein þe deaþ of saule Ant mid good richt 
muyen ha beon ihaten eilþurles for ha habbeþ idon muchel eil to moni ancre Al holi writ is ful of warningge of eie  
 Laverd he seiþ David went awei min echnen from þe worldes dweole Ich abbe ifestned 
foreward seiþ Job mid min echnen þet ich ne misþenche Hu dele þencheþ me 
mid echye God hit wat he seiþ wel for efter þe echye kimeþ þe þocht ant þerefter 
þe dede þet wiste wel Jeremie þet mende þus Weilawei he seiþ min eche 
haveþ irobbed al min saule Hwenne Godes prophete makede þulli mon of eche 
hwic man wenest þu þet beo icumen to moni mon ant to moni wumman sorege 
of heore echye þe wise askiþ hweþer ani þing harmi mare wimmon þenne deþ hire 
echye Al þe 
leor he seiþ schal floyen of teres for þe ehesichþe ane þis is nu of þis wit i
noch iseid to warni þe seli We schulen þauh sone herefter speken herof more  
Ore pur ceo toutes les overtures de toutes voz fenestres ausi come ci devant a la 
vewe de touz hommes unt este closes ausi soient ca en apres Et si plus fermement 
poient plus fermement soient closes Generale reule est toutes celes qe bien les closent 
Dieu bien les garde Et toutes celes qe issi qil pecche funt ensement pecchier 
ou od fol oil ou od bouche ou od main et cel od plus et multes tieles choses 
desavenantes et desnatureles a recluse sur toutes Les queux ne fuissent james avant 
venues si ele eust sa fenestre ferm estoppee Et si nule contredit ceste jeo treis a 
testmoigne sa conscience demeyne encontre lui qele parmi sa fenestre demeine ad oil 
ou bouche ou main receu et fole parole oveqe tout fut ele adubbe et od feinte seintete 
falsement coloree A tricheour traitre Dieu jeo nel faz a vous pur nul mal ne pur 
nule ordure dit il ou ele Et od cel meismes se soillent et coroucent les oilz dampne 
Dieu qi regarde la traisun inwiþ þe gale heorte Nawt ane euch fleschlich 
hondlunge ah yetten euch gal word is ladlich vilainie ant Godes grome wurþe þah hit 
ne weoxe forþre bitweone mon ant ancre Nu þurh riht Godes wrake geaþ hit forþre 
ant forþre ant bikimeþ ofte ant ear me least wene into þet fule sunne We hit habbeþ 
weilawei iherd of inohe Ne leve namon ancre þe let in monnes ehe to schawin 
hireseolven Over al þet ye habbeþ iwriten in ower riwle of þinges wiþuten þis 
point þis article of wel to beo bitunde ich wulle beo best ihalden To wummon 
þe wilneþ hit openiþ ow o Godes half Yef ha ne spekeþ nawt þe rof leoteþ swa i
wurþen bute yef ye dreden þet heo þe refter beo iscandlet Of hire ahne suster haveþ 
sum ibeon itemptet In toward ower weoved ne beode ye na mon forte bihalden Ah 
yef his devotiun bit hit ant haveþ grant draheþ ow wel inward ant te veil adun toward 
ower breoste ant sone doþ þe claþ ayein ant festniþ heteveste Yef he lokeþ toward 
bed oþer easkeþ hwer ye liggeþ ondswerieþ lihtliche Sire þerof wel mei duhen 
ant haldeþ ow stille Yef bischop kimeþ to seon ow hihiþ sone towart him ah 
sweteliche bisecheþ him yef he bit to seon ow þet ye moten þeronont halden ow 
towart him as ye habbeþ idon ant doþ to alle oþre Yef he wule allegate habben a 
sihþe lokiþ þet hit beo ful scheort þe veil anan adun ant draheþ ow bihinden An 
ancre wearnde eadmodliche Sein Martin hire sihþe ant he þervore dude hire þe 
menske þet he neaver ne dude to nan oþer Ant hervore hire word is aþet cume þis 
dei iboren in Hali Chirche For as we redeþ of hire hwase wule hire windowes witen 
wel wiþ þe uvele ha mot ec wiþ þe gode Hwense ye moten to eani mon eawiht 
biteachen þe hond ne cume nawt ut ne ower ut ne his in Ant yef hit mot cumen in 
ne rine nowþer oþer Heo is siker seiþ Hali Writ þe feor from grunen draheþ 
hire ant þeo þe luveþ peril i peril ha schal fallen þe deofles grune is ofte itild þer me least 
weneþ Nis nan þet nis dredful þet ha nis ilecchet for Godd nule wite nan þet is se 
folhardi þet ha ne wit wearliche wiþ him hireseolven þis is nu of þis wit inoh i
seid ed tis chearre to warnin þen seli We schulen þah sone herefter speoken herof mare 
Spellunge ant smechunge beoþ i muþ baþe as sihþe is i þe ehe ah we schulen 
leten smechunge aþet we speoken of ower mete ant speoken nu of spellunge ant 
þ refter of herunge of ba imeane sumchearre as ha gaþ togederes 
On alre earst hwen ye schulen to ower parlurs þurl witeþ ed ower meiden hwa hit 
beo þet beo icumen For swuch hit mei beon þet ye schule essinien ow Hwen ye alles 
moten forþ crossiþ ful yeorne muþ ehnen ant earen ant te breoste mid al ant gaþ 
forþ mid Godes dred To preost on earst ant þe refter þet 
he ah to seggen Hercniþ hise wordes ant haldeþ ow al stille þet hwen he parteþ 
from ow þet he ne cunne ower god ne ower uvel nowþer ne ne cunne ow nowþer 
lastin ne preisin Sum is se wel ilearet oþer se wis iwordet þet ha walde he wiste hit 
þe sit ant spekeþ toward hire ant yelt him word ayein word ant forwurþeþ meistre 
þe schulde beon ancre ant leareþ him þet is icumen hire forte learen walde bi hire 
tale beon sone wiþ wise icuþþet ant icnawen Icnawen ha is for þurh þet ilke þet 
ha weneþ to beo wis ihalden he understont þet ha is sot for ha hunteþ efter pris ant 
kecheþ lastunge For ed te alre leaste hwen he is awei iwent þeos ancre he wule 
seggen is of muche speche Eve heold i parais long tale wiþ þe neddre talde him al þe 
lesceun þet Godd hefde ired hire ant Adam of þe eappel ant swa þe feond þurh hire 
word understod ananriht hire wacnesse ant ifond wei toward hire of hire forlorenesse 
Ure Leafdi Seinte Marie dude al on oþer wise Ne talde ha þen engel na tale ah 
easkede him scheortliche þing þet ha ne cuþe Ye mine leove sustren folhiþ ure 
Leafdi ant nawt te cakele Eve Forþi ancre hwetse ha beo hu muchel se ha eaver 
cunne halde hire stille nabbe ha nawt henne cunde þe hen hwen ha haveþ ileid ne 
con bute cakelin ah hwet biyet ha þe rof Kimeþ þe kaue ananriht ant reaveþ hire 
hire eairen ant fret of þet schulde forþ bringe cwike briddes Al riht alswa þe cave 
deovel bereþ awei from cakelinde ancres ant forswolheþ al þe god þet ha istreonet 
habbeþ þet schulde as briddes beoren ham up towart heovene yef hit nere icakelet 
þe wrecche povre peoddere mare nurþ he makeþ to yeien his sape þen þe riche 
mercer al his deorewurþe ware as is iseid herefter To sum gastelich mon þet ye 
beoþ trusti upon as ye mahe beon o lut god is þet ye easki read ant salve þet he 
teache ow toyeines fondunges Ant i schrift schawiþ him yef he wule iheren ower 
greaste ant ower ladlukeste sunnen forþi þet him areowe ow ant þurh þe areownesse 
inwardluker crie Crist mearci for ow ant habbe ow in his bonen Ah witeþ ow ant 
beoþ warre he seiþ ure Laverd for monie cumeþ to ow ischrud mid lombes 
fleos ant beoþ wedde wulves Worltliche leveþ lut religiuse yet leas ne wilni ye 
nawt to muchel hare cuþþunge Eve wiþute dred spec wiþ þe neddre Ure Leafdi 
wes offearet of Gabrieles speche Ure freres prechurs ant ure freres meonurs beoþ of 
swuch ordre þet al folc mahte wundrin yef ei of ham wende ehe towart te wude lehe 
Forþi ed euch time þet eani of ham þurh chearite kimeþ ow to learen ant to frovrin 
i Godd yef he is preost seggeþ ear þen he parti Ich schrive me to Godd 
almihti ant to þe þet ich as ich drede riht repentant neaver nes of mine greaste 
sunnen þet ich habbe ischawet to mine schriftfeaderes Ant tah min entente beo to 
beten ham herinne ich hit do se povreliche ant sunegi in oþre deihwamliche seoþþen 
ich wes nest ischriven ant þet wes þenne ant of þe ant nempnin Ich habbe 
þus isunget Ant segge o hwucche wise as hit is iwriten ow in ower schriftes boc 
towart te ende þe rof Ant aleast seggeþ þis ant muche mare Ant bide 
him undervo þe spetiale in his god ant þonke him of his inturn ant bisech him aleast 
greten þe ant te ant þet ha bidden for þe 
Wiþuten witnesse of wummon oþer of wepmon þe ow mahe iheren ne speoke ye 
wiþ na mon ofte ne longe ant tah hit beo of schrift Allegate i þe ilke hus oþer þer he 
mahe iseon toward ow sitte þe þridde bute yef þe ilke þridde oþer stude trukie 
þis nis nawt for ow leove sustren iseid ne for oþre swucche nawtforþi þe 
treowe is ofte mistrowet ant te saclese bilohen as Josep i Genesy of þe gale leafdi for 
wone of witnesse Me leveþ þe uvele sone ant te unwreaste bliþeliche liheþ o þe 
gode Sum unseli haveþ hwen ha seide ha schraf hire ischriven hire al to wundre 
Forþi ahen þe gode habben eaver witnesse for twa acheisuns nomeliche þe an is 
þet te ondfule ne mahe lihen on ham swa þet te witnesse ne pruvie ham false þe 
oþer is forte yeoven þe oþre forbisne ant reavi þe uvele ancre þe ilke unseli gile þet 
ich of seide 
Ut þurh þe chircheþurl ne halde ye tale wiþ namon ah beoreþ þerto wurþmunt 
for þe hali sacrement þet ye seoþ þerþurh ant neomeþ oþerhwile to ower wummen 
þe huses þurl to oþre þe parlur Speoken ne ahe ye bute ed tes twa þurles 
Silence eaver ed te mete Yef oþre religiuse as ye witen doþ hit ye ahen over alle 
Yef ei haveþ deore geast do hire meidnes as in hire stude to gleadien hire feire Ant heo 
schal habbe leave forte unsperren hire þurl eanes oþer twien ant makie sines toward 
hire of a glead chere Summes curteisie is iturnt hire to uvel Under semblant of god is 
ofte ihulet sunne Ancre ant huses leafdi ah muchel to beon bitweonen Euche Fridei of 
þe yer haldeþ silence bute hit beo duble feaste ant tenne haldeþ hit sum oþer dei i þe 
wike I þe Advenz ant i þe Umbriwiken Weodnesdei ant Fridei i þe lenten þreo 
dahes ant al þe swiingwike aþet non on Easter even To ower wummen ye mahen 
þah seggen wiþ lut word hwetse ye wulleþ Yef eani god mon is of feorren icumen 
hercniþ his speche ant ondswerieþ wiþ lut word to his easkunges 
Muche fol were þe mahte to his bihove hweþer se he walde grinden greot oþer 
hweate yef he grunde þe greot ant lette þe hweate Hweate is hali speche as Seint 
Anselme seiþ Heo grint greot þe chafleþ þe twa cheken beoþ þe twa grindel
stanes þe tunge is þe cleappe Lokiþ leove sustren þet ower cheken ne grinden 
neaver bute sawle fode ne ower eare ne drinke neaver bute sawle heale ant nawt ane 
ower eare ah ower ehþurl sperreþ to ayeines idel speche To ow ne cume na tale 
ne tidinge of þe worlde 
Ye ne schule for na þing wearien ne swerien bute yef ye seggen witerliche oþer 
 sikerliche oþer o sum swuch wise Ne preachi ye to na mon ne mon ne easki ow 
cunsail ne ne telle ow Readeþ wummen ane Seint Pawel forbeot wummen to preachin Na wepmon ne chastie ye ne edwiten him his unþeaw 
bute he beo þe overcuþre Halie alde ancres hit mahe don summes weis ah hit nis 
nawt siker þing ne ne limpeþ nawt to yunge Hit is hare meoster þe beoþ over oþre 
iset ant habbeþ ham to witene as Hali Chirche larewes Ancre naveþ forte loken bute 
hire ant hire meidnes Halde euch hire ahne meoster ant nawt ne reavi oþres Moni 
weneþ to do wel þe deþ al to wundre for as ich seide ear under semblant of god is 
ofte ihulet sunne þurh swuch chastiement haveþ sum ancre arearet bitweonen hire 
ant hire preost oþer a falsinde luve oþer a muche weorre þet is þe 
ende of þe tale seiþ Seneke þe wise ich chulle þet ye speoken seldene ant þenne 
lutel Moni punt hire word forte leote ma ut as me deþ weater ed mulne Swa duden 
Jobes freond þe weren icumen to frovrin him seten stille seoveniht ah þa ha hefden 
alles bigunnen to speokene þa ne cuþen ha neaver stutten hare cleappe Swa hit is of monie as Sein Gregoire seiþ 
 Silence is wordes fostrilt ant bringeþ forþ chaffle On oþer half as he seiþ Long silence ant wel iwist nedeþ þe þohtes up 
towart heovene Alswa as ye mahe seon weater hwen me punt hit ant stoppeþ hit 
bivore wel þet hit ne mahe duneward þenne is hit inedd ayein forte climben uppart 
 ant ye al þisses weis pundeþ ower wordes forstoppiþ ower þohtes as ye wulleþ 
þet ha climben ant hehin toward heovene ant nawt ne fallen duneward ant tofleoten 
yont te worlt as deþ muchel chaffle Hwen ye nede moten a lute wiht lowsiþ up ower 
muþes flodyeten as me deþ ed mulne ant leoteþ adun sone 
Ma sleaþ word þen sweord Lif ant deaþ seiþ 
Salomon is i tunge honden Hwa
se witeþ wel his muþ he witeþ he seiþ his sawle Hwase ne wiþhalt his wordes seiþ Salomon þe wise he 
is as þe burh wiþute wal þet ferde mei in over al þe feond of helle mid his ferd wend 
þurhut te tutel þe is eaver open into þe heorte I hit teleþ þet an hali 
mon seide þa me preisede ane breþren þet he hefde iherd of muche speche Gode quoþ he ha beoþ ah hare wununge naveþ na yete Hare 
muþ meaþeleþ eaver Hwase eaver wule mei gan in ant leaden forþ hare asse 
þet is hare unwise sawle Forþi seiþ Sein Jame þet 
is yef eni weneþ þet he beo religius ant ne bridli nawt his tunge his religiun is fals 
he gileþ his heorte He seiþ swiþe wel ne bridleþ nawt his tunge Bridel nis nawt 
ane i þe horses muþ ah sit sum upo þe ehnen ant geaþ abute þe earen For alle 
þreo is muche neod þet ha beon ibridlet Ah i þe muþ sit tet irn ant o þe lihte tunge 
for þear is meast neod hald hwen þe tunge is o rune ant ifole to eornen 
Ofte we þencheþ hwen we foþ on to speoken forte speoke lutel ant wel isette 
wordes ah þe tunge is slubbri for ha wadeþ i wete ant slit lihtliche forþ from lut 
word into monie Ant tenne as Salomon seiþ 
 Ne mei nawt muche speche ne ginne hit neaver se wel beo wiþute sunne 
For from soþ hit slit to fals ut of god into sum uvel from meosure into unimete ant of 
a drope waxeþ into a muche flod þe adrencheþ þe sawle For wiþ þe fleotinde 
word tofleoteþ þe heorte swa þet longe þe refter ne mei ha beon riht igederet 
togederes 
þis beoþ Seint Gregoires word in his Ase neh as ure muþ is to worldlich 
speche ase feor he is Godd hwen he spekeþ toward him ant bit him eani bone Forþi 
is þet we yeiyeþ upon him ofte ant he firseþ him awei frommard ure stevene ne nule 
nawt iheren hire for ha stinkeþ to him al of þe worldes meaþelunge ant of hire 
chafle Hwase wule þenne þet Godes eare beo neh hire tunge firsi hire from þe 
world elles ha mei longe yeiyen ear Godd hire ihere ant seiþ þurh Ysaie þet is þah ye makien monifalde ower bonen to
ward me ye þe pleieþ wiþ þe world nule ich ow nawt iheren ah ich wulle turne me 
awei hwen ye heoveþ toward me hehe ower honden 
Ure deorewurþe Leafdi Seinte Marie þe ah to alle wummen to beo forbisne wes 
of se lutel speche þet nohwer in Hali Writ ne finde we þet ha spec bute fowr siþen 
ah for se selt speche hire wordes weren hevie ant hefden muche mihte 
 Hire forme wordes þet we redeþ 
of weren þa ha ondswerede Gabriel þen engel ant teo weren se mihtie þet wiþ þet 
ha seide ed tis word 
 Godes sune ant soþ Godd bicom mon ant te Laverd þet al þe world ne mahte nawt 
bifon bitunde him inwiþ hire meidnes wombe Hire oþre wordes weren þa ha com 
ant grette Elyzabeþ hire mehe Ant hwet mihte wes icud ed þeose wordes Hwet 
þet a child bigon to pleien toyeines ham þet wes Sein Juhan in his moder wombe þe þridde time þet ha spec 
þet wes ed te neoces ant ter þurh hire bisocne wes weater iwent to wine þe feorþe 
time wes þa ha hefde imist hire sune ant eft him ifunde Ant hu muche wunder 
folhede þeose wordes þet Godd almihti beah to mon to Marie ant to Joseph to a 
smiþ ant to a wummon ant folhede ham ase heoren hwider se ha walden Neomeþ nu 
her yeme ant leorniþ yeorne herbi hu seltsene speche haveþ muche strengþe Feole iwordet mon seiþ þe Salmwruhte 
 ne schal neaver leaden riht lif on eorþe Forþi he seiþ elleshwer Ypallage ant is as þah he seide Ich 
chulle wite mine weies wiþ mi tunge warde Wite ich wel mi tunge ich mei wel halden 
þe wei toward heovene For as Ysaie seiþ þe tilunge 
of rihtwisnesse þet is silence Silence tileþ hire ant heo itilet bringeþ forþ sawles 
eche fode for ha is undeadlich as Salomon witneþ Forþi 
feieþ Ysaie hope ant silence baþe togederes ant seiþ in ham schal stonden gastelich 
strengþe þet is i silence ant in hope schal 
beon ower strengþe Neomeþ yeme hu wel he seiþ for hwase is muche stille ant 
halt silence longe ha mei hopien sikerliche þet hwen ha spekeþ toward Godd þet he 
hire ihere Ha mei ec hopien þet ha schal singen þurh hire silence sweteliche in heovene 
þis is nu þe reisun of þe veiunge hwi Ysaie veieþ hope ant silence ant cupleþ ba 
togederes Teke þet he seiþ i þe ilke auctorite þet i silence ant in hope schal beon ure 
strengþe i Godes servise toyein þe deofles turnes ant his fondunges Ah lokiþ þurh 
hwet reisun hope is a swete spice inwiþ þe heorte þet sweteþ al þet bitter þet te 
bodi drinkeþ Ah hwase cheoweþ spice ha schal tunen hire muþ þet te swote 
breaþ ant te strengþe þe rof leave wiþinnen Ah heo þe openeþ hire muþ wiþ muche 
meaþelunge ant brekeþ silence ha spit hope al ut ant te swotnesse þe rof mid worltliche 
wordes ant leoseþ ayein þe feond gastelich strengþe For hwet makeþ us stronge i 
Godes servise ant ine fondunges forte drehe derf to wreastli stealewurþliche toyein 
þe deofles swenges bute hope of heh mede Hope halt te heorte hal hwetse þe flesch 
drehe as me seiþ yef hope nere heorte tobreke A Jesu þin are Hu stont ham 
þe beoþ þeras alle wa ant weane is wiþuten hope of utcume ant heorte ne mei 
bersten Forþi as ye wulleþ halden inwiþ ow hope ant te swete breaþ of hire þe 
yeveþ sawle mihte wiþ muþ itunet cheoweþ hire inwiþ ower heorte ne blawe ye 
hire nawt ut wiþ meaþelinde muþes wiþ yeoniende tuteles Lokiþ seiþ Sein Jerome þet ye nabben yicchinde nowþer 
tunge ne earen þet is to seggen þet ow ne luste nowþer speoken ne hercni worltlich 
speche Hiderto is iseid of ower silence ant hu ower speche schal beo seltsene Of silence ant of speche nis bute a lare ant for
þi i writunge ha eorneþ ba togederes Nu we schulen sumhwet speoken of ower 
herunge ayein uvel speche þet ye þertogeines tunen ower earen ant yef ned is 
spearren ower þurles 
For al uvel speche mine leove sustren stoppiþ ower earen ant habbeþ wleatunge 
of þe muþ þe speoweþ ut atter Uvel speche is 
þreofald attri ful ant idel Idel speche is uvel ful speche is wurse attri is þe wurste 
Idel is ant unnet al þet god ne kimeþ of ant of þulli speche seiþ ure Laverd schal 
euch word beon irikenet ant iyeve reisun hwi þe an hit seide ant te oþer hit lustnede 
Ant þis is þah þet leaste uvel of þe þreo uveles Hwet hu þenne schal me yelde 
reisun of þe wurse Hwet hu of þe wurste þet is of attri ant of ful speche Nawt 
ane þet hit spekeþ ah þet hit hercneþ Ful speche is as of leccherie ant of oþre 
fulþen þet unweschene muþes speokeþ oþerhwiles þeose beoþ alle ischrapede 
ut of ancre riwle þe swuch fulþe spit ut in eani ancre earen me schulde dutten his 
muþ nawt wiþ scharpe sneateres ah wiþ hearde fustes 
Attri speche is heresie þweartover leasunge bacbitunge ant fikelunge þeos 
beoþ þe wurste Heresie Godd have þonc ne rixleþ nawt in Englelond Leasunge is 
se uvel þing þet Seint Austin seiþ þet forte schilde þi feader from deaþ ne schuldest 
tu nawt lihen Godd seolf seiþ þet he is soþ ant hwet is mare ayein soþ þen is leas þe deovel is leas ant leasunge feader þe ilke 
þenne þe stureþ hire tunge i leasunge ha makeþ of hire tunge cradel to þe deofles 
bearn ant rockeþ hit yeornliche as his nurrice 
Bacbitunge ant fikelunge ant eggunge to don uvel ne beoþ nawt monnes speche ah 
beoþ þe deofles bleas ant his ahne stevene Yef ha ahen to beo feor alle worltliche men 
hwet hu ahen ancren heatien ham ant schunien þet ha ham ne iheren Iheren ich 
segge for hwase spekeþ ham nis ha nawt ancre 
 þe neddre seiþ Salomon 
 stingeþ al stille ant þeo þe spekeþ bihinden þet ha nalde bivoren nis nawiht betere 
Herst tu hu Salomon eveneþ bacbitere to stinginde neddre Swa hit is witerliche ha is 
neddre cundel ant bereþ þeo þe uvel spekeþ atter i þe tunge 
 þe fikelere blent mon ant put him preon i þe ehe þet he wiþ fikeleþ þe bac
bitere cheoweþ ofte monnes flesch i Fridei ant beakeþ wiþ his blake bile o cwike 
charoines as þe þet is þes deofles corbin of helle 
 Yef he walde 
pilewin ant toteoren wiþ his bile rotet stinkinde flesch as is reavenes cunde þet is 
walde he seggen uvel bi nan oþer bute bi þeo þe rotieþ ant stinkeþ al i fulþe of hare 
sunne hit were leasse wunder ah lihteþ upo cwic flesch tolimeþ ant tolukeþ hit 
 þet is misseiþ bi swuch þet is cwic ine Godd He is to yiver reven ant to bald mid 
alle On oþer half neomeþ nu yeme of hwucche twa meosters þes twa menestraws 
serviþ hare laverd þe deovel of helle Ful hit is to seggen ah fulre forte beon hit ant 
swa hit is allegate Ha beoþ þes deofles gongmen ant beoþ aa in his 
gonghus þe fikeleres meoster is to hulie þe gongþurl þet he deþ as ofte as he 
wiþ his fikelunge ant wiþ his preisunge wriþ mon his sunne þet stinkeþ na þing 
fulre Ant he hit huleþ ant lideþ swa þet he hit nawt ne stinkeþ þe bacbitere 
unlideþ hit ant openeþ swa þet fulþe þet hit stinkeþ wide þus ha beoþ aa bisie i 
þis fule meoster ant eiþer wiþ oþer striveþ herabuten þulliche men stinkeþ of 
hare stinkinde meoster ant bringeþ euch stude o stench þet ha to nahiþ Ure Laverd 
schilde þet te breaþ of hare stinkinde þrote ne nahi ow neaver Oþer spechen fuleþ 
ah þeose attriþ baþe þe earen ant te heorte þet ye bet icnawen ham yef ei kimeþ 
toward ow low her hare molden Fikeleres beoþ þreo cunnes þe forme beoþ uvele 
inoh þe oþre þah beoþ wurse þe þridde þah beoþ wurst þe forme yef a mon is god preiseþ him bivoren himseolf ant makeþ him 
inohreaþe yet betere þen he beo Ant yef he seiþ wel oþer deþ wel heveþ hit to 
hehe up wiþ overherunge þe oþer yef a mon is uvel ant seiþ ant deþ se muche 
mis þet hit beo se open sunne þet he hit ne mahe nanes weis allunge wiþseggen he 
þah bivore þe mon seolf makeþ his uvel leasse Nis hit nawt nu he seiþ se over
uvel as me hit makeþ Nart tu nawt i þis þing þe forme ne þe leaste þu havest 
monie feren Let iwurþe god mon ne geast tu nawt te ane moni deþ muche 
wurse þe þridde cunne of fikelere is wurst as ich seide for he preiseþ þe uvele 
ant his uvele dede as þe þe seiþ to þe cniht þe robbeþ his povre men A Sire as 
þu dest wel for eaver me schal þene cheorl peolkin ant pilien for he is as þe wiþin 
þe spruteþ ut þe betere þet me hine croppeþ ofte þus þes false fikeleres ablendeþ þe ham hercniþ as ich ear 
seide ant wriheþ hare fulþe þet ha hit ne mahe stinken ant þet is hare muchel 
unselhþe For yef ha hit stunken ham walde wleatie þerwiþ ant eornen to schrift ant 
speowen hit ut þer ant schunien hit þe refter 
Bacbiteres þe biteþ bihinde bac oþre beoþ of twa maneres ah þe leatere is 
wurse þe earre kimeþ al openliche ant seiþ uvel bi anoþer ant speoweþ ut his 
atter se muchel se him eaver to muþ kimeþ ant culcheþ al ut somet þet te attri heorte 
sent up to þe tunge Ah þe leatere kimeþ forþ al on oþer wise wurse feond þen 
þe oþer is ant under freondes huckel warpeþ adun þet heaved feþ on forte siken 
ear he eawt segge ant makeþ drupi chere bisampleþ longe abuten forte beo bet i
levet Hwen hit alles kimeþ forþ þenne is hit yeolow atter Weila ha seiþ wa is 
me þet he oþer heo habbeþ swuch word icaht Inoh ich wes abuten ah ne healp me 
nawt to don herof bote Yare is þet ich wiste þe rof ah þah þurh me ne schulde hit 
beon neaver mare iuppet Ah nu hit is þurh oþre swa wide ibroht forþ þet ich ne 
mei hit nawt wiþsaken Uvel me seiþ þet hit is ant yet hit is wurse Sorhful ich am ant 
sari þet ich hit schal seggen ah for soþe swa hit is ant þet is muchel sorhe for i feole 
oþer þing he oþer heo is swiþe to herien ah onont þis þing wa is me þervore 
ne mei ham namon werien þis beoþ þe deofles neddren þe Salomon spekeþ of 
Ure Laverd þurh his grace halde ower earen feor hare attrie tungen ne leve ow neaver 
stinken þet fule put þet ha unwreoþ as þe fikeleres wreoþ ant hulieþ as ich seide 
Unwreon hit to hamseolven þeo þe hit tolimpeþ ant hulien hit to oþre þet is a 
muche þeaw nawt to þeo þe hit schulden smeallen ant heatien þet fulþe 
Nu mine leove sustren from al uvel speche þet is þus þreovald idel ful ant 
attri haldeþ feor ower eare Me seiþ upon ancren þet euch meast haveþ an ald 
cwene to feden hire earen a meaþelilt þe meaþeleþ hire alle þe talen of þe lond a 
rikelot þe cakeleþ al þet ha siþ ant hereþ swa þet me seiþ i bisahe From mulne ant 
from chepinge from smiþþe ant from ancrehus me tidinge bringeþ Wat Crist þis 
is a sari sahe þet ancrehus þet schulde beon anlukest stude of alle schal beon ifeiet 
to þe ilke þreo studen þet meast is in of chaffle Ah ase cwite as ye beoþ of þullich 
leove sustren weren alle oþre ure Laverd hit uþe 
Nu ich habbe sunderlepes ispeken of þes þreo limen of ehe of muþ of eare 
Of eare is al þis leaste to ancre bihove for leflich þing nis hit nawt þet ancre beore 
swuch muþ ah muchel me mei dreden to swucche muþes sumcheare þet ha beie 
hire eare Of sihþe of speche of hercnunge is iseid sunderlepes of euchan o rawe 
Cume we nu eft ayein ant speoken of alle imeane Understond ancre hwas 
spuse þu art ant hu he is gelus of alle þine lates 
 Ich am he seiþ bi himseolf þe geluse Godd Ich am 
gelus of þe Syon mi leofmon wiþ muche gelusie þuhte him nawt inoh iseid þet 
he is gelus of þe bute he seide þerto wiþ muche gelusie 
seiþ Salomon þe wise Wite þe nu ful wel his eare is eaver 
toward te ant he hereþ al His ehe aa bihalt te yef þu makest ei semblant eani luvelates 
toward unþeawes Syon þet is schawere He cleopeþ þe his 
schawere swa his þet nan oþres forþi he seiþ in Canticis Schaw þi neb to me he seiþ ant to nan oþer Bihald me yef þu wult habbe 
briht sihþe wiþ þine heorte ehnen Bihald inward þer ich am ant ne sech þu me nawt 
wiþute þin heorte Ich am wohere scheomeful ne nule ich nohwer bicluppe mi leofmon 
bute i stude dearne O þulli wise ure Laverd spekeþ to his spuse Ne þunche hire 
neaver wunder yef ha nis muchel ane þah he hire schunie ant swa ane þet ha putte 
euch worldlich þrung ant euch nurþ eorþlich ut of hire heorte for heo is Godes 
chambre Nurþ ne kimeþ in heorte bute of sum þing þet me haveþ oþer isehen 
oþer iherd ismaht oþer ismeallet ant utewiþ ifelet Ant þet witeþ to soþe þet 
eaver se þes wittes beoþ mare isprengde utward se ha leasse wendeþ inward 
Eaver se recluse toteþ mare utward se ha haveþ leasse leome of ure Laverd inward 
ant alswa of þe oþre Lo hwet Sein Gregoire seiþ Hwase yemelesliche wit hire uttre 
ehnen þurh Godes rihtwise dom ha ablindeþ i þe inre þet ha ne mei iseo Godd mid 
gastelich sihþe ne þurh swuch sihþe icnawen ant þurh þe cnawleachunge over 
alle þing luvien For efter þet me cnaweþ his muchele godnesse ant efter þet me 
feleþ his swote swetnesse efter þet me luveþ him mare oþer leasse 
Forþi mine leove sustren beoþ wiþute blinde as wes þe hali Jacob ant Tobie þe 
gode ant Godd wule as he yef ham yeoven ow liht wiþinnen him to seon ant cnawen 
ant þurh þe cnawlechunge over alle þing him luvien þenne schule ye iseon hu al þe 
world is nawt hu hire frovre is fals þurh þet sihþe ye schule seon alle þe deofles 
wiheles hu he biwrencheþ wrecches Ye schulen iseon in owseolf hwet beo yet to 
beten of ower ahne sunnen Ye schulen bihalde sumcheare toward te pine of helle þet 
ow uggi wiþ ham ant fleo þe swiþere ham frommard Ye schulen gasteliche iseon 
þe blissen of heovene þe ontenden ower heorte to hihin ham toward Ye schulen as i 
schawere iseon ure Leafdi wiþ hire meidnes al þe englene weoret al þe halhene hird 
ant him over ham alle þe blisseþ ham alle ant is hare alre crune þis sihþe leove 
sustren schal frovrin ow mare þen mahte ei worltlich sihþe Hali men witen wel þe 
habbeþ hit ifondet þet euch eorþlich gleadunge is unwurþ hertoyeines Hit is 
a dearne healewi seiþ Seint Juhan Ewangeliste i þe Apocalipse Hit is a dearne 
healewi þet namon ne cnaweþ þet naveþ hit ismecchet þis smech ant tis cnawunge 
kimeþ of gastelich sihþe of gastelich herunge of gastelich speche þet ha schulen 
habben þe forgaþ for Godes luve worldliche herunges eorþliche spechen fleschliche 
sihþen Ant efter þet sihþe þet 
is nu dosc her ye schulen habbe þe ruppe þe brihte sihþe of Godes neb þet alle 
gleadunge is of i þe blisse of heovene muche bivore þe oþre For þe rihtwise Godd hit 
haveþ swa idemet þet euchanes mede þer ondswerie ayein þe swinc ant ayeines 
þe ennu þet ha her for his luve eadmodliche þolieþ Forþi hit is semlich þet ancren 
þeos twa marheyeoven habben bivoren oþre swiftnesse ant leome of a briht sihþe 
Swiftnes ayeines þet ha beoþ nu swa bipinnet Leome of briht sihþe ayeines þet ha 
her þeostriþ nu hamseolven ne nulleþ nowþer iseo mon ne of mon beon isehene 
Alle þeo in heovene schule beon ase swifte as is nu monnes þoht as is þe sunne 
gleam þe smit from est into west as þe ehe openeþ Ah ancres bisperret her schulen 
beo þer yef ei mei lihtre ba ant swiftre ant i se wide schakeles as me seiþ pleien 
in heovene large lesewen þet te bodi schal beon hwerseeaver þe gast wule in an 
hondhwile þis is nu þe an marheyeove þet ich seide ancren schulden habben bivoren 
oþre þe oþer is of sihþe Alle þeo in heovene seoþ i Godd alle þing ant ancren schule brihtluker for 
hare blindfellunge her iseon ant understonde þer Godes dearne runes ant his derve 
domes þe ne kepeþ nu to witen of þinges wiþuten wiþ eare ne wiþ ehe 
Forþi mine leove sustren yef ei mon bit to seon ow easkiþ him hwet god þerof 
mahte lihten For moni uvel ich iseo þe rin ant nane biheve Yef he is meadles leveþ 
him þe wurse Yef ei wurþeþ swa awed þet he warpe hond forþ toward te þurl
claþ swiftliche ananriht schutteþ al þet þurl to ant leoteþ him iwurþen Alswa 
sone se eaver eani feleþ into ei luþer speche þet falle toward ful luve sperreþ þe þurl 
ananriht ne ondswerie ye him nawiht ah wendeþ awei wiþ þis vers þet he hit 
mahe iheren Ant gaþ bivoren ower 
weoved wiþ þe Ne chastie ye na swuch mon neaver on oþer wise for in
wiþ þe chastiement he mahte ondswerie swa ant blawen se liþeliche þet sum sperke 
mahte acwikien Na wohlech nis se culvert as o pleinte wise as hwase þus seide ich 
nalde forte þolie deaþ þenche fulþe toward te ant swereþ deope aþes ah 
þah ich hefde isworen hit luvien ich mot te Hwa is wurse þen me Moni slep hit 
binimeþ me Nu me is wa þet tu hit wast ah foryef me nu þet ich habbe hit itald te 
þah ich schule wurþe wod ne schalt tu neaver mare witen hu me stonde Ha hit 
foryeveþ him for he spekeþ se feire speokeþ þenne of oþerhwet Ah eaver is þe 
ehe to þe wude lehe Eaver is þe heorte i þe earre speche Yet hwen he is forþe ha 
went in hire þoht ofte swucche wordes hwen ha schulde oþerhwet yeornliche yemen 
He eft secheþ his point forte breoke foreward swereþ he mot nede ant swa waxeþ 
þet wa se lengre se wurse For na feondschipe nis se uvel as is fals freondschipe 
Feond þe þuncheþ freond is sweoke over alle Forþi mine leove sustren ne yeove 
ye to swuch mon nan inyong to speokene For as Hali Writ seiþ hare speche spreat 
ase cancre Ah for alle ondsweres wendeþ ow frommard him alswa as ich seide 
þ ruppe Sawvin owseolven ne maten him betere ne mahe ye o nane wise 
Lokiþ nu hu propreliche þe leafdi i Canticis Godes deore spuse leareþ ow bi hire 
sahe hu ye schule seggen Low ha seiþ hercne ich ihere mi leof speoken He cleopeþ me 
ich mot gan Ant ye gan ananriht to ower deore leofmon ant meaneþ ow to his earen 
þe luveliche cleopeþ ow to him wiþ þes wordes þet is aris up hihe þe heonewart ant cum to me mi leofmon mi culvre mi 
feire ant mi schene spuse Schaw to me þi leove neb 
ant ti lufsume leor went te from oþre Sei hwa 
haveþ ido þe hwa haveþ ihurt mi deore sing i mine earen Forþi þet tu ne 
wilnest bute to seo mi wlite ne speoke bute to me þi stevene is me swete ant ti wlite 
schene þis beoþ nu twa 
þinges þe beoþ iluvet swiþe swete speche ant schene wlite Hwase ham haveþ 
togederes swucche cheoseþ Jesu Crist to leofmon ant to spuse Yef þu wult swuch 
beon ne schaw þu na mon þi wlite ne ne leote bliþeliche here þi speche ah turn ham 
ba to Jesu Crist to þi deorewurþe spus as he bit þe ruppe as þu wult þet ti speche 
þunche him swete ant ti wlite schene ant habben him to leofmon þet is þusentfald 
schenre þen þe sunne 
Hercniþ nu yeornliche mine leove sustren al anoþer speche ant frommard tis 
earre Hercniþ nu hu Jesu Crist spekeþ as o wreaþþe ant seiþ as o grim hoker ant o 
scarn to þe ancre þe schulde beon his leofmon ant secheþ þah gealunge utward ant 
frovre wiþ ehe oþer wiþ tunge þis beoþ þe wordes yef þu ne cnawest teseolf þu feier bimong 
wummen wend ut ant ga efter gateheorden ant lesewe þine tichnes bi heordemenne 
hulen of ris ant of leaves þis is a cruel word a grim word mid alle þet ure Laverd 
seiþ as o grome ant o scarn to totinde ant to hercwile ant to speokele ancres Hit is 
bileppet ant ihud ah ich hit wulle unvalden Yef þu ne cnawest teseolf he seiþ ure 
Laverd neomeþ nu gode yeme þet is yef þu nast hwas spuse þu art þet tu art 
cwen of heovene yef þu art me treowe as spuse ah to beonne yef þu þis havest 
foryeten ant telest herof to lutel wend ut ant ga he seiþ Hwider Ut of þis hehschipe 
of þis muchele menske ant folhe heorde of geat he seiþ Hwet beoþ heorde of geat 
þet beoþ flesches lustes þe stinkeþ ase geat doþ bivoren ure Laverd Yef þu 
havest foryete nu þi wurþfule leafdischipe ga ant folhe þeos geat folhe flesches 
lustes Nu kimeþ þe refter ant lesewe þine tichnes þet is as he seide fed tine 
ehnen wiþ uttotunge þi tunge wiþ chaflunge þine earen wiþ spellunge þi nease 
wiþ smeallunge þi flesch wiþ softe felunge þeos fif wittes he cleopeþ tichnes for 
alswa as of a ticchen þet haveþ swete flesch kimeþ a stinkinde gat oþer a ful bucke 
al riht alswa of a yung swete locunge oþer of a swote herunge oþer of a softe felunge 
waxeþ a stincinde lust ant a ful sunne Hweþer ei totilde ancre fondede eaver þis þe 
beakeþ eaver utward as untohe brid i cage Hweþer þe cat of helle cahte eaver 
towart hire ant lahte wiþ his cleavres hire heorte heved Ye soþes ant droh ut al þe 
bodi efter wiþ clokes of crokede ant kene fondunges ant makede hire to leosen baþe 
Godd ant mon wiþ brad scheome ant sunne ant bireafde hire ed an cleap þe eorþe ant 
ec þe heovene Inoh sari lure To wraþer heale beakede eaver swa ut ancre 
he seiþ o grome ga ut as dude Dyne Jacobes dohter to himmere heile hire to 
wraþer heale þet is to seggen leaf me ant mi cunfort þet is inwiþ þi breoste ant 
ga sech wiþuten þe worldes frakele frovre þe schal endin eaver i sar ant i sorhe Tac 
þerto ant leaf me hwen þe swa is leovere for ne schalt tu nanesweis þes ilke twa 
cunforz min ant te worldes þe joie of þe Hali Gast ant ec flesches frovre habbe 
togederes Cheos nu an of þes twa for þe oþer þu most leten Yef þu ne cnawest teseolf þu feier bimong wummen seiþ ure Laverd 
 þu feier bimong wummen ye nu her do þerto þet schalt ant tu wel wulle elles
hwer beo feier nawt ane bimong wummen ah bimong engles þu mi wurþli spuse 
seiþ ure Laverd schalt tu folhin geat o feld þet beoþ flesches lustes Feld is 
willes breade Schalt tu o þis wise folhi geat yont te feld þe schuldest i þin heorte bur 
biseche me cosses as mi leofmon þet seiþ to me i þet luveboc þet is cusse me mi leofmon wiþ þe coss of his muþ muþene 
swetest þis coss leove sustren is a swetnesse ant a delit of heorte swa unimete 
swete þet euch worldes savur is bitter þertoyeines Ah ure Laverd wiþ þis coss ne 
cusseþ na sawle þe luveþ ei þing buten him ant te ilke þinges for him þe helpeþ him 
to habben Ant tu þenne Godes spuse þet maht heren herbivoren hu sweteliche þi 
spus spekeþ ant cleopeþ þe to him se luveliche þe refter hu he went te lof ant spekeþ 
swiþe grimliche yef þu ut wendest Hald te i þi chambre Ne fed tu nawt wiþuten 
þine gate tichnes ah hald wiþinnen þin hercnunge þi speche ant ti sihþe ant tun 
feaste hare yeten muþ ant ehe ant eare For nawt ha beoþ bilokene inwiþ wah 
oþer wal þe þes yeten openiþ bute ayein Godes sonde ant liveneþ of sawle Over alle þing þenne as Salomon þe leareþ ant ich 
seide feor bivoren i þe frumþe of þis dale mine leove sustren witeþ ower heorte 
þe heorte is wel iloket yef muþ ant ehe ant eare wisliche beon ilokene For heo as 
ich seide þer beoþ þe heorte wardeins ant yef þe wardeins wendeþ ut þe ham biþ 
biwist uvele þis beoþ nu þe þreo wittes þet ich habbe ispeken of Speoke we nu 
scheortliche of þe twa oþre þah nis nawt speche þe muþes wit ah is smechunge 
þah ba beon i muþe 
Smeal of nease is þe feorþe of þe fif wittes Of þis wit seiþ Seint Austin 
 Of smealles he seiþ ne fondi ich nawt mucheles Yef ha beoþ neh o Godes half 
 yef feor me ne recche Ure Laverd þah þurh Ysaie þreateþ ham wiþ helle stench 
þe habbeþ delit her i fleschliche smealles þertoyeines 
ha schulen habben heovenliche smealles þe habbeþ her of irnes swat oþer of heren 
þet ha beoreþ oþer of swati hettren oþer of þicke eir in hire hus ant muhlinde 
þinges stench oþerhwiles ant strong breaþ i nease 
þerof beoþ iwarnet mine leove sustren þet oþerhwile þe feond makeþ sum 
þing to stinken þet ye schulden notien forþi þet he walde þet ye hit schulden 
schunien Oþerhwile þe wiheleare of sum dearne þing þet ye ne mahe nawt iseon 
as dust of dearne sedes makeþ a swote smeal cumen as þah hit were of heovene for 
ye schulden wenen þet Godd for ower hali lif sende ow his elne ant leote wel to ow
seolf ant leapen into prude Smeal þe kimeþ o Godes half frovreþ þe heorte mare 
þen þe nease þeos ant oþre truiles þet he bitruileþ monie schulen beon ibroht to 
nawt wiþ haliweater ant wiþ þe hali rodetaken Hwase þohte hu Godd seolf wes i 
þis wit idervet ha walde þe derf þe rof þuldeliche þolien 
I þe munt of Calvarie þer ure Laverd hongede wes þe cwalmstowe þer leien 
ofte licomes irotet buven eorþe ant stunken swiþe stronge He as he hongede mahte 
habben hare breaþ wiþ al his oþer wa riht amidden his nease 
Alswa as he wes idervet in alle his oþre wittes in his sihþe þa he seh his deore
wurþe moder teares ant Sein Juhanes Ewangeliste ant te oþre Maries ant þa he 
biheold hu his deore deciples fluhen alle from him ant leafden him ane He weop him
seolve þrien wiþ his feire ehnen He þolede al þuldeliche þet me him blindfeallede 
hwen his ehnen weren þus i schendlac iblintfeallet forte yeove þe ancre þe brihte 
sihþe of heovene þah þu þine ehnen for his luve ant i munegunge þe rof blintfealli 
on eorþe to beoren him feolahreadden nis na muche wunder 
Amid þe muþ me gurde him sumcheare inohreaþe as me tobeot his cheken ant 
spitte him o scarne ant an ancre is for a word ut of hire witte Hwen he þolede 
þuldeliche þet te Giws dutten as ha buffeteden him his deorewurþe muþ wiþ hare 
dreori fustes ant tu for þe luve of him ant for þin ahne muchele biheve þi tutelinde 
muþ dute wiþ þine lippen Teke þet he smahte galle on his tunge forte learen ancre 
þet ha ne grucchi neaver mare for na mete ne for na drunch ne beo hit swa unorne 
Yef ha hit mei eoten eote ant þonki Godd yeorne Yef ha ne mei nawt beo sari þet ha 
mot sechen estfulre Ah ear þen þet biddunge areare eani scandle ear deie martir in 
hire meoseise Deaþ me ah forte fleon ase forþ as me mei wiþute sunne ah me schal 
ear deien þen me do eani heaved sunne Ant nis hit muche sunne to makien þet me 
segge Estful is þeos ancre Muchel is þet ha bid Yet is wurse yef me seiþ þet ha 
is grucchilit ant fulitohe dangerus ant erveþ forte paien Were ha imid te world ha 
moste beo sumchearre ipaiet inohreaþe mid leasse ant mid wurse Muchel hofles hit 
is cumen into ancrehus into Godes prisun willes ant waldes to stude of meoseise for
te sechen eise þe rin ant meistrie ant leafdischipe mare þen ha mahte habben inoh
reaþe ihaved i þe worlde þenc ancre hwet tu sohtest þa þu forsoke þe world i 
þi biclusunge Biwepen þine ahne ant oþres sunnen ant forleosen alle þe blissen of 
þis lif forte cluppen blisfulliche þi blisfule leofmon i þe eche lif of heovene O 
seiþ Sein Jeremie O wei
lawei weilawei hu is gold iþeostret Hu is feherest heow biturnd ant forweolewet 
þe Apostle spekeþ to swucche grimliche as o wreaþþe Me hwuch unseli gast 
haveþ swa bimalscret ow þet ye i gast bigunnen ant i flesch wulleþ endin þe 
gastelich lif bigunnen i þe Hali Gast beoþ bicumene al fleschliche al fleschliche i
wurþen lahinde lihte ilatet ane hwile lihte iwordet anoþer luþere iwordet estfule 
ant sarcurne ant grucchildes meanildes ant yet þet wurse is cursildes ant chidildes 
bittre ant attrie wiþ heorte tobollen Bihofde nawt þet swuch were leafdi of castel 
Hoker ant hofles þing is þet a smiret ancre ant ancre biburiet for hwet is ancrehus 
bute hire burinesse ant heo schal beo greattre ibollen leafdiluker leoten of þen a 
leafdi of hames Yef ha makeþ hire wraþ ayeines gult of sunne ha shulde setten hire 
wordes swa efne þet ha ne þunche oversturet ne nawt ilead over skile ah inwardliche 
ant soþliche wiþuten hihþe ant hehschipe in a softe stevene þis is Salomones sahe þet hit limpe to ei of ow Godd ne leve 
neaver Cang dohter iwurþ as mone i wonunge þriveþ as þe cangun se lengre 
se wurse Ye as ye wulleþ waxen ant nawt wenden hindward sikerliche ye moten 
rowen ayein stream wiþ muchel swinc breoken forþ ant gasteliche earmes 
stealewurþliche sturien ant swa ye moten alle For alle we beoþ i þis stream i þe 
worldes wode weater þe bereþ adun monie Sone se we eaver wergiþ ant resteþ us i 
slawþe ure bat geaþ hindward ant we beoþ þe cang dohter þe gaþ woniende þe 
wlecche þe Godd speoweþ as is iwriten herefter þe bigunnen i gast ant i 
flesch endiþ Nai nai ah as Job seiþ þe delveþ efter golthord eaver se he mare 
nahheþ hit se his heortes gleadschipe makeþ him mare lusti ant mare fersch to diggin 
ant delven deoppre ant deoppre aþet he hit finde Ower heorte nis nawt on eorþe for
þi ne þurve ye nawt delven dunewardes ah heoven uppart þe heorte for þet is þe 
uprowunge ayein þis worldes stream driven hire ayeinward to delven þe golthord 
þet up is in heovene Ant hwet is þet delvunge Yeornful sechinde þoht hwer hit beo 
hwuch hit beo hu me hit mahe ifinden þis is þe delvunge Beon bisiliche ant 
yeornfulliche eaver herabuten wiþ anewil yirnunge wiþ heate of hungri heorte 
waden up of unþeawes creopen ut of flesch breoken up over hire astihen up on ow
seolf wiþ heh þoht toward heovene swa muchel þe neodeluker þet ower feble 
tendre flesch heardes ne mei þolien Nu þenne þerayein yeoveþ Godd ower heorte 
i softnesse i swetnesse in alles cunnes meoknesse ant softest eadmodnesse nawt 
nu granin ant peonsin þe refter hehi stevene wreaþen hire unweneliche sinetin hire 
wordes wrenchen aweiward wenden þe schuldre keaste þe heaved swa þet Godd 
heateþ hire ant mon hire scarneþ Nai nai Ripe wordes lates ripe ant werkes bilimpeþ 
to ancre Hwen wordes beoþ eadmodliche ant soþfestliche iseide nawt fulitoheliche 
ne babanliche þenne habbeþ ha burþerne to beo riht understonden Nu is þis al iseid 
þet ye efter Jesu Crist þe me gurde ine muþ ant galle yef to drinken wiþ muþes 
sunne witen ow ant þolieþ sum derf i þet wit as he wes þe rin idervet 
In his eare he hefde þe heovenliche Laverd al þe edwit ant te upbrud al þe scarn 
ant al þe scheome þet eare mahte iheren ant he seiþ bi himseolf us forte learen Ich 
heold me he seiþ stille as dumbe ant deaf deþ þet naveþ nan ondswere þah me 
him misdo oþer missegge þis is þi leofmonnes sahe ant tu seli ancre þe art his 
leove spuse leorne hit yeorne of him þet tu hit cunne ant mahe soþliche seggen 
Nu ich habbe ispeken of ower fowre wittes ant of Godes fowre hu he þurh hise 
frovreþ ow as ofte as ye in ower feleþ eani weane Nu hercniþ of þe fifte þet is 
meast neod elne for þe pine is meast þe rin þet is i felunge ant te licunge alswa 
yef hit swa turneþ 
þe fifte wit is felunge þis ilke an wit is in alle þe oþre ant yont al þe licome ant 
forþi hit is neod to habben best warde Ure Laverd wiste hit wel ant forþi he walde 
meast i þet wit þolien al forte frovrin us yef we þolieþ wa þe rin ant forte wenden 
us frommard te licunge þet flesches lust easkeþ nomeliche i felunge mare þen in 
oþre 
Ure Laverd i þis wit nefde nawt in a stude ah hefde over al pine nawt ane yond al 
his bodi ah hefde yet inwiþ in his seli sawle In hire he felde þe stiche of sari sorhe ant 
sorhful þet dude him sike sare þis stiche wes þreovald þe ase þreo speren smat 
him to þe heorte þe an wes his modres wop ant te oþre Maries þe flowen o teares 
þe oþer þet his ahne deore deciples ne lefden him na mare ne ne heolden for Godd 
forþi þet he ne healp himseolf in his muchele pine ant fluhen alle from him ant 
leafden him as fremede þe þridde wes þet muchele sar ant te ofþunchunge þet he 
hefde inwiþ him of hare forlorenesse þe drohen him to deaþe þet he seh onont ham 
al his swinc forloren þet he swonc on eorþe þeos ilke þreo stichen weren in his 
sawle In his licome euch lim as Seint Austin seiþ þolede sundri pine ant deide yond 
al his bodi as he ear yond al his bodi deaþes swat sweatte Ant her seiþ Sein Beornard 
þet he ne weop nawt ane wiþ ehnen ah dude as wiþ alle his limen For se ful of angoisse wes þet ilke nedswat þet 
lihte of his licome ayein þe angoisuse deaþ þet he schulde þolien þet hit þuhte read 
blod On oþer 
half swa largeliche ant swa swiþe fleaw þet ilke blodi swat of his blisfule bodi þet 
te streames urnen dun to þer eorþe Swuch grure hefde his monliche flesch ayein þe 
derve pinen þet hit schulde drehen þet nes na feorlich wunder for eaver se flesch is 
cwickre se þe reopunge þe rof ant te hurt is sarre A lutel hurt i þe ehe derveþ mare 
þen deþ a muchel i þe hele for þe flesch is deaddre Euch monnes flesch is dead 
flesch ayein þet wes Godes flesch as þet te wes inumen of þe tendre meiden ant 
na þing neaver nes þe rin þet hit adeadede ah eaver wes iliche cwic of þet cwike 
Goddhead þe wunede þe rinne Forþi in his flesch wes þe pine sarre þen eaver eani 
mon in his flesch þolede þet his flesch wes cwic over alle flesches lo hwuc an 
essample A mon for uvel þet he haveþ ne let him nawt blod o þe seke halve ah deþ 
þe hale to heale þe seke Ah in al þe world þe wes o þe fevre nes bimong al mon
cun an hal dale ifunden þe mahte beon ilete blod bute Godes bodi ane þe lette him 
blod o rode nawt o þe earm ane ah dude o fif halve forte healen moncun of þe 
secnesse þet te fif wittes hefden awakenet þus lo þe hale half ant te cwike dale 
droh þet uvele blod ut frommard te unhale ant healde swa þe seke þurh blod is in 
Hali Writ sunne bitacnet þe reisuns hwi beoþ efter sutelliche ischawet Ah þerof 
neomeþ yeme mine leove sustren þet ower deorewurþe spus þe luvewurþe Laverd 
þe Healent of heovene Jesu Godd Godes sune þe wealdent of al þe world þa he 
wes þus ilete blod understondeþ þet dei hwuch wes his diete I þe ilke blodletunge 
se baleful ant se bitter þe ilke þet he bledde fore ne brohten ha him to present ne win 
ne ale ne weater yet þa he seide ant meande as he bledde of þurst o þe rode 
ah duden bitter galle Hwer wes eaver iyeven to eani blodleten se povre pitance Ant 
tah ne gruchede he nawt ah underveng hit eadmodliche forte learen hise Ant yet he 
dude mare us to forbisne dude his deore muþ þerto ant smahte þe rof þah he hit 
notie ne mahte Hwa is þenne efter þis ant ancre hure ant hure þe gruccheþ yef ha 
naveþ nawt oþer mete oþer drunch efter hire eise Ant siker hwase gruccheþ ha 
offreþ yet ure Laverd his luþere pitance as duden þa þe Giws ant is Giwes fere to 
beoden him in his þurst drunch of sur galle His þurst nis bute yirnunge of ure sawle 
heale ant grucchunge of bitter ant of sur heorte is him surre ant bittrure nu þen wes þa 
þe galle Ant tu his deore spuse ne beo þu nawt Giwes make forte birlin him swa ah 
ber him feolahreadden ant drinc wiþ him bliþeliche al þet ti flesch þuncheþ sur 
oþer bitter þet is pine ant wone ant alle meoseises ant he hit wule þe yelden as 
his treowe fere wiþ healewi of heovene 
þus wes Jesu Crist þe almihti Godd in alle his fif wittes derfliche ipinet ant 
nomeliche i þis leaste þet is i felunge for his flesch wes al cwic as is þe tendre 
ehe Ant ye witen þis wit þet is flesches felunge over alle þe oþre Godes honden 
weren ineilet o rode þurh þe ilke neiles ich halsi ow ancres nawt ow ah do oþre 
for hit nis na neod mine leove sustren haldeþ ower honden inwiþ ower þurles 
Hondlunge oþer ei felunge bitweone mon ant ancre is þing swa uncumelich ant dede 
se scheomelich ant se naket sunne to al þe world se eatelich ant se muche scandle þet 
nis na neod to speoken ne writen þertoyeines for al wiþute writunge þet ful is to 
etscene Godd hit wat as me were muche deale leovere þet ich isehe ow alle þreo 
mine leove sustren wummen me leovest hongin on a gibet forte wiþbuhe sunne 
þen ich sehe an of ow yeoven anlepi cos eani mon on eorþe swa as ich meane Ich am 
stille of þet mare Nawt ane monglin honden ah putten hond utward bute hit beo for 
nede is wohunge efter Godes grome ant tollunge of his eorre Hireseolf bihalden hire 
ahne hwite honden deþ hearm moni ancre þe haveþ ham to feire as þeo þe beoþ 
foridlet Ha schulden schrapien euche dei þe eorþe up of hare put þet ha schulen 
rotien in Godd hit wat þet put deþ muche god moni ancre For as Salomon seiþ þeo þe haveþ eaver hire 
deaþ as bivoren hire ehnen þet te put munegeþ yef þet ha þencheþ wel o þe dom 
of Domesdei þer þe engles schule cwakien ant te eche ant te eateliche pinen of helle 
ant over al ant al o Jesu Cristes passiun hu he wes ipinet as is sumdeal iseid in 
alle his fif wittes lihtliche nule ha nawt folhi flesches licunge efter willes lust ne drahen 
in toward hire nan heaved sunne wiþ hire fif wittes þis is nu inoh iseid of þe fif 
wittes þe beoþ ase wardein wiþuten of þe heorte þet sawle lif is inne As we seiden 
þ ruppe on earst þet Salomon seide Nu beoþ Crist have þonc þe twa dalen overcumen Ga we nu 
wiþ his help upo þe þridde 
</td>
