<td align=left valign=top>
Mine leove sustren alswa as ye witeþ wel ower wittes utewiþ alswa over 
alle þing lokiþ þet ye beon inwiþ softe ant milde ant eadmode swete ant 
swote iheortet ant þolemode ayein woh of word þet me seiþ ow ant werc 
þet me misdeþ ow leste ye al leosen Ayein bittre ancres Daviþ seiþ þis vers Ich am he seiþ as pellican þe wuneþ 
bi him ane Pellican is a fuhel se weamod ant se wreaþful þet hit sleaþ ofte o grome 
his ahne briddes hwen ha doþ him teone ant þenne sone þe refter hit wurþ swiþe 
sari ant makeþ swiþe muche man ant smit himseolf wiþ his bile þet he sloh ear his 
briddes wiþ ant draheþ blod of his breoste ant wiþ þet blod acwikeþ eft his briddes 
isleine þis fuhel pellican is þe weamode ancre Hire briddes beoþ hire gode werkes 
þet ha sleaþ ofte wiþ bile of scharp wreþþe Ah hwen ha swa haveþ idon do as 
deþ þe pellican ofþunche hit swiþe sone ant wiþ hire ahne bile beaki hire breoste 
þet is wiþ schrift of hire muþ þet ha sunegede wiþ ant sloh hire gode werkes 
drahe þet blod of sunne ut of hire breoste þet is of þe heorte þet sawle lif is inne 
 ant swa schulen eft acwikien hire isleine briddes þet beoþ hire gode werkes Blod 
bitacneþ sunne for alswa as a mon bibled is grislich ant eatelich i monnes ehe alswa is 
þe sunfule bivore Godes ehe On oþer half namon ne mei juggi wel blod ear hit beo 
icolet Alswa is of sunne Hwil þe heorte walleþ inwiþ of wreaþþe nis þer na riht 
dom oþer hwil þe lust is hat toward eani sunne ne maht tu nawt te hwiles deme wel 
hwet hit is ne hwet ter wule cumen of Ah let lust overgan ant hit te wule likin Let þet 
hate acolin as deþ þe wule iuggi blod ant tu schalt demen ariht þe sunne ful ant ladlich 
þet te þuhte feier ant uvel se muchel cumen þe rof yef þu hit hefdest idon hwil þet 
hate leaste þet tu schalt deme wod teseolf þa þu þertoward þohtest þis is of 
euch sunne soþ hwi blod hit bitacneþ ant nomeliche of wreaþþe Wreaþþe hit seiþ hwil hit least ablindeþ 
swa þe heorte þet ha ne mei soþ icnawen Wreaþþe is a forschuppilt as me teleþ i spelles for ha reaveþ 
mon his wit ant changeþ al his chere ant forschuppeþ him from mon into beastes 
cunde Wummon wraþ is wulvene mon wulf oþer liun oþer unicorne Hwil þet 
eaver wreaþþe is i wummone heorte versaili segge hire ures ne 
deþ ha bute þeoteþ Naveþ ha bute as þeo þet is iwent to wulvene i Godes ehnen 
 wulvene stevene in his lihte earen Wreaþþe is a wodschipe 
Wraþ mon nis he wod Hu lokeþ he Hu spekeþ he Hu feareþ his heorte inwiþ 
Hwucche beoþ utewiþ alle hise lates He ne cnaweþ namon Hu is he mon þenne Mon cundelich is milde Sone se he 
leoseþ mildheortnesse he leoseþ monnes cunde ant wreaþþe þe forschuppilt 
forschuppeþ him into beast as ich ear seide Ant hwet yef eni ancre Jesu Cristes 
spuse is forschuppet into wulvene Nis þet muche sorhe Nis þer bute sone forwarpe 
þet ruhe fel abute þe heorte ant wiþ softe sahtnesse makien hire smeþe ant softe as 
is cundeliche wummone hude for wiþ þet wulvene fel na þing þet ha deþ nis Gode 
licwurþe 
Lo her ayeines wreaþþe monie remedies frovren a muche floc ant misliche boten 
Yef me misseiþ þe þench þet tu art eorþe Ne totret me eorþe Ne bispit me eorþe 
þah me dude swa bi þe me dude þe eorþe rihte Yef þu berkest ayein þu art 
hundes cunnes Yef þu stingest ayein þu art neddre cundel ant nawt Cristes spuse 
þench dude he swa Efter alle þe schendfule pinen þet he þolede o þe longe Friniht me leadde 
him ine marhen to hongin o wearitreo ant driven þurh his fowr limen irnene neiles ah 
 na mare þen a schep as þe Hali Writ seiþ cwich ne cweþ he neaver 
þench yet on oþer half hwet is word bute wind To wac ha is istrengþet þet a 
windes puf a word mei afellen ant warpen into sunne ant hwa nule þunche wunder of 
ancre windfeallet On oþer half yetten ne schaweþ ha þet ha is dust ant unstable 
þing þe wiþ a lute wordes wind is anan toblawen þe ilke puf of his muþ yef þu 
hit wurpe under þe hit schulde beore þe uppart toward te blisse of heovene ah nu is 
muche wunder of ure muchele meadschipe Understondeþ þis word Seint Andrew 
mahte þolien þet te hearde rode heve him toward heovene ant luveliche biclupte hire 
Sein Lorenz alswa þolede þet te gridil heve him uppardes wiþ bearninde gleden Seinte 
Stefne þolede þe stanes þet me sende him ant underveng ham gleadliche ant bed for 
ham þe ham senden him wiþ hommen ifalden ant we ne mahe nawt þolien þet te 
wind of a word beore us towart heovene ah beoþ wode ayeines ham þe we schulden 
þonkin as þe ilke þe serviþ us of muche servise þah hit beo hare unþonkes Al þet te unwreaste ant te uvele deþ for uvel al is þe gode to god 
al is his biheve ant timbrunge toward blisse Let him ant þet gleadliche breide þi 
crune þench hu þe hali mon i custe ant blescede þe oþres hond þe 
hefde him ihearmet ant seide se inwardliche cussinde hire yeorne iblescet beo eaver 
þeos hond for ha haveþ itimbret me þe blissen of heovene Ant tu segge alswa bi 
hond þe misdeþ þe ant bi þe muþ alswa þe ewt misseiþ þe iblescet beo þi 
muþ sei for þu makest lome þe rof to timbri mi crune Wel me is for mi god ant 
wa þah for þin uvel for þu dest me freame ant hearmest teseolven Yef ei mon 
oþer wummon misseide oþer misdude ow mine leove sustren swa ye schulden seggen 
Ah nu is muche wunder yef we wel bihaldeþ hu Godes halhen þoleden wunden on 
hare bodi ant we beoþ wode yef a wind blawe a lutel toward us Ant te wind ne 
wundeþ nawt bute þe eir ane for nowþer ne mei þe wind þet is þet word þet 
me seiþ ne wundi þe i þi flesch ne fule þi sawle þah hit puffe upo þe bute þe
seolf hit makie Wel þu maht underyeoten þet ter wes 
lute fur of chearite þet leiteþ al of ure Laverdes luve lute fur wes þer þet a puf 
acwencte for þear as muche fur is hit waxeþ wiþ winde 
Ayein misdede oþer missahe lo her on ende þe beste remedie ant cunneþ þis 
essample A mon þe leie i prisun oþer ahte muche rancun ne o nane wise ne schulde ut 
bute hit were to hongin ear he hefde his rancun fulleliche ipaiet nalde he cunne god 
þonc a mon þe duste uppon him of peonehes a bigurdel forte reimin him wiþ ant 
lesen him of pine þah he wurpe hit ful hearde ayeines his heorte Al þe hurd were 
foryeten for þe gleadnesse O þis ilke wise we beoþ alle i prisun her ant ahen Godd 
greate deattes of sunne forþi we yeiyeþ to him i þe Laverd we seggeþ foryef us ure deattes alswa as we foryeoveþ 
ure deatturs woh þet me deþ us oþer of word oþer of werc þet is ure rancun þet 
we schule reimin us wiþ ant cwitin ure deattes toward ure Laverd þet beoþ ure 
sunnen For wiþute cwitance up of þis prisun nis nan inumen þet nis anan ahonget 
oþer i purgatoire oþer i þe pine of helle Ant ure Laverd seolf seiþ Foryef ant ich foryeove þe as þah he seide þu art endeattet 
toward me swiþe wiþ sunnen ah wult tu god foreward Al þet eaver ei mon misseiþ 
þe oþer misdeþ þe ich wulle neomen onward þe deatte þe þu ahest me Nu 
þenne þah a word culle þe ful hearde upo þe breoste ant as þe þuncheþ on earst 
hurte þin heorte þench as þe prisun walde þe þe oþer hurte sare wiþ þe bigurdel 
ant underveng hit gleadliche forte acwiti þe wiþ ant þonke þe þe hit sent te þah 
Godd ne cunne him neaver þonc of his sonde He hearmeþ him ant freameþ þe yef 
þu hit const þolien For as Daviþ seiþ swiþe wel wiþ alle Godd deþ in his tresor 
þe unwreaste ant te uvele forte hure wiþ ham as me deþ wiþ gersum þeo þe wel 
fehteþ 
Eft upon oþer half pellican þis fuhel haveþ anoþer cunde þet hit is aa leane 
Forþi as ich seide Daviþ eveneþ him þerto in ancre persone in ancre stevene Ich am pellican ilich þe wuneþ bi him 
ane Ant ancre ah þus to seggen ant beon ilich pellican onond þet hit is leane Judiþ bitund inne 
as hit teleþ in hire boc leadde swiþe heard lif feaste ant werede here Judiþ bitund 
inne bitacneþ bitund ancre þe ah to leaden heard lif as dude þe leafdi Judiþ efter hire 
evene nawt ase swin ipund i sti to feattin ant to greatin ayein þe cul of þe axe 
Twa cunnes ancren beoþ þet ure Laverd spekeþ of ant seiþ i þe Godspel of false 
ant of treowe þet is foxes habbeþ 
hare holen ant briddes of heovene habbeþ hare nestes þe foxes beoþ false ancres 
ase fox is beast falsest þeose habbeþ he seiþ holen þe holieþ inward eorþe wiþ 
eorþliche unþeawes ant draheþ into hare hole al þet ha mahen reopen ant rinnen 
þus beoþ gederinde ancres of Godd i þe Godspel to voxes ievenet Fox ec is a frech 
beast ant freotewil mid alle ant te false ancre draheþ into hire hole ant fret ase fox 
deþ baþe ges ant hennen Habbeþ efter þe vox a simple semblant sumchearre ant 
beoþ þah ful of gile Makieþ ham oþre þen ha beoþ ase vox þe is ypocrite Weneþ 
forte gili Godd as ha bidweolieþ simple men ant giliþ meast hamseolven Gealstriþ 
as þe vox deþ ant yelpeþ of hare god hwerse ha durren ant mahen chaffliþ of idel 
ant se swiþe worltliche iwurþeþ þet on ende hare nome stinkeþ as fox þer he geaþ 
forþ For yef ha doþ uvele me seiþ bi ham wurse 
þeos eoden into ancrehus as dude Saul into hole nawt as Daviþ þe gode Ba ha 
wenden into hole Saul ant Daviþ as hit teleþ i Regum ah Saul wende þider in forte 
don his fulþe þe rin as deþ bimong monie sum unseli ancrewent into hole of ancre
hus to bifule þet stude ant don dearnluker þe rin fleschliche fulþen þen ha mahten yef 
ha weren amidde þe worlde For hwa haveþ mare eise to don hire cweadschipes þen 
þe false ancre þus wende Saul into hole to bidon þet stude ah Daviþ wende þider 
in ane forte huden him from Saul þet him heatede ant sohte to sleanne Swa deþ þe 
gode ancre þe Saul þet is þe feond heateþ ant hunteþ efter Ha deþ hire in to 
huden hire from hise kene clokes Ha hud hire in hire hole ba from worltliche men ant 
worltliche sunnen Ant forþi ha is gasteliche Daviþ þet is strong toyein þe feond 
 ant hire leor lufsum to ure Laverdes ehnen for swa muchel seiþ þis word 
 Daviþ on Ebreische ledene þe false ancre is Saul efter þet his nome seiþ For Saul on Ebreisch is misnotunge on Englisch ant te false 
ancre misnoteþ ancre nome ant al þet ha wurcheþ þe gode ancre is Judiþ as we 
ear seiden þet is bitund as heo wes ant alswa as heo dude feasteþ wakeþ swinkeþ 
ant wereþ hearde Ha is of þe briddes þet ure Laverd spekeþ of efter þe voxes þe 
wiþ hare lustes ne holieþ nawt duneward ase doþ þe voxes þet beoþ false 
ancres ah habbeþ on heh ase brid of heovene iset hare nestes þet is hare reste 
Treowe ancres beoþ briddes icleopede for ha leaveþ þe eorþeþet is þe luve of 
alle worltliche þinges ant þurh yirnunge of heorte to heovenliche þinges fleoþ 
uppart toward heovene Ant tah ha fleon hehe wiþ heh lif ant hali haldeþ þah þe 
heaved lah þurh milde eadmodnesse as brid fleonninde buheþ þet heaved leoteþ al 
noht wurþ þet ha wel wurcheþ ant seggeþ as ure Laverd learde alle hise Hwen ye al habbeþ wel i
don he seiþ ure Laverd seggeþ þet ye beoþ unnete þrealles Fleoþ hehe ant 
haldeþ þah þet heaved eaver lahe þe wengen þe uppard beoreþ ham þet beoþ 
gode þeawes þet ha moten sturien into gode werkes as brid hwen hit fleo wule stureþ 
hise wengen þe treowe ancres yetten þe we to briddes eveniþ nawt we þah ah 
deþ Godd ha spreadeþ hare wengen ant makieþ creoiz of hamseolf as brid deþ 
hwen hit fliþ þet is i þoht of heorte ant i bitternesse of flesch beoreþ Godes rode 
þeo briddes fleoþ wel þe habbeþ lutel flesch as þe pellican haveþ ant feole 
fiþeren þe strucion for his muchele flesch ant oþre swucche fuheles makieþ a 
semblant to fleon ant beateþ þe wengen ah þe vet eaver draheþ to þer eorþe 
Alswa fleschlich ancre þe liveþ i flesches lustes ant folheþ hire eise þe hevinesse 
of hire flesch ant flesches unþeawes bineomeþ hire hire fluht ant tah ha makie semblant 
ant muche nurþ wiþ wengen oþres nawt hiren þet is leote of as þah ha fluhe 
ant were an hali ancre Hwase yeorne bihalt lahheþ hire to bismere for hire vet eaver 
as doþ þe strucions þet beoþ hire lustes draheþ to þer eorþe þeos ne beoþ 
nawt ilich þe leane fuhel pellican ne ne fleoþ nawt on heh ah beoþ eorþbriddes ant 
nisteþ on eorþe Ah Godd cleopeþ þe gode ancres briddes of heovene as ich ear 
seide Foxes habbeþ hare holen ant 
briddes of heovene habbeþ hare nestes Treowe ancres beoþ ariht briddes of heovene 
þe fleoþ on heh ant sitteþ singinde murie o þe grene bohes þet is þencheþ 
uppart of þe blisse of heovene þe neaver ne faleweþ ah is aa grene ant sitteþ o þis 
grene singinde murie þet is resteþ ham i þulli þoht ant ase þeo þe singeþ 
habbeþ murhþe of heorte Brid tah oþerhwile forte sechen his mete for þe flesches 
neode lihteþ to þer eorþe Ah hwil hit sit on eorþe hit nis neaver siker ah biwent him 
ofte ant bilokeþ him aa yeornliche abuten alswa þe gode ancre Ne fleo ha neaver se 
hehe ha mot lihten oþerhwiles dun to þer eorþe of hire bodi eoten drinken slepen 
wurchen speoken heren of þet hire neodeþ to of eorþliche þinges Ah þenne as þe 
brid deþ ha mot wel biseon hire bilokin hire on euch half þet ha nohwer ne misneome 
leste ha beo icaht þurh sum of þe deofles grunen oþer ihurt summesweis þe hwil 
ha sit se lahe 
 þeos briddes habbeþ nestes he seiþ ure Laverd Nest is 
heard utewiþ of prikinde þornes inwiþ nesche ant softe swa schal ancre ute
wiþ þolien heard on hire flesch ant prikiende pinen swa wisliche þah ha schal swenche 
þet flesch þet ha mahe seggen wiþ þe Psalmwruhte þet is ich chulle wite mi strengþe Laverd to þine bihove Forþi beo 
flesches pine efter euchanes evene þet nest beo heard wiþuten ant softe ant swete 
þe heorte wiþinnen þeo þe beoþ of bitter oþer of heard heorte ant nesche to hare 
flesch ha makieþ frommard hare nest softe wiþuten ant þorni wiþinnen þis beoþ 
þe weamode ant te estfule ancres bittre wiþinnen as þet swete schulde beon ant 
estfule wiþuten as þet hearde schulde beon þeos i þulli nest mahen habben uvel 
rest hwen ha ham wel biþencheþ for leate ha schulen bringe forþ briddes of swuch 
nest þet beoþ gode werkes þe fleon toward heovene Job cleopeþ nest þe ancre
hus ant seiþ as he were ancre þet is ich chulle deien i mi 
nest beon ase dead þe rin for þet is ancres rihte ant wunien aþet deaþ þe rin 
þet ich nulle neaver slakien hwil þe sawle is i þe buc to drehen heard wiþuten 
alswa as nest is ant softe beo wiþinnen 
Of dumbe beastes leorne wisdom ant lare þe earn deþ in his nest a deorewurþe 
yimstan achate hatte for nan attri þing ne mei þe stan nahhin ne hwil he is i þe 
nest hearmin his briddes þis deorewurþe stan þet is Jesu Crist ase stan treowe ant 
ful of alle mihtes over alle yimstanes he is þe achate þet atter of sunne ne nahhede 
neaver Do him i þi nest þet is i þin heorte þench hwuch pine he þolede on his 
flesch wiþuten hu swote he wes iheortet hu softe wiþinnen ant swa þu schalt 
driven ut euch atter of þin heorte ant bitternesse of þi bodi For i þulli þoht ne beo 
hit neaver se bitter pine þet tu þolie for þe luve of him þe droh mare for þe schal 
þunche þe swote þes stan as ich seide afleieþ attrie þinges Habbe þu þes stan 
inwiþ þi breoste þer Godes nest is Ne þearf þu noht dreden þe attri neddre of 
helle þine briddes þet beoþ þine gode werkes beoþ al sker of his atter 
Hwase ne mei þes yimstan habben ne halden i þe nest of hire heorte lanhure i þe 
nest of hire ancrehus habbe his iliche þet is þe crucifix Bihalde ofte þe ron ant 
cusse þe wundestuden i swote munegunge of þe soþe wunden þe he o þe soþe 
rode þuldeliche þolede Se vorþ se ha mei beo Judiþ þet is libben hearde beon 
cnawen ofte to Godd his muchele godlec toward hire ant hire fawtes toward him 
þet ha him yelt hit uvele Crie him yeorne þe rof mearci ant are ant schrive hire ilome 
þenne is ha Judiþ þe sloh Oloferne For Judiþ on Ebreisch is schrift on Englisch 
þet sleaþ gasteliche þen deovel of helle Forþi seiþ ancre to 
euch preost on alre earst ant schriveþ hire ofte forte beo Judiþ ant slean 
Oloferne þet is þe deofles strengþe For ase muchel seiþ þis nome Oloferne as 
 stinkinde in helle On Ebreische ledene 
Oloferne is þe feond þe makeþ feble ant unstrong feat kealf ant to wilde þet is 
þet flesch þe awildgeþ sone se hit eaver featteþ þurh eise ant þurh este Mi leof is ifeatted he seiþ ure Laverd ant smit me 
wiþ his hele Sone se flesch haveþ his wil hit regibeþ anan ase feat meare ant idel 
þis featte kealf haveþ þe feond strengþe to unstrengen ant buhen toward sunne for 
swa muche seiþ þis nome Oloferne Ah ancre schal beo Judiþ þurh heard lif ant 
þurh soþ schrift ant slean as dude Judiþ þes uvele Oloferne temie ful wel hire 
flesch sone se ha ifeleþ þet hit awilgeþ to swiþe mid feasten mid wecchen wiþ 
here wiþ heard swinc wiþ hearde disceplines wisliche þah ant wearliche þet is in euch 
sacrefise he seiþ ure Laverd offriþ me salt eaver Veaste wecche ant oþre swucche 
as ich nempnede nu beoþ mi sacrefises Salt bitacneþ wisdom for salt yeveþ mete 
smech ant wisdom yeveþ savur al þet we wel wurcheþ Wiþute salt of wisdom 
þuncheþ Godd smechles alle ure deden On oþer half wiþute salt flesch gedereþ 
wurmes stinkeþ swiþe fule ant forroteþ sone Alswa wiþute wisdom flesch as 
wurm forfret hire ant wasteþ hireseolven forfeareþ as þing þe forroteþ ant sleaþ 
hire on ende Ah þulli sacrefise stinkeþ ure Laverd 
þah þe flesch beo ure fa hit is us ihaten þet we halden hit up Wa we moten don 
hit as hit is wel ofte wurþe ah nawt fordon mid alle For hu wac se hit eaver beo 
þenne is hit swa icuplet ant se feste ifeiet to ure deorewurþe gast Godes ahne 
furme þet we mahten sone slean þet an wiþ þet oþer Ant tis is an of þe measte wundres on eorþe þet te heste þing under Godd 
þet is monnes sawle as Seint Austin witneþ schal beo se feste ifeiet to flesch þet 
nis bute fen ant a ful eorþe ant þurh þet ilke limunge luvien hit se swiþe þet ha for
te cwemen hit in his fule cunde geaþ ut of hire hehe heovenliche cunde ant forte 
paien hire wreaþeþ hire Schuppere þe scheop hire efter himseolf þet is king ant 
keiser of eorþe ant of heovene Wunder over wunder ant hokerlich wunder þet se 
unimete lah þing for neh nawt seiþ Seint Austin schal drahen into 
sunne se unimete heh þing ase sawle is þet Seint Awstin cleopeþ 
þet is for neh hest þing wiþute Godd Ah Godd nalde nawt þet ha lupe i prude ne 
wilnede to climben ant feolle as dude Lucifer for he wes bute charge ant teide forþi 
a clot of hevi eorþe to hire as me deþ þe cubbel to þe ku oþer to þe oþer beast þet 
is to recchinde ant renginde abuten þis is þet Job seide Laverd he seiþ þu havest imaket foþer to feþerin wiþ 
þe sawlen þet is þet hevie flesch þet draheþ hire duneward Ah þurh þe 
hehschipe of hire hit schal wurþe ful liht lihtre þen þe wind is ant brihtre þen þe 
sunne yef hit folheþ hire her ne ne draheþ hire to swiþe into hire lahe cunde Leove 
sustren for his luve þet ha is ilich to beoreþ hire menske ne leote ye nawt þe lahe 
flesch meistrin hire to swiþe Ha is her in uncuþþe iput in a prisun bitund in a 
cwalmhus ne nis nawt edscene of hwuch dignete ha is hu heh is hire cunde ne 
hwuch ha schal þunche yet in hire ahne riche þet flesch is her ed hame as eorþe þe 
is in eorþe ant is forþi cointe ant cover As me seiþ þet curre is kene on his ahne 
mixne Ha haveþ to much meistrie weilawei o monie Ah ancre as ich habbe iseid 
ah to beon al gastelich yef ha wule wel fleon as brid þet haveþ lutel flesch ant feole 
fiþeren Nawt ane yet tis ah teke þet ha temeþ wel hire fulitohe flesch ant strengeþ 
ant deþ menske þe wurþfule sawle teke þis ha mot yet þurh hire forbisne ant 
þurh hire hali beoden yeoven strengþe oþre ant uphalden ham þet ha ne fallen i þe 
dunge of sunne Ant forþi Daviþ anan efter þet he haveþ ievenet ancre to pellican 
he eveneþ hire to nihtfuhel þe is under evesunges 
þe nihtfuhel i þe evesunges bitacneþ recluses þe wunieþ forþi under chirche 
evesunges þet ha understonden þet ha ahen to beon of se hali lif þet al Hali Chirche
þet is Cristene folc leonie ant wreoþie upon ham ant heo halden hire up wiþ hare 
lif halinesse ant hare eadie bonen Forþi is ancre ancre icleopet ant under chirche 
iancret as ancre under schipes bord forte halden þet schip þet uþen ant stormes hit 
ne overwarpen Alswa al Hali Chirche þet is schip icleopet schal ancrin o þe ancre 
þet heo hit swa halde þet te deofles puffesþet beoþ temptatiuns ne hit overwarpen 
Euch ancre haveþ þis o foreward ba þurh nome of ancre ant þurh þet ha wuneþ 
under þe chirche to understiprin hire yef ha walde fallen Yef ha brekeþ foreward loki 
hwam ha lihe ant hu continuelement for ha ne stureþ neaver Ancre wununge ant hire 
nome yeieþ eaver þis foreward yet hwen ha slepeþ 
On oþer half þe nihtfuhel fliþ bi niht ant biyet i þeosternesse his fode Alswa 
schal ancre fleon wiþ contemplatiun þet is wiþ heh þoht ant wiþ hali bonen bi 
niht toward heovene ant biyeote bi niht hire sawle fode Bi niht ah ancre to beon 
waker ant bisiliche abuten gastelich biyete Forþi kimeþ anan þe refter Ich wes waker seiþ Daviþ 
in ancre persone ant ilich spearewe under rof ane ich wes waker for 
þet is ancre rihte muchel forte wakien Na þing ne awealdeþ wilde flesch ne ne makeþ hit tomre þen muche wecche 
Wecche is in Hali Writ i feole studen ipreiset Alswa as ye nulleþ nawt fallen into fondunge he seiþ ure Laverd 
 wakieþ ant ibiddeþ ow þet schal don ow stonden Eft he seiþ Eadi is þe ilke þet hwen ure Laverd kimeþ ifint wakiende 
Ant he himseolf sumchearre wakede i beoden al niht Ant 
swa he tahte us wecche nawt ane wiþ his lare ah dude wiþ his dede 
Eahte þinges nomeliche leaþieþ us to wakien eaver i sum god ant beo wurchinde 
þis scheorte lif þis stronge wei ure god þet is se þunne ure sunnen þe beoþ se 
monie deaþ þet we beoþ siker of ant unsiker hwenne þet sterke dom of Domes
dei ant se nearow mid alle þet euch idel word biþ þer ibroht forþ ant idele þohtes 
þe neren ear her ibette Loke nu hwet beo 
of unwreaste willes ant sunfule werkes Yet þe seoveþe þing þe munegeþ us to 
wakien þet is þe sorhe of helle þer bihald þreo þing þe untaleliche pinen þe 
echnesse of euchan þe unimete bitternesse þe eahtuþe þing hu muchel is þe 
mede i þe blisse of heovene world buten ende Hwase wakeþ her wel ane hond
hwile hwase haveþ þeos eahte þing ofte in hire heorte ha wule schaken of hire slep 
of uvel slawþe I þe stille niht hwen me ne siþ nawiht nowþer ne ne hereþ þet lette 
þe bone þe heorte is ofte se schir for na þing nis witnesse of þing þet me þenne 
deþ bute Godes engel þe is i swuch time bisiliche abuten to eggin us to gode For þer 
nis nawt forloren as is bi dei ofte Hercniþ nu leove sustren hu hit is uvel to uppin ant 
hu god þing hit is to heolen goddede ant fleo bi niht as nihtfuhel ant gederin bi 
þeostre þet is i privite ant dearnliche sawle fode þet is Hesteres bone þe cwen wes þe 
King Assuer licwurþe ant icweme Hester on Ebreisch þet is ihud on Englisch 
ant is to understonden þet bone ant oþer goddede þet is idon on hudles is Assuer i
cweme þet is þe king of heovene For Assuer on Ebreisch is eadi on Englisch 
 þet is ure Laverd þe is eadi over alle Daviþ spekeþ to ancre þe wes iwunet in 
hudles wel forte wurchen ant seoþþen o sum wise uppeþ hit ant schaweþ þet is 
 hwi drahest tu ut þin hond ant yet ti riht hond of midde þi bosum on 
ende Riht hond is god werc Bosum is privite ant is as þah he seide þe riht hond 
þet tu heolde ancre i þi bosum þet is þi gode werc þet tu hefdest idon privement 
as þing is dearne i bosum hwi drahest tu hit ut on ende þet is þet 
ti mede endi se sone þi mede þet were endeles yef þi goddede ihole were Hwi 
openest tu hit ant nimest se scheort mede hure þet is agan in an hondhwile þu havest iuppet þi god he seiþ ure 
Laverd witerliche þu havest undervo þi mede Sein Gregoire awundreþ him ant 
seiþ þet men beoþ wode þe trochiþ swa uvele Muchel meadschipe hit is he seiþ don wel ant wilni word þe rof don 
hwerþurh he buþ þe kinedom of heovene ant sullen hit for a windes puf of wordes 
hereword of monnes herunge Forþi mine leove sustren haldeþ ower riht hond in
wiþ ower bosum leste mede endeles neome scheort ende We redeþ in Hali Writ þet 
Moyseses hond Godes prophete sone se he hefde idrahen hire ut of his bosum bisemde 
þe spiteluvel ant þuhte lepruse þurh hwet is bitacnet þet goddede idrahe forþ 
nis nawt ane forloren þurh þet uppinge ah þuncheþ yet eatelich bivore Godes ehe as 
spiteluvel is eatelich bivore monnes sihþe Lo a feorli god word þet te hali Job seiþ I mi bosum he seiþ is al min hope i
halden as þah he seide hwet god se ich do were hit ut of bosum iuppet ant idrahe 
forþ al min hope were edslopen Ah forþi þet ich hit heole ant hude as i bosum ich 
hopie to mede Forþi yef ei deþ eani god ne drahe ha hit nawt utward ne yelpe na
wiht þe rof for wiþ a lutel puf wiþ a wordes wind hit mei beon al toweavet 
Ure Laverd i Johel meaneþ him swiþe of þeo þe forleoseþ ant spilleþ al hare god 
þurh wilnunge of hereword ant seiþ þeos wordes Allas seiþ ure Laverd þeos 
þe schaweþ hire god haveþ bipilet mi fier irend al þe rinde of despuilet hire steort
naket ant iwarpen awei ant te grene bohes beoþ fordruhede ant forwurþen to drue 
hwite rondes þis word is dosc ah neomeþ nu yeme hu ich hit wulle brihtin Fier is 
a cunnes treo þe bereþ swete frut þet me cleopeþ figes þenne is þe fier bipilet 
ant te rinde irend of hwen goddede is iuppet þenne is þe lif ut þenne adeadeþ þe 
treo hwen þe rinde is awei ne nowþer ne bereþ hit frut ne greneþ þe refter i lufsume 
leaves ah druhieþ þe bohes ant wurþeþ hwite rondes to na þing betere þen to 
fures fode þe boh hwen hit adeadeþ hit hwiteþ utewiþ ant adruheþ inwiþ ant 
warpeþ his rinde Alswa goddede þe wule adeadin forwarpeþ his rinde þet is 
unhuleþ him þe rinde þe wriþ hit is þe treoes warde ant wit hit i strengþe ant i 
cwicnesse Alswa þe hulunge is þe goddedes lif ant halt hit i strengþe Ah hwen þe 
rinde is offe þenne as þe boh deþ hwiteþ hit utewiþ þurh worltlich hereword ant 
adruheþ inwiþ ant leoseþ þe swetnesse of Godes grace þe makede hit grene ant lic
wurþe Godd to bihalden For grene over alle heowes frovreþ meast ehnen Hwen 
hit is swa adruhet þenne nis hit to nawt se god as to þe fur of helle for þe earste 
bipilunge hwerof al þis uvel is nis bute of prude Ant nis þis muche reowþe þet te 
fier þe schulde wiþ hire swete frut þet is goddede fede Godd gasteliche þe 
Laverd of heovene schal adruhien rindeles þurh þet hit is unhulet ant wurþen buten 
ende helle fures fode Ant nis ha to unseli þe wiþ þe wurþ of heovene buþ hire helle 
Ure Laverd i þe Godspel seolf eveneþ heoveriche to goldhord þe hwase hit fint 
as he seiþ hudeþ hit Golthord is goddede 
þe is to heovene ievenet for me hit buþ þerwiþ ant þis golthord bute hit beo þe 
betere ihud ant iholen hit is forlore sone For as Sein Gregoire seiþ þe bereþ tresor openliche i wei 
þet is al ful of reaveres ant of þeoves him luste leosen hit ant beon irobbet þis 
world nis bute a wei to heovene oþer to helle ant is al biset of hellene mucheres þe 
robbiþ alle þe golthordes þet ha mahen underyeoten þet mon oþer wummon i þis 
wei openeþ For ase muchel wurþ is as hwase seide ant yeide as he eode Ich beore 
golthord Ich beore golthord Lowr hit her read gold hwit seolver inoh ant deore
wurþe stanes A sapere þe ne bereþ bute sape ant nelden yeiyeþ hehe þet he bereþ 
A riche mercer geaþ forþ al stille Freiniþ hwet itidde of Ezechie þe gode king for
þi þet he schawde þe celles of his aromaz his muchele þinges his deorewurþe 
tresor Nis hit nawt for nawt iwriten i þe hali Godspel of þe þreo kinges þe comen to 
offrin Jesu Crist þe deore þreo lakes þet tet ha walden offrin him ha heolden eaver 
ihud aþet ha comen bivoren him þa earst ha unduden þe presenz þet ha beren For
þi mine leove sustren bi niht as þe nihtfuhel þet ancre is to ievenet beoþ yeorne 
sturiende Niht ich cleopie privite þis niht ye mahen habben euch time of þe dei þet 
al þe god þet ye eaver doþ beo idon as bi niht ant bi þeosternesse ut of monnes ehe 
ut of monnes eare þus i niht beoþ fleonninde ant sechinde ower sawle heovenliche 
fode þenne ne beo ye nawt ane ah beoþ ec Yet is ancre ievenet her to 
spearewe þet is ane under rof as ancre Spearewe is a chiterinde brid chitereþ aa ant 
chirmeþ Ah forþi þet moni ancre haveþ þet ilke unþeaw Daviþ ne eveneþ hire 
nawt to spearewe þe haveþ fere ah deþ to spearewe ane 
 Ich am he seiþ bi ancre as spearewe þet is ane For swa ah ancre hire ane in 
anlich stude as ha is chirmin ant chiterin eaver hire bonen Ant understondeþ leofliche 
mine leove sustren þet ich write of anlich lif forte frovrin ancren ant ow over alle 
Hu god is to beon ane is ba i þe alde lahe ant i þe neowe isutelet For i baþe me i
fint þet Godd his dearne runes ant heovenliche privitez schawde his leoveste freond 
nawt i monne floc ah dude þer ha weren ane bi hamseolven Ant heo hamseolf alswa 
as ofte as ha walden þenchen schirliche of Godd ant makien cleane bonen ant beon in 
heorte gasteliche ihehet toward heovene aa me ifint þet ha fluhen monne sturbunge 
ant wenden bi ham ane ant þer Godd edeawde ham ant schawde himseolf to ham ant 
yef ham hare bonen Forþi þet ich seide þet me ifint tis ba i þe alde testament ant ec 
i þe neowe ich chulle of ba twa schawin forbisne Ysaac þe patriarche forte þenche deopliche sohte anlich stude 
ant wende bi him ane as Genesys teleþ Ant swa he imette wiþ þe eadi Rebecca 
þet is wiþ Godes grace Alswa þe eadi Jacob þa ure Laverd schawde 
him his deorewurþe nebscheft ant yef him his blesceunge ant wende his nome betere 
he wes iflohe men ant wes him al ane Neaver yete i monne floc ne cahte he swuch 
biyete Bi Moysen ant bi Helye Godes deorewurþe freond is sutel ant edscene hwuch 
baret ant hu dredful lif is eaver imong þrung ant hu Godd his privitez schaweþ to 
þeo þe beoþ privement ham ane Me schal leove sustren þeose estoires tellen ow 
for ha weren to longe to writen ham here ant þenne schule ye al þis brihte understonden þe eadi Jeremie seiþ he sit ane ant seiþ þe reisun for
hwi Ure Laverd hefde ifullet him of his 
þreatunge Godes þreatunge is wontreaþe ant weane i licome ant i sawle worlt buten 
ende þe were of þis þreatunge as he wes wel ifullet nere þer nan empti stude i þe 
heorte to underfon fleschliche lahtren Forþi he bed wealle of teares þet ha ne adruhede neaver na mare þen wealle forte 
biwepe slei folc þet is meast al þe world þet is gasteliche islein mid deadliche 
sunnen Ant to þis wop lokiþ nu he bit anlich 
stude þe hali 
prophete forte schawi witerliche þet hwase wule biwepen hire ahne ant oþres sunnen 
as ancre ah to donne ant hwase wule ifinden ed te nearewe domesmon mearci ant 
are a þing þet let him meast is beowiste þet is wununge bimong men ant þet 
swiþest furþreþ hit þet is anlich stude mon oþer wummon eiþer to beon ane Yet 
spekeþ Jeremie of anlich stude mare Me schal sitten 
he seiþ him ane ant beo stille Of þis stilnesse he spekeþ þerbivoren lutel God hit is i silence ikepen Godes grace ant þet me beore Godes 
yeoc anan from his yuheþe ant þenne kimeþ þe refter Hwase swa wule don ha schal sitten ane ant halden hire 
stille ant swa heoven hireseolf buven hireseolven þet is wiþ heh lif hehi toward

smitere beode forþ þe cheke ant beo þurhfullet wiþ schentfule wordes Her beoþ

þolemodnesse i þe earre half i þe leatere eadmodnesse of milde ant meoke heorte 
For þolemod is þe þuldeliche abereþ woh þet me him deþ Eadmod is þe þolie 
mei þet me him missegge þeos þe ich habbe inempnet her weren of þe alde 
testament Cume we nu to þe neowe 
Sein Juhan Baptiste bi hwam ure Laverd seide þet bimong wives sunen ne aras neaver herre 
he kenneþ us openliche bi his ahne dede þet anlich stude is baþe siker ant biheve For 
þah þe engel Gabriel hefde his burde ibocket al were he ifullet of þe Hali Gast anan 
inwiþ his moder wombe al were he þurh miracle of baraigne iboren ant in his i
nobr>borenesse unspende his feader tunge into prophecie for al þis ne durste he yet 
wunie bimong men se dredful lif he seh þe rin þah hit nere of nawt elles bute of 
speche ane Ant forþi hwet dude he Yung of yeres fleh awei into wildernesse leste 
he wiþ speche sulde his cleane lif for swa is in his ymne He hefde as hit þuncheþ iherd Ysaie þe meande him ant seide Wumme wa is me he seiþ þe hali prophete for 
ich am a mon of sulede lippen ant seiþ þe acheisun hwervore Ant þet is forþi he seiþ þet ich 
wunie bimong men þe suleþ hare lippen mid misliche spechen Lo hu Godes prophete 
seiþ he wes isulet þurh beowiste bimong monne Swa hit is sikerliche beo neaver se 
briht or metal gold seolver irn stel þet hit ne schal drahe rust of anoþer þet is i
rustet forhwon þet ha longe liggen togedere Forþi fleh Sein Juhan þe feolahschipe 
of fule men leste he were ifulet Ah yet forte schawin us þet me ne mei þe uvele 
fleon bute me fleo þe gode he fleh his hali cun icoren of ure Laverd ant wende into 
anli stude ant wunede i þe wildernesse Ant hwet biyet he þer He biyet þet he wes 
Godes baptiste O þe muchele hehnesse þet he heold i fulluht under hise honden þe 
Laverd of heovene þe halt up al þe world wiþ his anes mihte þer þe Hali Trinite 
 þrumnesse on Englisch schawde hire al to him þe Feader in his stevene þe Hali 
Gast i culvre heow þe Sune in his honden In anlich lif he biyet þreo preminences 
privilegie of preachur merite of martirdom meidenes mede þeos þreo manere men 
habbeþ in heovene wiþ overfullet mede crune upo crune Ant te eadi Juhan in anlich 
stude as he wes alle þeose þreo estaz ofearnede him ane 
Ure leove Leafdi ne leadde ha anlich lif Ne fond te engel hire in anli stude al ane 
Nes ha nowher ute ah wes biloken feste for swa we ifindeþ 
þet is þe engel wende into hire þenne wes heo inne in anli stude hire ane Engel 
to mon i þrung ne edeawede neaver ofte On oþer half þurh þet nowher in Hali Writ 
nis iwriten of hire speche bute fowr siþen as is iseid þe ruppe sutel prufunge hit is 
þet ha wes muchel ane þe heold swa silence 
Hwet seche ich oþer Of Godd ane were inoh forbisne to alle þe wende himseolf 
into anli stude ant feaste þeras he wes ane i wildernesse forte schawin þerbi þet 
bimong monne þrung ne mei nan makien riht penitence þer in anli stude him 
hungrede hit seiþ ancre to frovre þet is meoseise þer he þolede þet te feond 
fondede him feoleweis ah he overcom him alswa forte schawin þet te feond fondeþ 
muchel þeo þe leadeþ anlich lif for onde þet he haveþ to ham Ah he is þer overcumen 
for ure Laverd seolf þer stont bi ham i fehte ant bealdeþ ham hu ha schulen stonden 
strongliche ayein ant yeveþ ham of his strengþe He as Hali Writ seiþ þet na nurþ 
ne þrung of folc ne mahte letten him of his beoden ne desturbin his god he þah no
þeleatere hwen he walde beon i beoden he fleh nawt ane oþre men ah dude yet his 
halie deorewurþe apostles ant wende ane upon hulles us to forbisne þet we schule 
turne bi usseolf ant climben wiþ him on hulles þet is þenchen hehe ant leaven lahe 
under us alle eorþliche þohtes hwiles we beoþ i bonen Pawel ant Antonie Hylariun 
ant Benedict Sincletice ant Sare ant oþre swucche monie men ant wummen baþe 
fondeden witerliche ant underyeten soþliche þe biyete of anlich lif as þeo þe duden

men ich wende from ham leasse mon þen ich ear wes Forþi seiþ þe wise 
Ecclesiasticus þet is ne 
þunche þe neaver god imong monne floc for þer is eaver sunne Ne seide þe 
stevene to Arsenie of heovene Arseni flih 
men ant tu schalt beon iborhen Ant eft hit com ant seide 
þet is Arseni flih beo stille ant wune studevestliche i sum stude ut of monne 
Nu ye habbeþ iherd mine leove sustren forbisne of þe alde lahe ant ek of þe 
neowe hwi ye ahen anlich lif swiþe to luvien Efter þe forbisnes hereþ nu reisuns hwi 
me ah to fleo þe world eahte ed te leaste Ich ham segge scheortliche neomeþ þe 
betere yeme 
þe forme is sikernesse Yef a wod liun urne yont te strete nalde þe wise bitunen 
hire sone Ant Seinte Peter seiþ þet helle liun rengeþ ant reccheþ eaver abuten forte 
sechen inyong sawle to forswolhen ant bid us beo wakere ant bisie in hali beoden leste 
he us lecche þis is Seinte Petres word þet 
ich ear seide Forþi beoþ ancren wise þe habbeþ wel bitund ham ayein helle liun for
te beo þe sikerure 
þe oþer reisun is þe bere a deore licur a deorewurþe wet as basme is in a 
feble vetles healewi i bruchel gles nalde ha gan ut of þrung bute ha fol were þis bruchele vetles þet is 
wummone flesch þah noþeleatere þe basme þe healewi is meidenhad þet is þe rin 
oþer efter meiþlure chaste cleannesse þis bruchele vetles is bruchel as is 
eani gles For beo hit eanes tobroken ibet ne biþ hit neaver ibet ne hal as hit wes ear 
na mare þene gles Ah yet hit brekeþ mid leasse þen bruchel gles do For gles ne 
tobrekeþ nawt bute sum þing hit rine ant hit onont meiþlure mei leosen his halnesse 
wiþ a stinkinde wil swa vorþ hit mei gan ant leaste se longe Ah þis manere bruche 
mei beon ibet eft ase hal allunge as hit wes eaver halest þurh medecine of schrift ant 
bireowsunge Nu þe preove herof Sein Juhan Ewangeliste nefde he brud ibroht 
ham Nefde he iþoht þa yef Godd nefde ilet him meiþhad to forleosen 
Seoþþen þah nes he meiden neaver þe unhalre ah wes meiden bitaht meiden to 
witene Nu as ich segge þis deorewurþe healewi 
i bruchel vetles is meiþhad ant cleannesse in ower bruchele flesch bruchelure þen eani 
gles þet yef ye weren i worldes þrung wiþ a lutel hurlunge ye mahten al leosen as þe 
wrecches i þe world þe hurliþ togederes ant breokeþ hare vetles ant cleannesse 
schedeþ Forþi ure Laverd cleopeþ þus Leaveþ þe world ant cumeþ to me for þer ye schulen beon i þrung ah 
reste ant peis is in me 
þe þridde reisun of þe worldes fluht is þe biyete of heovene þe heovene is 
swiþe heh Hwase wule biyeoten hit ant areachen þerto hire is lutel inoh forte 
warpen al þe world under hire fotes Forþi alle þe halhen makeden of al þe world as 
a scheomel to hare vet to areache þe heovene þis is Sein Juhanes word Ewangeliste i þe Apocalipse 
 Ich iseh a wummon ischrud mid te sunne ant under hire vet þe mone þe mone 
woneþ ant waxeþ ne nis neaver studevest ant bitacneþ forþi worltliche þinges 
þe beoþ as þe mone eaver i change þes mone mot te wummon halden under hire 
vet þet is worldliche þinges totreoden ant forhohien þe wule heovene areachen 
ant beo þer ischrud mid te soþe sunne 
þe feorþe reisun is preove of noblesce ant of largesce Noble men ant gentile ne 
beoreþ nane packes ne ne feareþ itrusset wiþ trussews ne wiþ purses Hit is 
beggilde riht to beore bagge on bac burgeise to beore purse nawt Godes spuse þe 
is leafdi of heovene Trussen ant purses baggen ant packes beoþ worltliche þinges 
alle eorþliche weolen ant worltliche rentes 
þe fifte resiun is noble men ant wummen makieþ large relef ah hwa mei makie 
largere þen þe oþer þeo þe seiþ wiþ Seinte Peter Laverd forte folhi þe we habbeþ al forleavet Nis þis large 
relef Nis þis muche lave Mine leove sustren kinges ant keisers habbeþ hare liveneþ 
of ower large relef þet ye ileavet habbeþ Laverd forte folhi þe seiþ Seinte Peter 
 we habbeþ al forleavet as þah he seide we wulleþ folhi þe i þe muchele genterise 
of þi largesce þu leafdest to oþre men alle richesces ant makedest of al relef ant lave 
se large We wulleþ folhi þe We wulleþ don alswa leaven al as þu dudest folhi þe 
on eorþe i þet ant in oþerhwet forte folhi þe ec into þe blisse of heovene ant 
yet tear over al folhi þe hwiderward se þu eaver wendest as nane ne mahen bute ane 
meidnes 
þe seste reisun is hwi ye habbeþ þe world iflohen familiarite muche cun
redden forte beo prive wiþ ure Laverd For þus he seiþ bi Osee Ich chulle leade þe he seiþ to his leofmon 
 into anli stude ant ter ich chulle luveliche speoke to þin heorte for me is laþ preasse 
þe seoveþe reisun is forte beo þe brihtre ant brihtluker seon in heovene Godes 
brihte nebscheft for ye beoþ iflohe þe world ant hudeþ ow for hire her Yet terteken 
þet ye beon swifte as þe sunne gleam for ye beoþ wiþ Jesu Crist bitund as i sepulcre 
bibarret as he wes o þe deore rode as is iseid þe ruppe 
þe eahtuþe reisun is to habben cwic bone ant lokiþ yeorne hwervore þe 
eadmode cwen Hester bitacneþ ancre for hire nome seiþ ihud on Englische ledene 
As me ret in hire boc ha wes þe King Assuer over al icweme ant þurh hire bone 
arudde of deaþ al hire folc þe wes to deaþ idemet þis nome Assuer is ispealet 
 eadi as is ear iseid ant bitacneþ Godd eadi over alle He yetteþ Hester þe cwen 
þet is þe treowe ancre þet is riht Hester þet is riht ihud he hereþ ant yetteþ 
hire alle hire benen ant sawveþ þurh ham muche folc Monie schulde beo forloren þe 
beoþ þurh þe ancre benen iborhen as weren þurh Hesteres forhwon þet ha beo 
Hester ant halde hire as heo dude Mardochees dohter Mardoche is ispealet þet is bitterliche totreodinde þene scheomelese 
Scheomeles is þe mon þe seiþ eani untu oþer deþ bivoren ancre Yef eani þah swa 
do ant heo breoke bitterliche his untohe word oþer his fol dede totreode ham ananriht 
wiþ unwurþ tellunge þenne is ha Hester Mardochees dohter bitterliche breokinde 
þene scheomelese Bitterluker ne betere ne mei ha him neaver breoken þen is itaht 
þ ruppe wiþ oþer mid tis vers ant wende inward anan toward hire weovede ant halde 
hire ed hame as Hester þe ihudde Semei i Regum hefde deaþ ofservet ah he 
criede mearci ant Salomon foryef hit him þah þurh swuch a foreward þet he ed 
hame heolde him i Jerusalem as he wunede ant hudde him in his huse yef he ohwider 
wende ut swuch wes þe foreward þet he were eft al ful ant to deaþ idemet He 
þah brec foreward þurh his unselhþe His þrealles edfluhen him ant edbreken him ut 
ant he folhede ham ant wende ut efter ham hwet wult tu mare wes sone forwreiet 
to þe king Salomon ant for þe foreward tobroken wes fordemet to deaþe 
Understondeþ yeorne þis mine leove sustren Semey bitacneþ þe utwarde ancre 
nawt Hester þe ihudde For Semey seiþ þet is herinde on ure ledene 
þet is þe recluse þe haveþ asse earen longe to here feor þet is hercninde efter ut
runes Semeis stude wes Jerusalem þet he schulde in huden him yef he walde libben 
þis word Jerusalem spealeþ sihþe of peis ant bitacneþ ancrehus For þe rinne 
ne þearf ha seon bute peis ane Ne beo neaver Semei þet is þe recluse swa swiþe 
forgult toward te soþe Salomon þet is ure Laverd Halde hire ed hame i Jerusalem 
þet ha nawiht nute of þe worldes baret Salomon yetteþ hire bliþeliche his are ah yef 
ha entremeateþ hire of þinges wiþuten mare þen ha þurfte ant hire heorte beo ute
wiþ þah a clot of eorþe þet is hire licome beo inwiþ þe fowr wahes ha is 
iwend wiþ Semei ut of Jerusalem alswa as he dude efter his þrealles þeos þrealles 
beoþ þe eþele fif wittes þe schulden beon et hame ant servin hare leafdi þenne ha 
serviþ wel þe ancre hare leafdi hwen ha notieþ ham wel in hare sawle neode hwen 
þe ehe is o þe boc oþer o sum oþer god þe eare to Godes word þe muþ in hali bonen 
Yef ha wit ham uvele ant let ham þurh yemeles etfleon hire servise ant folhi ham utwart 
wiþ hire heorte as hit bitimeþ eaver meast þet gan þe wittes ut þe heorte geaþ ut 
efter ha brekeþ Salomon foreward wiþ þe unseli Semey ant is to deaþ idemet 
Forþi mine leove sustren ne beo ye nawt Semey ah beoþ Hester þe ihudde 
ant ye schule beon ihehet i þe blisse of heovene For þe nome of Hester ne seiþ nawt 
ane þet is nawt ane ihud ah deþ þerteken þet is i folc ihehet Ant swa wes Hester as hire nome cwiddeþ ihehet to cwen 
of a povre meiden I þis word Hester beoþ hudunge ant hehnesse ifeiet togederes 
ant nawt ane hehnesse ah hehnesse over folc forte schawin witerliche þet teo þe 
hudeþ ham ariht in hare ancrehus ha schulen beon in heovene over oþres cunnes 
folc wurþliche ihehet Ba Hesteres nome ant hire hehunge pruvieþ þet ich segge On 
oþer half understondeþ ye beoþ i Jerusalem Ye beoþ iflohe to chirche griþ For nis 
ower nan þet nere sumchearre Godes þeof Me weiteþ ow þet wite ye ful yeorne 
 wiþuten as me deþ þeoves þe beoþ ibroke to chirche Haldeþ ow feaste inne 
Nawt te bodi ane for þet is þe unwurþest ah ower fif wittes ant te heorte over al ant 
al þer þe sawle lif is For beo ha bitrept utewiþ nis þer bute leade forþ toward te 
gealforke þet is þe wearitreo of helle Beoþ ofdred of euch mon alswa as þe 
þeof is leste he drahe ow utwart þet is biswike wiþ sunne ant weiti forte 
warpen upon ow his cleches Bisecheþ yeornliche Godd as þeof ibroke to chirche 
þet he wite ant wardi ow wiþ alle þe ow weitiþ Chiteriþ ower beoden aa as spearewe 
deþ þet is ane for þis an word is iseid of anlich lif of anlich stude þer me mei 
beon Hester ihud ut of þe world ant do betere þen i þrung euch gastelich biyete 
Forþi eveneþ Daviþ ancre to pellican þet leat anlich lif ant to spearewe ane 
Spearewe haveþ yet a cunde þet is biheve ancre þah me hit heatie þet is þe 
fallinde uvel For muche neod is þet ancre of hali lif ant of heh habbe fallinde uvel þet 
uvel ne segge ich nawt þet me swa nempneþ ah fallinde uvel ich cleopie licomes 
secnesse oþer temptatiuns of flesches fondunges hwerþurh hire þunche þet ha falle 
duneward of hali hehnesse Ha walde awilgin elles oþer to wel leoten of hireseolven 
ant swa to noht iwurþen þe flesch walde awilgin ant bicumen to fulitohen toward 
hire leafdi yef hit nere ibeaten ant makie sec þe sawle yef secnesse hit ne 
temede wiþ uvel oþer wiþ sunne 
þe licome ne þe gast yef hare nowþer nere sec as hit timeþ seldene orhel 
walde awakenin þet is þe measte dredfule secnesse of alle Yef Godd fondeþ ancre 
wiþ ei uvel utewiþ oþer þe feonde inwiþ wiþ gasteliche unþeawes ase prude 
wreaþþe onde oþer wiþ flesches lustes ha haveþ þet fallinde uvel þet me seiþ is 
spearewe uvel Godd hit wule forþi þet ha beo eaver eadmod ant wiþ lah haldunge of 
hireseolven falle to þer eorþe leste ha falle i prude 
Nu we hurteþ leove sustren to þe feorþe dale þet ich seide schulde beon of feole 
fondunges for þer beoþ uttre ant inre ant eiþer monivalde Salve ich bihet to teachen 
toyeines ham ant bote ant hu hwase haveþ ham mei gederin of þis dale cunfort ant 
frovre toyeines ham alle þet ich þurh þe lare of þe Hali Gast mote halden foreward 
he hit yetti me þurh ower bonen 
</td>

<td align=left valign=top>
Ne wene nan of heh lif þet ha ne beo itemptet mare beoþ þe gode þe
beoþ iclumben hehe itemptet þen þe wake ant þet is reisun For se 
þe hul is herre se þe wind is mare þe ron Se þe hul is herre of hali lif 
ant of heh se þe feondes puffes þe windes of fondunges beoþ strengre 
þ ron ant mare Yef ei ancre is þe ne veleþ nane fondunges swiþe drede i þet 
puint þet ha beo overmuchel ant overswiþe ifondet For swa Sein Gregoire 
seiþ Sec mon haveþ 
twa estaz swiþe dredfule þet an is hwen he ne feleþ nawt his ahne secnesse ant 
forþi ne secheþ nawt leche ne lechecreft ne easkeþ namon read ant asteorveþ 
ferliche ear me least wene þis is þe ancre þe nat nawt hwet is fondunge To 
þeos spekeþ þe engel i þe Apocalipse þu seist þe nis neod na 
medecine ah þu art blind iheortet ne ne sist nawt hu þu art povre ant naket of 
halinesse ant gastelich wrecche þet oþer dredfule estat þet te seke haveþ is al 
frommard þis þet is hwen he feleþ se muchel angoise þet he ne mei þolien 
þet me hondli his sar ne þet me him heale þis is sum ancre þe feleþ se swiþe 
hire fondunges ant is se sare ofdred þet na gastelich cunfort ne mei hire gleadien 
ne makien to understonden þet ha mahe ant schule þurh ham þe betere beon i
borhen Ne teleþ hit i þe Godspel þet te Hali Gast leadde ure Laverd seolf into 
anlich stude to leaden anlich lif forte beon itemptet of þe unwine of helle Ah his 
temptatiun þe ne mahte sunegin wes ane wiþuten 
Understondeþ þenne on alre earst leove sustren þet twa cunne temptatiuns 
twa cunne fondunges beoþ uttre ant inre ant ba beoþ feolevalde Uttre 
fondunge is hwerof kimeþ licunge oþer mislicunge wiþuten oþer wiþinnen 
Mislicunge wiþuten ase secnesse meoseise scheome unhap ant euch licomlich 
derf þet te flesch eileþ Wiþinnen heorte sar grome ant wreaþþe alswa 
onont þet ha is pine Licunge wiþuten licomes heale mete drunch claþ inoh 
ant euch flesches eise onont swucche þinges Licunge wiþinnen as sum fals 
gleadschipe oþer of monne hereword oþer yef me is iluvet mare þen anoþer 
mare iolhnet mare idon god oþer menske þis dale of þis temptatiun þet is 
uttre icleopet is swikelure þen þe oþer half Ba beoþ a temptatiun ant eiþer 
wiþinnen ant wiþuten baþe of hire twa dalen Ah ha is uttre icleopet for ha is 
eaver oþer i þing wiþuten oþer of þing wiþuten ant te uttre þing is þe 
fondunge þeos fondunge kimeþ oþerhwile of Godd of mon oþerhwiles Of 
Godd as of freondes deaþ secnesse oþer on ham oþer o þeseolven poverte 
mishapnunge ant oþre swucche heale alswa ant eise 
Of mon as mislich woh oþer of word oþer of werc o þe oþer o þine 
alswa hereword oþer goddede þeos cumeþ alswa of Godd ah nawt as doþ 
þe oþre wiþuten euch middel Ah wiþ alle he fondeþ mon hu he him drede ant 
luvie Inre fondunges beoþ misliche unþeawes oþer lust towart ham oþer þohtes 
swikele þe þuncheþ þah gode þeos inre fondunge kimeþ of þe feond of þe 
world of ure flesch oþerhwile To þe uttre temptatiun is neod patience þet 
is þolemodnesse To þe inre is neod wisdom ant gastelich strengþe We schulen 
nu speoken of þe uttre ant teachen þeo þe habbeþ hire hu ha mahen wiþ Godes 
grace ifinde remedie þet is elne ayeines hire to frovrin hamseolven Eadi is ant seli þe haveþ 
i temptatiun þolemodnesse for hwen ha is ipruvet hit seiþ ha schal beon i
crunet mid te crune of lif þe Godd haveþ bihaten his leove icorene Hwen ha 
is ipruvet hit seiþ Wel is hit iseid for alswa pruveþ Godd his leove i
corene as þe goltsmiþ fondeþ þet gold i þe fure þet false gold forwurþeþ 
þ rin þet gode kimeþ ut brihtre Secnesse is a brune hat forte þolien ah na 
þing ne clenseþ gold as hit deþ þe sawle 
Secnesse þet Godd send nawt þet sum lecheþ þurh hire ahne dusischipe 
 deþ þeose six þinges i wescheþ þe sunnen þe beoþ ear iwrahte ii 
wardeþ toyein þeo þe weren towardes iii pruveþ pacience iiii halt in 
eadmodnesse v muchleþ þe mede vi eveneþ to martir þene þolemode 
þus is secnesse sawlene heale salve of hire wunden scheld þet ha ne kecche 
ma as Godd siþ þet ha schulde yef secnesse hit ne lette Secnesse makeþ mon 
to understonden hwet he is to cnawen himseolven ant as god meister beat 
forte leorni wel hu mihti is Godd hu frakel is þe worldes blisse Secnesse is þi 
goldsmiþ þe i þe blisse of heovene overguldeþ þi crune Se þe secnesse is 
mare se þe goltsmiþ is bisgre ant se hit lengre least se he brihteþ hire swiþere 
to beo martirs evening þurh a hwilinde wa Hwet is mare grace to þeo þe hefde 
ofearnet þe pinen of helle world abuten ende Nalde me tellen him alre monne 
dusegest þe forseke a buffet for a speres wunde a nelde pricchunge for an 
bihefdunge a beatunge for an hongunge on helle wearitreo aa on ecnesse Godd 
hit wat leove sustren al þe wa of þis world is ievenet to helle alre leaste pine 
Al nis bute balplohe Al nis nawt swa muchel as is a lutel deawes drope toyeines 
þe brade sea ant alle worldes weattres þe mei þenne edstearten þet ilke grisliche 
wa þe eateliche pinen þurh secnesse þet ageaþ þurh ei uvel þet her is seliliche 
mei ha seggen 
On oþer half leorniþ monivalde frovren ayein þe uttre fondunge þe kimeþ 
of monnes uvel for þeos þe ich habbe iseid of is of Godes sonde Hwase 
eaver misseiþ þe oþer misdeþ þe nim yeme ant understond þet he is þi vile 
þe lorimers habbeþ ant fileþ al þi rust awei ant ti ruhe of sunne For he fret 
himseolven weilawei as þe file deþ ah he makeþ smeþe ant brihteþ þi sawle 
On oþer wise þench hwaseeaver hearmeþ þe oþer eni wa deþ þe scheome 
grome teone he is Godes yerde For swa he seiþ þurh Sein Juhanes muþ i þe 
Apocalipse Ne beat he nan bute hwamse he 
luveþ ant halt for his dohter namare þen þu waldest beaten a fremede child 
þah hit al gulte Ah nawt ne leote he wel of þet is Godes yerde for as þe feader 
hwen he haveþ inoh ibeaten his child ant haveþ hit ituht wel warpeþ þe 
yerde i þe fur for ha nis noht namare alswa þe Feder of heovene hwen he 
haveþ ibeaten wiþ an unwreast mon oþer an unwrest wummon his leove child 
for his god he warpeþ þe yerde þet is þe unwreste into þe fur of helle 
Forþi he seiþ elleshwer þet is min is 
þe wrake ich chulle yelden as þah he seide ne wreoke ye nawt owseolven 
ne grucchi ye ne wearien hwen me gulteþ wiþ ow ah þencheþ anan þet he is 
ower feadres yerde ant þet he wule yelden him yerde servise Ant nis þet child 
fulitohen þet scratleþ ayein ant bit upo þe yerde þet deboneire child hwen 
hit is ibeaten yef þe feader hat hit hit cusseþ þe yerde ant ye don alswa 
mine leove sustren For swa hat ower feader þet ye cussen nawt wiþ muþ ah 
wiþ luve of heorte þeo þe he ow wiþ beateþ þis is Godes heste þet him is muchel leovre þen þet tu eote gruttene bred 
oþer weredest hearde here luvieþ ower vamen he seiþ ant doþ god yef ye 
mahen to þeo þet ow weorriþ Yef ye elles ne mahen biddeþ yeorne for þeo 
þet ow eni eil doþ oþer misseggeþ Ant te Apostle leareþ ne yelde ye neaver 
uvel for uvel ah doþ god eaver ayein uvel as dude ure Laverd seolf ant alle his 
hali halhen Yef ye þus haldeþ Godes heaste þenne beo ye his hende child ant 
cusseþ þe yerde þe he haveþ ow wiþ iþorschen Nu seiþ oþerhwile sum 
 his sawle oþer hiren ich chulle wel luvien his bodi o nane wise Ah þet 
nis nawt to seggen þe sawle ant te licome nis bute a mon ant ba ham tit a dom 
Wult tu dealen o twa þe Godd haveþ to an isompnet He forbeot hit ant seiþ Ne wurþe nan se wod þet he todeale 
þe þing þe Godd haveþ iveiet 
þencheþ yet þisses weis þet child yef hit spurneþ o sum þing oþer hurteþ 
me beat þet hit hurte on ant þet child is wel ipaiet foryeteþ al his hurt ant 
stilleþ hise teares Forþi frovriþ owseolven Godd schal o Domesdei don as þah he seide Dohter hurte þes 
þe Dude he þe spurnen i wreaþþe oþer in heorte sar i scheome oþer in eani 
teone Loke dohter loke he seiþ hu he hit schal abuggen Ant þer ye schule 
seon bunkin him wiþ þes deofles betles þet wa biþ him þes lives Ye schulen 
beo wel ipaiet þe rof for ower wil ant Godes wil schal swa beon iveiet þet ye 
schulen wullen al þet he eaver wule ant he al þet ye wulleþ 
Over alle oþre þohtes in alle ower passiuns þencheþ eaver inwardliche up
Godes pinen þet te worldes wealdent walde for his þrealles þolien swucche 
schendlakes hokeres buffez spatlunge blindfeallunge þornene crununge þet 
set him i þe heaved swa þet te blodi strundes striken adun ant leaveden dun to 
þer eorþe his swete bodi ibunden naket to þe hearde piler ant ibeate swa þet 
tet deorewurþe blod ron on euche halve þet attri drunch þet me him yef þa 
him þurste o rode hare heafde sturunge upon him þa heo on hokerunge gredden 
se lude Lo her þe healde oþre Lo hu he healeþ nu ant helpeþ himseolven 
Turneþ þe ruppe þer ich spec hu he wes ipinet in alle his fif wittes ant eveneþ al 
ower wa secnesse ant oþerhwet woh of word oþer of werc ant al þet mon mei 
þolien to þet tet he þolede ant ye schulen lihtliche iseon hu lutel hit reacheþ 
nomeliche yef ye þencheþ þet he wes al ladles ant þet he droh al þis nawt for 
himseolven for he ne agulte neaver Yef ye þolieþ wa ye habbeþ wurse ofservet 
ant al þet ye þolieþ al is for owseolven 
Gaþ nu þenne gleadluker bi strong wei ant bi swincful toward te muchele 
feaste of heovene þeras ower gleade freond ower cume ikepeþ þenne dusie 
worldes men gaþ bi grene wei toward te wearitreo ant te deaþ of helle Betere is 
ga sec to heovene þen hal to helle to murhþe wiþ meoseise þen to wa wiþ eise Nawt forþi witerliche wrecche worltliche men buggeþ deorre 
helle þen ye doþ þe heovene A þing to soþe wite ye a misword þet ye 
þolieþ a deies longunge a secnesse of a stunde yef me chapede ed ow an of 
þeos o Domesdei þet is þe mede þe ariseþ þe rof ye hit nalden sullen 
for al þe world of golde For þet schal beon ower song bivoren ure Laverd 
þet is wel is us for þe dahes þet tu lahedest us wiþ oþer monne wohes ant 
wel is us nu Laverd for þe ilke yeres þet we weren seke in ant sehen sar ant 
sorhe Euch worltlich wa hit is Godes sonde Heh monnes messager me schal 
hehliche undervon ant makien him glead chere nomeliche yef he is prive wiþ 
his laverd Ant hwa wes mare prive wiþ þe king of heovene hwil he her wunede 
þen wes þes sondesmon þet is worldes weane þe ne com neaver from him 
aþet his lives ende þes messager hwet teleþ he ow He frovreþ ow o þis 
wise Godd as he luvede me he send me to his leove freond Mi cume ant mi 
wununge þah hit þunche attri hit is halwende Nere þet þing grislich hwas 
schadewe ye ne mahte nawt wiþuten hurt felen Hwet walde ye seggen bi þet 
eisfule wiht þet hit of come Wite ye to soþe þet al þe wa of þis world nis bute 
schadewe of þe wa of helle Ich am þe schadewe seiþ þes messager þet is 
worldes weane nedlunge ye moten oþer undervo me oþer þet grisliche wa 
þet ich am of schadewe Hwase underveþ me gleadliche ant makeþ me feier 
chere mi laverd send hire word þet ha is cwite of þet þing þet ich am of 
schadewe þus spekeþ Godes messager Forþi seiþ Sein Jame Alle blisse 
haldeþ hit to fallen i misliche of þeose fondunges þe uttre beoþ ihaten Ant 
Seint Pawel Alle þe ilke fondunges þe we beoþ nu i
beaten wiþ þuncheþ wop nawt wunne ah ha wendeþ efterward to weole ant 
to eche blisse 
þe inre fondunge is twavalt alswa as is þe uttre For þe uttre is adversite 
ant prosperte ant þeos cundleþ þe inre mislicunge in adversite ant i prosperite 
licunge þe limpeþ to sunne þis ich segge forþi þet sum licunge is ant sum 
mislicunge þe ofearneþ muche mede as licunge i Godes luve ant mislicunge for 
sunne Nu as ich segge þe inre fondunge is twavald fleschlich ant gastelich 
Fleschlich as of leccherie of glutunie of slawþe Gastelich as of prude of 
onde ant of wreaþþe alswa of yiscunge þus beoþ þe inre fondunges þe 
seoven heaved sunnen ant hare fule cundles Flesches fondunge mei beon ievenet 
to fotwunde Gastelich fondunge þet is mare dred of mei beon for þe peril i
cleopet breostwunde Ah us þuncheþ greattre flesliche temptatiuns forþi þet 
heo beoþ eþfele þe oþre þah we habben ham ofte nute we hit nawt ant 
beoþ þah greate ant grisliche i Godes ehe ant beoþ muchel forþi to drede þe 
mare For þe oþre þe me feleþ wel secheþ leche ant salve þe gasteliche hurtes 
ne þuncheþ nawt sare ne ne salviþ ham wiþ schrift ne wiþ penitence ant draheþ 
to eche deaþ ear me least wene 
Hali men ant wummen beoþ of alle fondunges swiþest ofte itemptet ant ham 
to goder heale For þurh þe feht toyeines ham ha biyeoteþ þe blisfule kempene 
crune Lo þah hu ha meaneþ ham i Jeremie 
þet is Ure wiþeriwines swiftre þen earnes upo þe hulles ha clumben efter 
us ant þer fuhten wiþ us ant yet i þe wildernesse ha spieden us to sleanne Ure 
wiþeriwines beoþ þreo þe feond þe worlt ure ahne flesch as ich ear seide 
Lihtliche ne mei me nawt oþerhwile icnawen hwuch of þeos þreo him weorreþ 
for euch helpeþ oþer þah þe feond proprement eggeþ to atternesse as to prude 
to overhohe to onde ant to wreaþþe ant to hare attri cundles þe herefter beoþ 
inempnet þe flesch sput proprement toward swetnesse eise ant softnesse þe 
world bit mon yiscin worldes weole ant wurþschipe ant oþre swucche give
gaven þe bidweolieþ cang men to luvien a schadewe þeos wiþeriwines hit 
seiþ folhiþ us on hulles ant weitiþ i wildernesse hu ha us mahen hearmin 
Hul þet is heh lif þer þe deofles asawz ofte beoþ strengest Wildernesse is 
anlich lif of ancre wununge For alswa as i wildernes beoþ alle wilde beastes ant 
nulleþ nawt þolien monne nahunge ah fleoþ hwen ha heom ihereþ alswa 
schulen ancres over alle oþre wummen beo wilde o þisse wise ant þenne beoþ 
ha over oþre leove to ure Laverd ant swetest him þuncheþ ham For of all flesches 
is wilde deores flesch leovest ant swetest 
Bi þis wildernesse wende ure Laverdes folc as Exode teleþ toward te eadi 
lond of Jerusalem þet he ham hefde bihaten Ant ye mine leove sustren wendeþ 
bi þe ilke wei toward te hehe Jerusalem þe kinedom þet he haveþ bihaten his i
corene Gaþ þah ful warliche for i þis wildernesse beoþ uvele beastes monie 
liun of prude neddre of attri onde unicorne of wreaþþe beore of dead slawþe 
vox of yisceunge suhe of yivernesse scorpiun wiþ þe teil of stinginde leccherie 
 þet is galnesse Her beoþ nu o rawe itald þe seoven heaved sunnen 
þe Liun of prude haveþ swiþe monie hwelpes ant ich chulle nempni summe þet is hwase let wel of ei þing þet ha deþ oþer seiþ oþer 
haveþ wlite oþer wit god acointance oþer word mare þen anoþer cun oþer 
meistrie ant hire wil forþre Ant hwet is wlite wurþ her Gold ring i suhe nease 
 acointance i religiun Wa deþ hit ofte Al is þe let eawiht wel 
of ant walde habben word þe rof ant is wel ipaiet yef ha is ipreiset mispaiet yef 
ha nis itald swuch as ha walde Anoþer is þet is þe þuncheþ 
hokerlich of ei þing þet ha siþ bi oþer oþer hereþ ant forhoheþ chastiement 
oþer ei lahres lare þe þridde hwelp is þe makeþ hire betere þen 
ha is þe feorþe is þe nimeþ mare on hond þen ha mei overcumen 
oþer entremeteþ hire of þing þet to hire ne falleþ oþer is to overtrusti upo 
Godes grace oþer on hireseolven to bald upon ei mon þet is fleschlich as heo 
is ant mei beon itemptet þe fifte hwelp hatte inobedience nawt ane þe ne 
buheþ ah þe oþer grucchinde deþ oþer targeþ to longe þet child þe ne 
buheþ ealdren underling his prelat paroschien his preost meiden hire dame 
euch lahre his herre þe seste is loquacite þe fedeþ þis hwelp þe is of muche 
speche yelpeþ demeþ oþre liheþ oþerhwile gabbeþ upbreideþ chideþ 
fikeleþ stureþ lahtre þe seoveþe is blasphemie þis hwelpes nurrice is þe 
swereþ greate aþes oþer bitterliche curseþ oþer misseiþ bi Godd oþer bi his 
halhen for ei þing þet he þoleþ siþ oþer hereþ þe eahtuþe is inpatience 
þis hwelp fet þe nis þolemod ayein alle wohes ant in alle uveles þe niheþe 
is contumace ant þis fet hwase is anewil i þing þet ha haveþ undernume to 
donne beo hit god beo hit uvel þet na wisure read ne mei bringen hire ut of 
hire riote þe teoheþe is þet is strif to overcumen þet te oþer 
þunche underneoþen awarpen ant cravant ant heo meistre of þe mot ant crenge 
ase champiun þe haveþ biyete þe place I þis unþeaw is upbrud ant edwitunge 
of al þet uvel þet ha mei bi þe oþer ofþenchen ant eaver se hit biteþ bittrure 
se hire likeþ betere þah hit were of þing þe wes bivore yare amendet Her
imong beoþ oþerhwiles nawt ane bittre wordes ah beoþ fule stinkinde 
scheomelese ant schentfule sumchearre mid great sware monie ant prude wordes 
wiþ warinesses ant bileasunges Herto falleþ evenunge of hamseolf of hare 
cun of sahe oþer of dede þis is among nunnen ant gaþ wiþ swuch muþ 
seoþþen ear schrift ham habbe iweschen to herie Godd wiþ loftsong oþer 
biddeþ him privee bonen Me þinges amansede nuten ha þet hare song ant hare 
bonen to Godd stinkeþ fulre to him ant to alle his halhen þen ei rotet dogge 
þe ealleofte hwelp is ifed wiþ supersticiuns wiþ semblanz ant wiþ sines as 
beoren on heh þet heaved crenge wiþ swire lokin o siden bihalden on hokere 
winche mid ehe binde seode mid te muþ wiþ hond oþer wiþ heaved makie 
scuter signe warpe schonke over schench sitten oþer gan stif as ha istaket were 
luve lokin o mon speoken as an innocent ant wlispin for þen anes Herto falleþ 
of veil of heaved claþ of euch oþer claþ to overgart acemunge oþer in 
heowunge oþer i pinchunge gurdles ant gurdunge o dameiseles wise scleaterunge 
mid smirles fule fluþrunges heowin her litien leor pinchen bruhen oþer bencin 
ham uppart wiþ wete fingres Monie oþre þer beoþ þe cumeþ of weole of 
wunne of heh cun of feier claþ of wit of wlite of strengþe Of heh lif waxeþ 
prude ant of hali þeawes Monie ma hwelpes þen ich habbe inempnet haveþ 
þe liun of prude Ah abute þeose studieþ wel swiþe for ich ga lihtliche over ne 
do bute nempni ham Ah ye eaver ihwer se ich ga swiþere vorþ leaveþ þer 
lengest for þer ich feþeri on a word tene oþer tweolve Hwaseeaver haveþ 
eani unþeaw of þeo þe ich her nempnede oþer ham iliche ha haveþ prude 
sikerliche huseeaver hire curtel beo ischapet oþer iheowet Heo is þe liunes 
make þet ich habbe ispeken of ant fet hire wode hwelpes inwiþ hire breoste 
þe Neddre of attri onde haveþ seove hwelpes þis cundel 
bret hwase nis icnawen goddede ah teleþ lutel þe rof oþer foryet mid alle 
Goddede ich segge nawt ane þet mon deþ him ah þet Godd deþ him oþer 
haveþ idon him oþer him oþer hire mare þen ha understont yef ha hire 
wel biþohte Of þis unþeaw me nimeþ to lutel yeme ant is þah of alle an 
laþest Godd ant meast ayein his grace þe oþer cundel is 
þet is heatunge oþer great heorte þe bret hit i breoste al is attri to Godd þet 
he eaver wurcheþ þe þridde cundel is ofþunchunge of oþres god þe feorþe 
gleadschipe of his uvel þe fifte wreiunge þe seste bacbitunge þe seoveþe 
upbrud oþer scarnunge þe eahtuþe is þet is misortrowunge bi 
mon oþer bi wummon wiþuten witer tacne þenchen þis semblant ha makeþ 
þis ha seiþ oþer deþ me forte gremien hokerin oþer hearmin ant þet 
hwen þe oþer neaver þiderward ne þencheþ Herto falleþ falsdom þet 
Godd forbeot swiþe as þenchen oþer seggen ye ne luveþ ha me nawt Herof 
ha wreide me Lo nu ha speokeþ of me þe twa þe þreo oþer þe ma þe 
sitteþ togederes Swuch ha is ant swuch ant for uvel ha hit dude I þulli þoht 
we beoþ ofte bichearret for ofte is god þet þuncheþ uvel ant forþi beoþ al 
dei monnes domes false Herto limpeþ alswa luþere neowe fundles ant leasunges 
ladliche þurh niþ ant þurh onde þe niheþe cundel is sawunge of unsibsumnesse 
of wreaþþe ant of descorde þeo þe saweþ þis deofles sed ha is of Godd 
amanset þe teoheþe is luþer stilþe þe deofles silence þet te an nule for onde 
speoken o þe oþer ant þis spece is alswa cundel of wreaþþe for hare teames 
beoþ imengt ofte togederes Hwer as ei of þeos wes þer wes þe cundel 
oþer þe alde moder of þe attri neddre of onde 
þe Unicorne of wreaþþe þe bereþ on his nease þe þorn þet he asneaseþ 
wiþ al þet he areacheþ haveþ six hwelpes þe earste is chast oþer strif þe 
oþer is wodschipe Bihald te ehnen ant te neb hwen wod wreaþþe is imunt 
Bihald hire contenemenz loke on hire lates hercne hu þe muþ geaþ ant tu maht 
demen hire wel ut of hire witte þe þridde is schentful upbrud þe feorþe is 
wariunge þe fifte is dunt þe seste is wil þet him uvel tidde oþer on him
seolf oþer on his freond oþer on his ahte þe seoveþe hwelp is don for 
wreaþþe mis oþer leaven wel to don forgan mete oþer drunch wreoken hire 
wiþ teares yef ha elles ne mei ant wiþ weariunges hire heaved spillen o grome 
oþer on oþer wise hearmin hire i sawle ant i bodi baþe þeos is homicide ant 
morþre of hireseolven 
þe Beore of hevi slawþe haveþ þeose hwelpes is þe forme þet is 
wlech heorte unlust to eni þing þe schulde leitin al o lei i luve of ure 
Laverd þe oþer is þet is to povre heorte ant to earh mid alle 
ei heh þing to underneomen in hope of Godes help ant i trust on his grace nawt 
of hire strengþe þe þridde is þis haveþ hwase wurcheþ 
god ant deþ hit tah mid a dead ant mid an hevi heorte þe feorþe is ydelnesse 
hwase stut mid alle þe fifte is heorte grucchunge þe seste is a dead sorhe for 
lure of ei worltlich þing oþer for eni unþonc bute for sunne ane þe seoveþe 
is yemelesschipe oþer to seggen oþer to don oþer to biseon bivoren oþer to 
þenchen efter oþer to miswiten eni þing þet ha haveþ to yemen þe eahtuþe 
is unhope þis leaste beore hwelp is grimmest of alle for hit tocheoweþ ant 
tofret Godes milde milce ant his muchele mearci ant his unimete grace 
þe Vox of yisceunge haveþ þeose hwelpes triccherie ant gile þeofþe 
reaflac wite ant herrure strengþe false witnesse oþer aþ dearne symonie gavel 
oker festschipe prinschipe of yeove oþer of lane þis is icluht heorte unþeaw 
Gode laþest þe yef us al himseolven monslaht oþerhwile þis unþeaw is 
to vox for moni reisun ievenet Twa ich chulle seggen Muche gile is i vox ant 
swa is i yisceunge of worltlich biyete Anoþer þe vox awurieþ al a floc þah he 
ne mahe buten an frechliche swolhen Alswa yisceþ a yiscere þet tet moni þusent 
mahten bi flutten ah þah his heorte berste ne mei he bruken on himseolf bute a 
monnes dale Al þet mon wilneþ mare oþer wummon þen ha mei rihtliche 
leade þet lif bi euch efter þet ha is al is yisceunge ant rote of deadlich 
sunne þet is riht religiun þet euch efter his stat borhi ed tis frakele world se 
lutel se ha least mei of mete of claþ of ahte of alle hire þinges Notiþ þet ich 
segge euch efter his stat for þet word is ifeþeret Ye mote makien þet 
wite ye i moni word muche strengþe þenchen longe þerabuten ant bi þet 
ilke an word understonden monie þe limpeþ þerto For yef ich schulde writen 
al hwenne come ich to ende 
þe Suhe of yivernesse haveþ gris þus inempnet to earliche hatte þet an 
þet oþer to esteliche þet þridde to frechliche þet feorþe hatte to muche 
þet fifte to ofte I drunch mare þen i mete beoþ þeos gris iferhet Ich speoke 
scheortliche of ham for nam ich nawt ofdred mine leove sustren leste ye ham 
feden 
þe Scorpiun of leccherie þet is of galnesse haveþ swucche cundles 
þet in a wel itohe muþ hare summes nome ne sit nawt forte nempnin for þe 
nome ane mahte hurten alle wel itohene earen ant sulen cleane heorten þeo 
þah me mei nempnin wel hwas nomen me icnaweþ wel ant beoþ mare 
hearm is to monie al to cuþe horedom eawbruche meiþlure ant incest 
þet is bituhe sibbe fleschliche oþer gasteliche þet is o feole idealet ful wil to 
þet fulþe wiþ skiles yettunge helpen oþre þiderward beo weote ant witnesse 
þ rof hunti þe refter wiþ wohunge wiþ toggunge oþer wiþ eni tollunge wiþ 
gigge lahtre hore ehe eanie lihte lates wiþ yeove wiþ tollinde word oþer wiþ 
luvespeche cos unhende grapunge þet mei beon heaved sunne luvie tide oþer 
stude forte cumen i swuch keast ant oþre foreridles þe me mot nede forbuhen 
þe i þe muchele fulþe nule fenniliche fallen As Seint Austin seiþ þet is hwase wule hire inwit witen hal ant fere ha mot fleon þe 
foreridles þe weren iwunet ofte to openin þe inyong ant leoten in sunne Ich 
ne dear nempnin þe uncundeliche cundles of þis deofles scorpiun attri iteilet 
Ah sari mei ha beon þe bute fere oþer wiþ haveþ swa ifed cundel of hire 
galnesse þet ich ne mei speoken of for scheome ne ne dear for drede leste sum 
leorni mare uvel þen ha con ant beo þe rof itemptet Ah þenche on hire ahne 
aweariede fundles in hire galnesse for hu se hit eaver is icwenct wakinde ant 
willes wiþ flesches licunge bute ane i wedlac hit geaþ to deadlich sunne I 
yuheþe me deþ wundres Culche hit i schrift ut utterliche as ha hit dude þe 
feleþ hire schuldi oþer ha is idemet þurh þet fule brune cwench to þet eche 
brune of helle þe scorpiunes cundel þe ha bret in hire bosum schake hit ut 
wiþ schrift ant slea wiþ deadbote Ye þe of swucches nute nawt ne þurve ye 
nawt wundrin ow ne þenchen hwet ich meane ah yeldeþ graces Godd þet ye 
swuch uncleannesse nabbeþ ifondet ant habbeþ reowþe of ham þe i swuch 
beoþ ifallen 
Inoh is etscene hwi ich habbe ievenet prude to liun onde to neddre ant of þeo 
alle þe oþre wiþute þis leaste þet is hwi galnesse beo to scorpiun ievenet 
Ah lo her þe skile þe rof sutel ant etscene scorpiun is a cunnes wurm þe haveþ 
neb as me seiþ sumdeal ilich wummon ant neddre is bihinden makeþ 
feier semblant ant fikeþ mid te heaved ant stingeþ mid te teile þis is leccherie 
þis is þe deofles beast þet he leat to chepinge ant to euch gederunge ant chepeþ 
forte sullen ant biswikeþ monie þurh þet ha ne bihaldeþ nawt bute þe feire 
neb oþer þet feire heaved þet heaved is þe biginnunge of galnesse sunne ant 
te licunge hwil hit least þe þuncheþ swiþe swote þe teil þet is þe ende 
þ rof is sar ofþunchunge ant stingeþ her wiþ atter of bitter bireowsunge ant of 
deadbote Ant seliliche mahen ha seggen þe þe teil swuch ifindeþ for þet 
atter ageaþ ah yef hit ne suheþ her þe teil ant te attri ende is þe eche pine of 
helle Ant nis he fol chapmon þe hwen he wule buggen hors oþer oxe yef he 
nule bihalden bute þet heaved ane Forþi hwen þe deovel beodeþ forþ þis 
beast beot hit to sullen ant bit ti sawle þervore he hut eaver þe teil ant 
schaweþ forþ þe heaved Ah þu ga al abuten ant schaw þe ende forþ mid al 
hu þe teil stingeþ ant swiþe flih þerfrommard ear þu beo iattret 
þus mine leove sustren i þe wildernesse þer ye gaþ in wiþ Godes folc 
toward Jerusalemes lond þet is þe riche of heovene beoþ þulliche beastes 
þulliche wurmes Ne nat ich na sunne þet ne mei beon ilead oþer to an of ham 
seovene oþer to hare streones Unsteaþelvest bileave ayein Godes lare nis hit 
te spece of prude inobedience Herto falleþ sygaldren false teolunges lefunge 
swefne o nore ant on alle wicchecreftes Neomunge of husel in eani heaved 
sunne oþer ei oþer sacrement nis hit te spece of prude þet ich cleopede yef me wat hwuch sunne hit is Yef me hit nat nawt þenne is hit 
yemeles under accidie þet ich slawþe cleopede þe ne warneþ oþer of his 
uvel oþer of his biyete nis hit slaw yemeles oþer attri onde Teoheþi mis 
edhalden cwide fundles oþer lane oþer þerwiþ misfearen nis hit spece of 
yisceunge ant anes cunnes þeofþe Edhalden oþres hure over his rihte terme 
nis hit strong reaflac hwase yelden hit mei þe is under yisceunge Yef me 
yemeþ wurse ei þing ileanet oþer bitaht to witene þen he wene þe ah hit 
nis hit oþer triccherie oþer yemeles of slawþe Alswa is dusi heast oþer folliche 
ipliht trowþe longe beon unbischpet falsliche gan to schrift oþer to longe 
abiden ne teache godchild ne þeos ant alle þulliche 
beoþ ilead to slawþe þet is þe feorþe moder of þe seove sunnen þe 
dronc drunch oþer ei þing dude hwerþurh na child ne schulde beon on hire i
streonet oþer þet istreonede schulde forwurþen nis þis strong monslaht of 
galnesse awakenet Alle sunnen sunderliche bi hare nomeliche nomen ne mahte 
namon rikenin ah i þeo þe ich habbe iseid alle oþre beoþ bilokene Ant nis 
ich wene namon þe ne mei understonden him of his sunne nomeliche under sum 
of þe ilke imeane þe beoþ her iwritene Of þeose seove beastes ant of hare 
streones i wildernesse of anlich lif is iseid herto þe alle þe forþfearinde 
fondiþ to fordonne þe liun of prude sleaþ alle þe prude alle þe beoþ hehe 
ant overhohe iheortet þe attri neddre þe ontfule ant te luþere iþonket 
wreaþfule þe unicorne alswa of þe oþre o rawe To Godd ha beoþ isleine ah 
ha libbeþ to þe feond ant beoþ alle in his hond ant serviþ him in his curt euch 
of þe meoster þe him to falleþ 
þe prude beoþ his bemeres draheþ wind inward wiþ worltlich hereword 
ant eft wiþ idel yelp puffeþ hit utward as þe bemeres doþ makieþ noise ant 
lud dream to schawin hare orhel Ah yef ha wel þohten of Godes bemeres of þe 
englene bemen þe schulen o fowr half þe world bivore þe grurefule dom grisliche 
blawen Ariseþ deade Ariseþ Cumeþ to Drihtines dom forte beon idemet 
þear na prud bemere ne schal beon iborhen yef ha þohten þis wel ha walden 
inohreaþe i þe deofles servise dimluker bemin Of þeose bemeres seiþ Jeremie Of þe 
wind drahinde in for luve of hereword seiþ Jeremie as ich seide 
Summe juglurs beoþ þe ne cunnen servin of nan oþer gleo bute makien cheres 
wrenche þe muþ mis schulen wiþ ehnen Of þis meoster serviþ þe unseli 
ontfule i þe deofles curt to bringen o lahtre hare ondfule laverd Yef ei seiþ wel 
oþer deþ wel ne mahen ha nanes weis lokin þider wiþ riht ehe of god heorte 
ah winkiþ o þet half ant bihaldeþ o luft yef þer is eawt to edwiten oþer ladliche 
þiderward schuleþ mid eiþer Hwen ha ihereþ þet god skleatteþ þe earen 
adun ah þe lust ayein þet uvel is eaver wid open þenne he wrencheþ þe 
muþ hwen he turneþ god to uvel ant yef hit is sumdel uvel þurh mare lastunge 
wrencheþ hit to wurse þeos beoþ forecwidderes hare ahne prophetes þeos 
bodieþ bivoren hu þe eateliche deoflen schulen yet ageasten ham wiþ hare 
grennunge ant hu ha schulen hamseolf grennin ant nivelin ant makien sur semblant 
for þe muchele angoise i þe pine of helle Ah forþi ha beoþ þe leasse to meanen 
þet ha bivorenhond leorniþ hare meoster to makien grim chere 
þe wreaþfule bivore þe feond skirmeþ mid cnives ant is his cnif warpere 
ant pleieþ mid sweordes bereþ ham bi þe scharp ord upon his tunge Sweord 
ant cnif eiþer beoþ scharpe ant keorvinde word þet he warpeþ from him ant 
skirmeþ toward oþre ant he bodeþ hu þe deoflen schulen pleien wiþ him mid 
hare scharpe eawles skirmi wiþ him abuten ant dusten ase pilcheclut euch to
ward oþer ant wiþ helle sweordes asneasen him þurhut þet beoþ kene ant 
eateliche ant keorvinde pinen 
þe slawe liþ ant slepeþ o þe deofles bearm as his deore deorling ant te 
deovel leiþ his tutel dun to his eare ant tuteleþ him al þet he wule For swa hit is 
sikerliche to hwamse is idel of god meaþeleþ þe feond yeorne ant te idele 
underveþ luveliche his lare Idel ant yemeles is þes deofles bearnes slep ah he 
schal o Domesdei grimliche abreiden wiþ þe dredfule dream of þe englene 
bemen ant in helle wontreaþe echeliche wakien 
þe yiscere is his eskibah feareþ abuten esken ant bisiliche stureþ him to 
rukelin togederes muchele ant monie ruken blaweþ þe rin ant blent himseolf 
peaþereþ ant makeþ þe rin figures of augrim as þes rikeneres doþ þe habbeþ 
muche to rikenin þis is al þe canges blisse ant te feond bihalt tis gomen ant 
laheþ þet he bersteþ Wel understont euch wis mon þet gold ba ant seolver 
ant euch eorþlich ahte nis bute eorþe ant esken þe ablendeþ euch mon þe ham 
in blaweþ þet is þe bolheþ him þurh ham in heorte prude Ant al þet he 
rukeleþ ant gedereþ togederes ant eþalt of ei þing þet nis bute esken mare þen 
hit neodeþ schal in helle wurþen him tadden ant neddren Ant ba as Ysaie 
seiþ schulen beon of wurmes his cuvertur ant his hwitel þe nalde þer
wiþ neodfule feden ne schruden 
þe yivere glutun is þe feondes manciple ah he stikeþ eaver i celer oþer i 
cuchene His heorte is i þe dissches his þoht al i þe neppes his lif i þe tunne 
his sawle i þe crohhe Kimeþ bivoren his laverd bismuddet ant bismulret a disch 
in his an hond a scale in his oþer Meaþeleþ mis wordes wigleþ as fordrunke 
mon þe haveþ imunt to fallen bihalt his greate wombe ant te deovel lahheþ 
þeose þreatiþ þus Godd þurh Ysaie Mine men schulen eoten ant ow schal eaver hungrin ant ye schule beon 
feondes fode world buten ende Yef þe kealchecuppe wallinde bres to drinken 
yeot in his wide þrote þet he swelte inwiþ Ayein an yef him twa þullich is 
Godes dom ayein yivere ant druncwile i þe Apocalipse 
þe lecchurs i þe deofles curt habbeþ riht hare ahne nome for i þes muchele 
curz þeo me cleopeþ lecchurs þe habbeþ swa forlore scheome þet heom nis 
nawiht of scheome ah secheþ hu ha mahen meast vilainie wurchen þe lecchur 
i þe deofles curt bifuleþ himseolven fulliche ant his feolahes alle stinkeþ of 
þet fulþe ant paieþ wel his laverd wiþ þet stinkinde breaþ betere þen he schulde 
wiþ eani swote rechles Hu he stinke to Godd i þe engel hit 
schawde þe heold his nease þa þer com þe prude lecchur ridinde ant nawt for 
þet rotede lich þet he healp þe hali earmite to biburien Of alle oþre þenne 
habbeþ þeos þe fuleste meoster i þe feondes curt þe swa bidoþ hamseolven 
Ant he schal bidon ham pinin ham wiþ eche stench i þe put of helle 
Nu ye habbeþ ane dale iherd mine leove sustren of þeo þe me cleopeþ þe 
seove modersunnen ant of hare teames ant of hwucche meosters þes ilke men 
serviþ i þe feondes curt þe habbeþ iwivet o þeose seoven haggen ant hwi ha 
beoþ swiþe to heatien ant to schunien Ye beoþ ful feor from ham ure Laverd 
beo iþoncket Ah þet fule breaþ of þis leaste unþeaw þet is of leccherie 
 stinkeþ se swiþe feor for þe feond hit saweþ ant toblaweþ over al þet ich 
am sumdel ofdred leste hit leape sumchearre into ower heortes nease Stench 
stiheþ uppart ant ye beoþ hehe iclumben þer þe wind is muchel of stronge 
temptatiuns Ure Laverd yeove ow strengþe wel to wiþstonden 
Sum weneþ þet ha schule stronglukest beon ifondet i þe forme tweofmoneþ 
þet ha bigon ancre lif ant i þe oþer þe refter Ant hwen ha efter feole yer feleþ 
ham stronge wundreþ hire swiþe ant is ofdred leste Godd habbe hire al 
forwarpen Nai nawt nis hit swa I þe forme yeres nis bute balplohe to monie 
men of ordre Ah neomeþ yeme hu hit feareþ bi a forbisne Hwen a wis mon 
neowliche haveþ wif ilead ham he nimeþ yeme al softeliche of hire maneres 
þah he seo bi hire þet him mispaieþ he let yet iwurþen makeþ hire feire 
chere ant is umben euches weis þet ha him luvie inwardliche in hire heorte 
Hwen he understont wel þet hire luve is treoweliche toward him ifestnet þenne 
mei he sikerliche chastien hire openliche of hire unþeawes þet he ear forber as 
he ham nawt nuste Makeþ him swiþe sturne ant went te grimme toþ to forte
