fondin yetten yef he mahte hire luve toward him unfestnin Alest hwen he 
understont þet ha is al wel ituht ne for þing þet he deþ hire ne luveþ him þe 
leasse ah mare ant mare yef ha mei from deie to deie þenne schaweþ he 
hire þet he hire luveþ sweteliche ant deþ al þet ha wule as þeo þet he wel i
cnaweþ þenne is al þet wa iwurþe to wunne Yef Jesu Crist ower spus deþ 
alswa bi ow mine leove sustren ne þunche ow neaver wunder I þe frumþe nis 
þer buten olhnunge forte drahen in luve Ah sone se he eaver understont þet he 
beo wel acointet he wule forbeoren ow leasse Efter þe spreove on ende þenne 
is þe muchele joie Al o þis ilke wise þa he walde his folc leaden ut of þeowdom 
ut of Pharaones hond ut of Egypte he dude for ham al þet ha walden miracles 
feole ant feire druhede þe Reade Sea ant makede ham freo wei þurh hire ant 
þer ha eoden drufot adrencte Pharaon ant hare fan alle I þe desert forþre þa 
he hefde ilead ham feor i þe wildernesse he lette ham þolien wa inoh hunger 
þurst ant muche swinc ant weorren muchele ant monie On ende he yef ham 
reste ant alle weole ant wunne al hare heorte wil ant flesches eise ant este þus ure Laverd speareþ on earst þe yunge ant 
te feble ant draheþ ham ut of þis world swoteliche ant wiþ liste Sone se he 
siþ ham heardin he let weorre awakenin ant teacheþ ham to fehten ant weane to 
þolien On ende efter long swinc he yeveþ ham swote reste her ich segge i 
þis world ear ha cumen to heovene Ant þuncheþ þenne swa god þe reste 
efter þe swinc þe muchele eise efter þe muchele meoseise þuncheþ se swote 
Nu beoþ i þe Sawter under þe twa temptatiuns þet ich ear seide þet beoþ 
þe uttre ant te inre þe temeþ alle þe oþre fowr dalen todealet þus fondunge 
liht ant dearne fondunge liht ant openlich fondunge strong ant dearne fondunge 
strong ant openlich as is þer understonden Of fondunge liht ant dearne seiþ Job þeose wordes Lutle dropen þurliþ 
þe flint þe ofte falleþ þe ron ant lihte dearne fondunges þe me nis war of 
falsiþ a treowe heorte Of þe lihte openliche bi hwam he seiþ alswa nis nawt se muche dute Of strong temptatiun þet is þah dearne 
is ec þet Job meaneþ þet is mine fan weitiþ me wiþ triccherie ant wiþ treisun ant ha 
strengden upo me ant nes hwa me hulpe Wa schal cumen on þe ant tu ne schalt witen hweonne Of 
þe feorþe fondunge þet is strong ant openlich he makeþ his man of his 
fan þe hali Job ant seiþ þet is ha þreasten in upo me as þah þe wal were tobroken ant te yeten 
opene þe forme ant te þridde fondunge of þeose fowre beoþ al meast under 
þe inre þe oþer ant te feorþe falleþ under þe uttre ant beoþ al meast 
fleschliche ant eþ forþi to felen þe oþre twa beoþ gasteliche of gasteliche 
unþeawes ant beoþ ihud ofte ant dearne hwen ha derveþ meast ant beoþ muche 
forþi þe mare to dreden Moni þet ne weneþ nawt bret in hire breoste sum 
liunes hwelp sum neddre cundel þe forfret þe sawle of hwucche Osee seiþ þet is Unholde forfreten þe 
strengþe of his sawle ant he hit nawt nuste Yet is meast dred of hwen þe sweoke 
of helle eggeþ to a þing þet þuncheþ swiþe god mid alle ant is þah sawle 
bone ant wei to deadlich sunne Swa he deþ as ofte as he ne mei wiþ open uvel 
cuþen his strengþe Na he seiþ ne mei ich nawt makien þeos to sungin 
þurh yivernesse ant ich chulle as þe wreastleare wrenchen hire þiderward as 
ha meast dreaieþ ant warpen hire o þet half ant breiden ferliche adun ear ha 
least wene ant eggeþ hire toward se muchel abstinence þet ha is þe unstrengre 
i Godes servise ant to leaden se heard lif ant pinin swa þet licome þet te sawle 
asteorve He bihalt anoþer þet he ne mei nanesweis makien luþere iþoncket 
se luveful ant se reowþful is hire heorte Ich chulle makien hire he seiþ to 
reowþful mid alle Ich schal don hire se muchel þet ha schal luvien ahte þenchen 
leasse of Godd ant leosen hire fame ant put þenne a þulli þonc in hire softe 
heorte Seinte Marie naveþ þe mon oþer þe wummon meoseise ant na mon 
nule don ham nawt Me walde me yef ich bede ant swa ich mahte helpen ham ant 
don on ham ealmesse bringeþ hire on to gederin ant yeoven al earst to povre 
forþre to oþer freond aleast makien feaste ant wurþen al worldlich forschuppet 
of ancre to husewif of halle Godd wat swuch feaste makeþ sum hore Weneþ 
þet ha wel do as dusie ant adotede doþ hire to understonden flatriþ hire of 
freolec herieþ ant heoveþ up þe ealmesse þet ha deþ hu wide ha is icnawen 
Ant heo let wel of ant leapeþ in orhel Sum seiþ inohreaþe þet ha gedereþ 
hord swa þet hire hus mei ant heo ba beon irobbet Reowþe over reowþe 
þus þe traitre of helle makeþ him treowe readesmon Ne leve ye him neaver 
Daviþ cleopeþ him briht schininde deovel ant Seinte 
Pawel þet is engel of liht For swuch ofte he makeþ him 
ant schaweþ him to monie Na sihþe þet ye seoþ ne i swefne ne waken ne telle 
ye bute dweole for nis hit bute his gile He haveþ wise men of hali ant of heh lif 
ofte swa bichearret as þe þet he com to i wummone liche i þe wildernesse 
seide ha wes igan o dweole ant weop as meoseise þing efter herbearhe Ant te 
oþer hali mon þet he makede ileven þet he wes engel bi his feader þet he wes 
þe deovel ant makede him to slean his feader swa ofte þerbivoren he heafde 
iseid him eaver soþ forte biswiken him sariliche on ende Alswa of þe hali 
mon þet he makede cumen ham forte dealen his feader feh to neodfule ant to 
povre se longe þet he deadliche sunegede o wummon ant swa feol into unhope 
ant deide in heaved sunne Of mon þe spekeþ wiþ ow þulliche talen hereþ hu 
ye schulen witen ow wiþ þes deofles wiltes þet he ow ne bichearre 
Sum of ow sumchearre he makede to leven þet hit were fikelunge yef ha speke 
feire ant yef ha eadmodliche meande hire neode yef ha þonckede mon of his 
goddede ant wes mare overhohe forte acwenchen chearite þen rihtwisnesse 
Sum he is umben to makien se swiþe fleon monne frovre þet ha falleþ i deadlich 
sar þet is accidie oþer into deop þoht swa þet ha dotie Sum heateþ swa 
sunne þet ha haveþ overhohe of oþre þe falleþ þe schulde wepen for hire 
ant sare dreden for a swuch onont hireseolven ant seggen as þe hali mon þe 
seac ant weop ant seide þa me him talde þe fal of an of his breþren Weilawei strongliche wes he itemptet ear he swa feolle As he feol 
todei ich mei quoþ he alswa fallen tomarhen 
Nu mine leove sustren monie temptatiuns ich habbe ow inempnet under þe 
seove sunnen nawt þah þe þusentfald þet me is wiþ itemptet Ne mahte 
 ich wene ham namon nomeliche nempnin Ah i þeo þe beoþ iseid alle 
beoþ bilokene Lut beoþ i þis world oþer nan mid alle þet ne beo wiþ hare 
sum oþerhwile itemptet He haveþ se monie buistes ful of his letuaires þe 
luþere leche of helle þe forsakeþ an he beot anoþer forþ ananriht þe 
þridde þe feorþe ant swa eaver forþ aþet he cume o swuch þet me on ende 
undervo Ant he þenne wiþ þet birleþ him ilome þencheþ her of þe tale of 
his ampoiles Hereþ nu as ich bihet ayein alle fondunges moni cunne frovre ant 
wiþ Godes grace þe refter þe salve 
Siker beo of fondunge hwase eaver stont in heh lif ant þis is þe earste 
frovre For eaver se herre tur se haveþ mare windes Ye beoþ tur owseolven 
mine leove sustren ah ne drede ye nawt hwil ye beoþ se treoweliche ant se feste 
ilimet wiþ lim of anred luve euch of ow to oþer For na deofles puf ne þurve 
ye dreden bute þet lim falsi þet is to seggen bute luve bitweonen ow þurh þe 
feond wursi Sone se ei unlimeþ hire ha biþ sone iswipt forþ bute yef þe 
oþre halden hire ha biþ sone ikeast adun as þe lowse stan is from þe tures cop 
into þe deope dich of sum suti sunne 
Nu anoþer elne muchel ah to frovrin ow hwen ye beoþ itemptet þe tur nis 
nawt asailit ne castel ne cite hwen ha beoþ iwunnen Alswa þe helle weorrur 
ne asaileþ nan wiþ fondunge þe he haveþ in his hond ah deþ þeo þe he naveþ 
nawt Forþi leove sustren hwase nis nawt asailet ha mei sare beon ofdred 
leste ha beo biwunnen 
þe þridde cunfort is þet ure Laverd seolf i þe teacheþ us to 
bidden þet is Laverd Feader ne suffre 
þu nawt þe feond þet he leade us allunge into fondunge Lo neomeþ yeme 
He nule nawt þet we bidden þet we ne beon nawt ifondet for þet is ure 
purgatoire ure cleansing fur ah þet we ne beon nawt allunge ibroht þe rin wiþ 
consens of heorte wiþ skiles yettunge 
þe feorþe frovre is sikernesse of Godes help i þe fehtunge ayein as Seinte 
Pawel witneþ Godd he seiþ is treowe Nule he neaver suffrin þet 
te deovel tempti us over þet he siþ wel þet we mahen þolien Ah i þe temptatiun 
he haveþ iset to þe feond a mearke as þah he seide Tempte hire swa feor ah 
ne schalt tu gan na forþre Ant swa feor he yeveþ hire strengþe to wiþstonden 
þe feond ne mei nawt forþre gan a pricke 
Ant þis is þe fifte frovre þet he ne mei na þing don us bute bi Godes leave 
þet wes wel ischawet as þe Godspel teleþ þa þe deoflen þet ure Laverd 
weorp ut of a mon bisohten ant seiden 
 Yef þu heonne drivest us do us i þeos swin her þe eoden þer an heorde Ant 
he yettede ham Lo hu ha ne mahten nawt fule swin swenchen wiþuten his 
leave Ant te swin ananriht urnen an urn to þe sea to adrenchen hamseolven 
Seinte Marie swa he stonc to þe swin þet ham wes leovre to adrenchen ham
seolven þen forte beoren him ant an unseli sunful Godes ilicnesse bereþ him 
in his breoste ant ne nimeþ neaver yeme Al þet he dude Job eaver he nom leve 
þ rof ed ure Laverd þe tale i Dyaloge lokiþ þet ye cunnen hu þe hali mon 
wes iwunet to seggen to þe deofles neddre Yef þu havest leave do sting yef þu maht ant bead forþ his 
cheke Ah he nefde þa nan bute to offearen him yef bileave him trukede Ant 
hwen Godd yeveþ him leave on his leove children hwi is hit bute for hare muchele 
biheve þah hit ham grevi sare 
þe seste confort is þet ure Laverd hwen he þoleþ þet we beon itemptet he 
pleieþ wiþ us as þe moder wiþ hire yunge deorling fliþ from him ant hut hire 
ant let him sitten ane ant lokin yeorne abuten cleopien Dame Dame ant wepen 
ane hwile ant þenne wiþ spredde earmes leapeþ lahhinde forþ cluppeþ ant 
cusseþ ant wipeþ his ehnen Swa ure Laverd let us ane iwurþen oþerhwile 
ant wiþdraheþ his grace his cunfort ant his elne þet we ne findeþ swetnesse i 
na þing þet we wel doþ ne savur of heorte ant þah i þet ilke point ne luveþ us 
ure Laverd neaver þe leasse ah deþ hit for muche luve Ant þet understod wel 
Daviþ þa he seide Allunge quoþ he 
 Laverd ne leaf þu me nawt Lo hu he walde þet he leafde him ah nawt allunge 
Ant six acheisuns notiþ hwi Godd for ure god wiþdraheþ him oþerhwiles An 
is þet we ne pruden anoþer þet we cnawen ure ahne feblesce ure muchele 
unstrengþe ant ure wacnesse Ant þis is a swiþe muche god as Seint Gregoire 
seiþ þet is muche godnesse 
hit is to cnawen wel his wrecchehead ant his wacnesse Hwet wat he seiþ Salomon þe þet is unfondet 
Ant Seint Austin bereþ Seint Gregoire witnesse wiþ þeose wordes Betere is þe þe truddeþ ant ofsecheþ wel ut his 
ahne feblesce þen þe þe meteþ hu heh is þe heovene ant hu deop þe eorþe 
Hwen twa beoreþ a burþerne ant te oþer leaveþ hit þenne mei þe þe up 
haldeþ hit felen hu hit weieþ Alswa leove suster hwil þet Godd wiþ þe bereþ 
þi temptatiun nast tu neaver hu hevi hit is ant forþi ed sumchearre he leaveþ 
þe ane þet tu understonde þin ahne feblesce ant his help cleopie ant yeie lude 
efter him yef he is to longe Hald hit wel þe hwile up ne derve hit te se sare 
Hwase is siker of sucurs þet him schal cume sone ant yelt tah up his castel to his 
wiþeriwines swiþe he is to edwiten þencheþ her of þe tale hu þe hali 
mon in his fondunge seh bi west toyeines him se muche ferd of deoflen ant forleas 
for muche dred þe strengþe of his bileave aþet te oþre seide him Bihald 
quoþ he bi esten we habbeþ ma 
þen heo beoþ to help on ure halve For þe þridde þing is þet tu neaver ne beo 
al siker for sikernesse streoneþ yemeles ant overhohe ant ba þeose streoniþ 
inobedience þe feorþe acheisun is hwi ure Laverd hut him þet tu seche him 
yeornluker ant cleopie ant wepe efter him as deþ þe lutel baban efter his moder 
þ refter is þe fifte þet tu his yeincume undervo þe gleadluker þe seste 
þet tu þe refter þe wisluker wite him hwen þu havest icaht him ant festluker 
halde ant segge wiþ his leofmon þeose six reisuns 
beoþ under þe seste frovre þe ye mahen habben mine leove sustren ayeines 
fondunge 
þe seoveþe confort is þet alle þe hali halhen weren wodeliche itemptet 
Nim of þe heste on alre earst to Seinte Peter seide ure Laverd Lo quoþ he Saþan is 
yeorne abuten forte ridli þe ut of mine icorene Ah ich habbe for þe bisoht þet 
ti bileave allunge ne trukie Seint Pawel hefde as he teleþ himseolf flesches 
pricunge ant bed ure Laverd yeorne þet 
he dude hit from him ant he nalde ah seide þet is mi grace schal wite þe þet tu ne beo overcumen 
Beo strong in unstrengþe þet is muche mihte Alle þe oþre beoþ icrunet 
þurh feht of fondunge Seinte Sare nes ha fulle þreottene yer itemptet of hire 
flesch Ah forþi þet ha wiste þet i þe muchele angoise aras þe muchele mede 
nalde ha neaver eanes bisechen ure Laverd þet he allunge delivrede hire þe rof 
ah þis wes hire bone Laverd yef me 
strengþe forte wiþstonden Efter þreottene yer com þe acursede gast þe hefde 
hire itemptet blac ase blamon ant bigon to greden Sare þu havest me 
overcumen Ant heo him ondswerede þu lihest quoþ ha ful þing Nawt 
ich ah haveþ Jesu Crist mi Laverd Lo þe sweoke hu he walde makien hire 
aleast to leapen into prude Ah ha wes wel war þe rof ant turnde al þe meistrie to 
Godes strengþe Sein Beneit Seint Antonie ant te oþre wel ye witen hu ha 
weren itemptet ant þurh þe temptatiuns ipruvede to treowe champiuns ant 
swa wiþ rihte ofserveden kempene crune 
Ant þis is þe eahtuþe elne þet alswa as þe goltsmiþ cleanseþ þet gold 
i þe fur alswa deþ Godd te sawle i fur of fondunge 
þe niheþe confort is þet yef þe feond wiþ fondunge greveþ þe sare þu 
grevest him hwen þu edstondest hundret siþe sarre for þreo reisuns nomeliche 
þe an is þet he forleoseþ as Origene seiþ his strengþe forte temptin eaver 
mare þeronuven of swuch manere sunne þe oþer is þet he forþluker echeþ 
his pine þe þridde fret his heorte of sar grome ant of teone þet he unþonc hise 
teþ i þe temptatiun þet tu stondest ayein muchleþ þi mede ant for pine þet 
he wende forte drahe þe toward breideþ þe crune of blisse ant nawt ane an 
ne twa ah ase feole siþen as þu overkimest him ase feole crunen þet is to 
seggen ase feole mensken of misliche murhþen For swa Sein Beornard seiþ þe tale i witneþ þis ilke 
of þe deciple þe set bivoren his meistre ant his meistre warþ o slepe hwil þet he 
learde him ant slepte aþet midniht þa he awakede Art tu quoþ he yet her 
Ga ant slep swiþe þe hali mon his meistre warþ eft o slep sone as þe þe 
hefde þerbivoren ibeon i muche wecche ant seh a swiþe feier stude ant iset 
forþ a trone ant þe ron seove crunen ant com a stevene ant seide þis sege ant 
þeose crunen haveþ þin deciple þis ilke niht ofsarvet Ant te hali mon abreaid 
ant cleopede him to him Sei quoþ he hu stod te hwil þu as ich slepte sete 
bivore me Ich þohte quoþ he ofte þet ich walde awakenin þe ant for þu 
sleptest swote ne mahte ich for reowþe Ant þenne þohte ich gan awei to 
slepen for me luste ant nalde bute leave Hu ofte quoþ his meister over
come þu þi þoht þus Seove siþen seide he þa understond his meister 
wel hwet weren þe seove crunen seove cunne blissen þet his deciple hefde in 
euch a chearre ofservet þet he wiþseide þe feond ant overcom himseolven 
Al þus leove sustren i wreastlunge of temptatiun ariseþ þe biyete Ne schal nan beon icrunet seiþ 
Seinte Pawel bute hwase strongliche ant treoweliche fehteþ ayein þe world 
ayein himseolf ayein þe feond of helle þeo fehteþ treoweliche þe hu se ha 
eaver beoþ iweorret wiþ þeos þreo wiþeriwines nomeliche of þe flesch 
 hwuch se eaver þe lust beo se hit meadluker is wrinniþ ayein festluker ant 
wiþseggeþ þe grant þe rof wiþ anewile heorte ne prokie hit se swiþe þeo 
þe þus doþ beoþ Jesu Cristes feolahes for ha doþ as he dude honginde o rode þet is he smahte þet bittre drunch 
ant wiþdroh him anan ant nalde hit nawt drinken þah he ofþurst were Heo is 
þe swa deþ wiþ Godd on his rode þah hire þurste i þe lust ant te deovel beot 
hire his healewi to drinken Understonde ant þenche þah þet ter is galle under 
Ant tah hit beo a pine betere is forte þolien þurst þen to beon iattret Let lust 
overgan ant hit te wule eft likin Hwil þe yicchunge least hit þuncheþ god to 
gnuddin ah þe refter me feleþ hit bitterliche smeorten Weilawei Ant moni an 
is for muchel heate se swiþe ofþurst mid alle þet hwil ha drinkeþ þet drunch 
ne beo hit ne se bitter ne feleþ ha hit neaver ah gluccheþ in yiverliche ne nimeþ 
neaver yeme Hwen hit is al over spit ant schakeþ þet heaved feþ on forte 
nivelin ant makien grim chere ah to leate þenne nautforþi For efter uvel 
god is penitence þet is þe best þenne  Speowen hit anan ut wiþ schrift to þe 
preoste For leave hit inwiþ hit wule deaþ breden Forþi mine leove sustren 
beoþ bivoren warre ant efter þe frovren þe beoþ her iwritene ayein alle 
fondunges secheþ þeose salven 
Ayein alle temptatiuns ant nomeliche ayein fleschliche salven beoþ ant 
bote under Godes grace halie meditatiuns inwarde ant meadlese ant angoisuse 
bonen hardi bileave redunge veasten wecchen ant licomliche swinkes oþres 
frovre forte speoke toward i þe ilke stunde þet hire stont stronge Eadmodnesse 
freolec of heorte ant alle gode þeawes beoþ armes i þis feht ant anrednesse of 
luve over alle þe oþre þe his wepnen warpeþ awei him luste beon iwundet 
Hali meditatiuns beoþ bicluppet in a vers þet wes yare itaht ow mine leove 
sustren 
þet is 
þench ofte wiþ sar of þine sunnen 
þench of helle wa of heoveriches wunnen 
þench of þin ahne deaþ of Godes deaþ o rode 
þe grimme dom of Domesdei munneþ ofte i mode 
þench hu fals is þe worlt hwucche beoþ hire meden 
þench hwet tua hest Godd for his god deden 
Euchan of þeose word walde a long hwile forte beo wel iopenet 
Ah yef ich hihi forþward demeori ye þe lengre A word ich segge efter 
ower sunnen hwense ye þencheþ of helle wa ant of heoveriches wunnen 
understondeþ þet Godd walde o sum wise schawin ham to men i þis world bi 
worltliche pinen ant worltliche wunnen ant schaweþ ham forþ as schadewe 
For na lickre ne beoþ ha to þe wunne of heovene ne to þe wa of helle þen is 
schadewe to þet þing þet hit is of schadewe Ye beoþ over þis worldes sea up
þe brugge of heovene lokiþ þet ye ne beon nawt þe hors eschif iliche þe 
schuncheþ for a schadewe ant falleþ adun i þe weater of þe hehe brugge To 
childene ha beoþ þe fleoþ a peinture þe þuncheþ ham grislich ant grureful to 
bihalden Wa ant wunne i þis world al nis bute peintunge al nis bute schadewe 
Nawt ane hali meditatiuns as of ure Laverd ant of alle his werkes ant of alle 
his wordes of þe deore Leafdi ant of alle hali halhen ah oþre þohtes sum
chearre i meadlese fondunges habbeþ iholpen fowr cunne nomeliche to þeo 
þe beoþ of flesches fondunges meadlese asailet dredfule wunderfule gleadfule 
ant sorhfule willes wiþute neod arearet i þe heorte As þenchen hwet tu waldest 
don yef þu sehe openliche stonde bivore þe ant yeoniende wide upo þe þen 
deovel of helle as he deþ dearnliche i þe fondunge Yef me yeide Fur Fur 
þet te chirche bearnde Yef þu herdest burgurs breoke þine wahes þeos ant 
oþre þulliche dredfule þohtes Wunderfule ant gleadfule as yef þu sehe Jesu 
Crist ant herdest him easki þe hwet te were leovest efter þi salvatiun ant þine 
leoveste freond of þing o þisse live ant beode þe cheosen wiþ þet tu wiþstode 
Yef þu sehe al witerliche heovene ware ant helle ware i þe temptatiun bihalde 
þe ane Yef me come ant talde þe þet mon þet te is leovest þurh sum miracle 
as þurh stevene of heovene were icoren to Pape ant alle oþre swucche 
Wunderfule ant sorhfule as yef þu herdest seggen þet mon þet te is leovest 
were ferliche adrenct islein oþer imurþret þet tine sustren weren in hare hus 
forbearnde þulliche þohtes ofte i fleschliche sawlen wrencheþ ut sonre 
fleschliche temptatiuns þen sum of þe oþre earre Inwarde ant meadlese ant 
ancrefule bonen biwinneþ sone sucurs ant help ed ure Laverd ayeines flesches 
fondunges ne beon ha neaver se ancrefule ne se fulitohene þe deovel of 
helle duteþ ham swiþe For teke þet ha draheþ adun sucurs ayein him ant 
Godes hond of heovene ha doþ him twa hearmes bindeþ him ant bearneþ 
Lo her preove of baþe Publius an hali mon wes in his bonen ant com þe feond 
fleonninde bi þe lufte ant schulde al on toward te west half of þe worlt þurh 
Julienes heast þe empereur ant warþ ibunden heteveste wiþ þe hali monne 
bonen þe oftoken him as ha fluhen uppard toward heovene þet he ne mahte 
hider ne þider ten dahes fulle Nabbe ye alswa of Ruffin þe deovel Beliales 
broþer in ower Englische boc of Seinte Margarete Of þet oþer me redeþ þet 
he gredde lude to Sein Barþolomew þe muchel wes i benen Barþolomew wa me þine beoden forbearneþ me Hwase 
mei þurh Godes yeove i beoden habbe teares ha mei don wiþ Godd al þet ha 
eaver wule for swa we redeþ 
 Eadi bone softeþ ant paieþ ure Laverd ah teares doþ him strengþe Beoden 
smirieþ him wiþ softe olhnunge ah teares prikieþ him ne ne yeoveþ him neaver 
pes ear þen he yetti ham al þet ha easkiþ Hwen me asaileþ burhes oþer castel 
þeo wiþinnen healdeþ scaldinde weater ut ant werieþ swa þe walles Ant ye 
don alswa as ofte as þe feond asaileþ ower castel ant te sawle burh wiþ in
warde bonen warpeþ ut upon him scaldinde teares þet Daviþ segge bi þe þu havest forscaldet te drake heaved 
wiþ wallinde weater þet is wiþ hate teares þear as þis weater is sikerliche 
þe feond fliþ leste he beo forscaldet Eft anoþer castel þe haveþ dich abuten 
ant weater beo i þe dich þe castel is wel carles ayeines his unwines Castel is 
euch god mon þet te deovel weorreþ Ah habbe ye deop dich of deop eadmodnesse 
ant wete teares þerto ye beoþ strong castel þe weorrur of helle mei longe 
asailin ow ant leosen his hwile Eft me seiþ ant soþ hit is þet a muche wind 
aliþ wiþ a lute rein ant te sunne þe refter schineþ þe schenre Alswa a muche 
temptatiun þet is þe feondes bleas afealleþ wiþ a softe rein of ane lut 
wordes teares ant te soþe sunne schineþ þe refter schenre to þe sawle þus 
beoþ teares gode wiþ inwarde bonen ant yef ye understondeþ ich habbe iseid 
of ham her fowr muchele efficaces forhwi ha beoþ to luvien In alle ower neoden 
sendeþ cwicliche anan þes sonde toward heovene For as Salomon seiþ þet is þe eadmodies bone þurleþ 
þe weolcne Ant ter seiþ Seint Austin O muchel is 
þe mihte of schir ant cleane bone þe fliþ up ant kimeþ in bivoren almihti Godd 
 ant deþ þe ernde se wel þet Godd haveþ o lives boc iwriten al þet ha seiþ 
as Sein Beornard witneþ edhalt hire wiþ himseolf ant sent adun his engel to 
don al þet ha easkeþ Nule ich her of bone segge na mare 
Hardi bileave bringeþ þe deovel o fluht ananrihtes þet witneþ Sein Jame Edstont ane þe feond ant he deþ him o 
fluhte Edstond þurh hwet strengþe Seinte Peter teacheþ Stondeþ ayein him wiþ stronge bileave beoþ hardi of Godes 
help ant witeþ hu he is wac þe na strengþe naveþ on us bute of usseolven Ne 
mei he bute schawin forþ sumhwet of his eapeware ant olhnin oþer þreatin 
þet me bugge þe rof Hweþer se he deþ scarniþ him lahheþ þe alde eape lude 
to bismere þurh treowe bileave ant he halt him ischent ant deþ him o fluht 
swiþe þet is þe hali halhen alle overcomen 
þurh bileave þe deofles rixlunge þet nis bute sunne for ne rixleþ he i nan 
bute þurh sunne ane Neomeþ nu gode yeme hu alle þe seovene deadliche sunnen 
muhen beon afleiet þurh treowe bileave On earst nu of prude 
Hwa halt him muchel as þe prude deþ hwen he bihalt hu lutel þe muchele 
Laverd makede him inwiþ a povre meidenes breoste Hwa is ontful þe bihalt 
wiþ ehnen of bileave hu Jesu Godd nawt for his god ah for oþres god 
dude ant seide ant þolede al þet he þolede þe ontfule ne kepte nawt þet eani 
dealde of his god Ant Godd almihti yet efter al þet oþer lihte dun to helle for
te sechen feolahes ant to deale wiþ ham þe god þet he hefde Lo nu hu frommard 
beoþ ontfule ure Laverd þe ancre þe wearnde anoþer a cwaer to lane 
feor ha hefde heoneward hire bileave ehe 
Hwa halt wreaþþe þe bihalt þet God lihte on eorþe to makien þreofald 
sahte bitweone mon ant mon bitweone Godd ant mon bitweone mon ant engel 
Ant efter his ariste þa he com ant schawde him þis wes his gretunge to his deore 
deciples Sahtnesse beo bitweonen ow Neomeþ nu yeorne yeme 
Hwen leof freond went from oþer þe leaste wordes þet he seiþ þeo schulen 
beo best edhalden Ure Laverdes leaste wordes þa he steah to heovene ant leafde 
his leove freond in uncuþe þeode weren of swote luve ant of sahtnesse þet is Sahtnesse ich do imong ow 
Sahtnesse ich leave wiþ ow þis wes his druerie þet he leafde ant yef ham in 
his departunge Lokiþ nu yeorne for his deorewurþe luve hwuch a 
mearke he leide upon his icorene þa he steah to heovene Bi þet ye schulen icnawen quoþ he þet ye beoþ mine 
deciples yef swete luve ant sahtnesse is eaver ow bitweonen Godd hit wite 
ant he hit wat me were leovere þet ye weren alle o þe spiteluvel þen ye 
weren ontfule oþer feol iheortet For Jesu is al luve ant i luve he resteþ him ant 
haveþ his wununge þet is i sahtnesse is Godes stude Ant hwerse 
sahte is ant luve þear he bringeþ to nawt al þes deofles strengþe þer he 
brekeþ his bohe hit seiþ þet beoþ dearne fondunges þet he scheot of feor 
 ant his sweord baþe þet beoþ temptatiuns keorvinde of neh ant kene 
Neomeþ nu yeorne yeme bi moni forbisne hu god is anrednesse of luve ant 
annesse of heorte For nis þing under sunne þet me is leovere ne se leof þet ye 
habben Nute ye þer men fehteþ i þes stronge ferdes þe ilke þe haldeþ ham 
feaste togederes ne muhe beo descumfit o neaver nane wise Alswa hit is in 
gastelich feht ayeines þe deovel al his entente is forte tweamen heorten forte 
bineomen luve þet halt men togederes For hwen luve aliþ þenne beoþ ha i
sundret ant te deovel deþ him bitweonen ananriht ant sleaþ on euche halve 
Dumbe beastes habbeþ þis ilke warschipe þet hwen ha beoþ asailet of wulf 
oþer of liun ha þrungeþ togederes al þe floc feste ant makieþ scheld of ham
seolf euch of heom to oþer ant beoþ þe hwile sikere Yef eani unseli went ut 
hit is sone awuriet þe þridde þer an geaþ him ane in a slubbri wei he slit ant 
falleþ sone þer monie gaþ togederes ant euch halt oþres hond yef eani feþ to 
sliden þe oþer hine breid up ear he ful falle yef ha wergiþ euchan halt him bi 
oþer Fondunge is sliddrunge þurh wergunge beoþ bitacnet þe unþeawes un
der slawþe þe beoþ inempnet þe ruppe þis is þet Sein Gregoire seiþ Alswa i strong wind ant swifte weattres þe me mot overwaden of monie 
euch halt oþer þe isundrede is iswipt forþ ant forfeareþ eaver To wel we 
witen hu þe wei of þis world is slubbri hu þe wind ant te stream of fondunge 
aren stronge Muche neod is þet euch halde wiþ bisie bonen ant wiþ luve oþres 
honden for as Salomon seiþ Wa eaver þe ane for hwen he falleþ naveþ he hwa him areare 
Nan nis ane þe haveþ Godd to fere ant þet is euch þet soþ luve haveþ in his 
heorte þe seoveþe forbisne is þis yef ye riht telleþ dust ant greot as ye 
seoþ for hit is isundret ant nan ne halt to oþer a lutel windes puf todriveþ hit 
al to nawt þear hit is in a clot ilimet togederes hit liþ al stille An hondful of 
yerden beoþ earveþ to breoken hwil ha beoþ togederes euchan itweamet 
lihtliche bersteþ A treo þe wule fallen undersete hit wiþ anoþer ant hit 
stont feste tweam ham ant ba falleþ Nu ye habbeþ nihene þus i þinges ute
wiþ neomeþ forbisne hu god is annesse of luve ant sometreadnesse þet halt 
þe gode somet þet nan ne mei forwurþen Ant þis wule iwiss habben þe rihte 
bileave Bihald yeorne ant understont Jesu Cristes deorewurþe wordes ant werkes 
þe i luve weren alle ant i swetnesse Over alle þing ich walde þet ancren leorneden 
wel þis lesceunes lare For monie mare hearm is beoþ Samsones foxes 
þe hefden þe neb euchan iwend frommard oþer ant weren bi þe teiles iteiet 
togederes as teleþ ant in euchanes teil a blease bearninde Of þeose 
foxes ich spec feor þe ruppe ah nawt o þisse wise Neomeþ gode yeme hwet þis 
beo to seggen me turneþ þe neb bliþeliche towart þing þet me luveþ ant 
frommard þing þet me heateþ þeo þenne habbeþ þe nebbes wrongwende 
euch frommard oþer hwen nan ne luveþ oþer ah bi þe teiles ha beoþ somet 
ant beoreþ þes deofles bleasen þe brune of galnesse On anoþer wise teil 
bitacneþ ende In hare ende ha schulen beon ibunden togederes as weren 
Samsones foxes bi þe teiles ant iset bleasen þe rin þet is þet fur of helle 
Al þis is iseid mine leove sustren þet ower leove nebbes beon eaver iwent 
somet wiþ luveful semblant ant wiþ swote chere þet ye beon aa wiþ annesse 
of an heorte ant of a wil ilimet togederes as hit iwriten is bi ure Laverdes deore 
deciples 
þis wes Godes gretunge to his deore deciples Griþ beo bimong ow Ye beoþ 
þe ancren of Englond swa feole togederes twenti nuþe oþer ma Godd i god ow 
multi þet meast griþ is among meast annesse ant anrednesse ant somet
readnesse of anred lif efter a riwle swa þet alle teoþ an alle iturnt anesweis 
ant nan frommard oþer efter þet word is Forþi ye gaþ wel forþ ant spedeþ 
in ower wei for euch is wiþward oþer in an manere of liflade as þah ye weren 
an cuvent of Lundene ant of Oxnefort of Schreobsburi oþer of Chester þear as 
alle beoþ an wiþ an imeane manere ant wiþuten singularite þet is anful 
frommardschipe lah þing i religiun for hit towarpeþ annesse ant manere i
meane þet ah to beon in ordre þis nu þenne þet ye beoþ alle as an cuvent 
 is ower hehe fame þis is Godd icweme þis is nunan wide cuþ swa þet 
ower cuvent biginneþ to spreaden toward Englondes ende Ye beoþ as þe moder
hus þet heo beoþ of istreonet Ye beoþ ase wealle yef þe wealle woreþ þe 
strunden woriþ alswa A wei la yef ye woriþ ne bide ich hit neaver Yef ei 
is imong ow þe geaþ i singularite ant ne folheþ nawt þe cuvent ah went ut of 
þe floc þet is as in a cloistre þet Jesu is heh priur over went ut as a teowi schep 
ant meapeþ hire ane into breres teilac into wulves muþ toward te þrote of helle 
 yef ei swuch is imong ow Godd turne hire into floc wende hire into cuvent 
ant leve ow þe beoþ þe rin swa halden ow þe rin þet Godd þe hehe priur neome 
ow on ende þeonne up into þe cloistre of heovene Hwil ye haldeþ ow in an 
offearen ow mei þe feond yef he haveþ leave ah hearmin nawt mid alle 
þet he wat ful wel ant is forþi umben deies ant nihtes to unlimin ow wiþ 
wreaþþe oþer wiþ luþer onde ant sent mon oþer wummon þe telle þe an bi 
þe oþer sum suhinde sahe þet suster ne schulde nawt segge bi suster Ower nan 
 ich forbeode ow ne leve þe deofles sondesmon ah lokiþ þet euch of ow i
cnawe wel hwen he spekeþ i þe uvele monnes tunge ant segge ananrihtes Ure 
meistre haveþ iwriten us as in heast to halden þet we tellen him al þet euch of 
oþer hereþ ant forþi loke þe þet tu na þing ne telle me þet ich ne muhe him 
tellen þe mei don þe amendement ant con swaliches don hit þet ich ant tu 
baþe yef we beoþ i þe soþ schule beon unblamet Euch noþeles warni 
oþer þurh ful siker sondesmon sweteliche ant luveliche as hire leove suster of 
þing þet ha misnimeþ yef ha hit wat to soþe Ant makie hwase bereþ þet 
word recordin hit ofte bivoren hire ear ha ga hu ha wule seggen þet ha ne 
segge hit oþerweis ne cluti þerto mare For a lute clut mei ladlechin swiþe a 
muchel hal pece þeo þe ed hire suster þis luvesalve underveþ þoncki hire 
yeorne ant segge wiþ þe Salmwruhte Ant þe refter 
wiþ Salomon Yef 
ha ne luvede me nalde ha nawt warni me i misericorde Leovere me beoþ hire 
wunden þen fikiende cosses þus ondswerie eaver Ant yef hit is oþerweis 
þen þe oþer understont sende hire word ayein þe rof luveliche ant softe ant te 
oþer leve ananriht for þet ich chulle alswa þet euch of ow luvie oþer as hire
seolven Yef þe feond bitweonen ow toblaweþ eani wreaþþe oþer great heorte 
 þet Jesu Crist forbeode ear ha beo iset wel nawt ane to neomen Godes 
flesch ant his blod ne wurþe nan se witles ah yet þet is leasse þet ha eanes ne 
bihalde þeron ne loki i ful wreaþþe toward him þe lihte to mon in eorþe of 
heovene to makien þreovald sahte as is iseid þe ruppe Sende eiþer þenne 
oþer word þet ha haveþ imaket hire as þah ha were bivoren hire 
eadmodliche Ant þeo þe ear ofdraheþ þus luve of hire suster ant ofgeaþ 
sahte ant nimeþ þe gult toward hire þah þe oþer hit habbe mare ha schal beo 
mi deorewurþe ant mi deore dohter for ha is Godes dohter He himseolf hit 
seiþ þus prude ant onde ant 
wreaþþe beoþ ihwer afleiet hwerse soþ luve is ant treowe bileave to Godes 
milde werkes ant luvefule wordes Ga we nu forþre to þe oþre on a reawe 
Hwa mei beo for scheome slummi sloggi ant slaw þe bihalt hu swiþe bisi 
ure Laverd wes on eorþe Efter al 
þet oþer bihaldeþ hu he i þe even of his lif swong o þe hearde rode Oþre 
habbeþ reste fleoþ liht i chambre hudeþ ham hwen ha beoþ ilete blod on an 
earm eþre Ant he o munt Calvaire steah yet o rode herre ne ne swong neaver 
mon se swiþe ne se sare as he dude þet ilke dei þet he bledde o fif half brokes of 
ful brade wunden ant deope wiþuten þe eþren capitale þe bledden on his heaved 
under þe kene þornene crune ant wiþuten þe ilke reowfule garces of þe luþere 
scurgunge yont al his leofliche lich nawt ane o þe schonken Toyeines slawe ant 
sleperes is swiþe openliche his earliche ariste from deaþe to live 
Ayeines yisceunge is his muchele poverte þe weox eaver upon him se lengre 
se mare For þa he wes iboren earst þe þet wrahte þe eorþe ne fond nawt on 
eorþe swa muche place as his lutle licome mahte beon ileid upon Swa nearow 
wes þet stude þet unneaþe his moder ant Josep seten þe rin Ant swa ha leiden 
him on heh up in a crecche wiþ clutes biwrabbet as þet Godspel seiþ þus feire he wes ischrud þe heovenliche Schuppent þe schrudeþ 
þe sunne Herefter þe povre meiden of heovene fostrede him ant fedde wiþ 
hire lutle milc as meiden deh to habben þis wes muche poverte ah mare com 
þ refter For lanhure þe yet he hefde fode as feol to him ant i stude of in his 
cradel herbearhede him Seoþþen as he meande him nefde he hwer he mahte 
his heaved huden þus 
povre he wes of in of mete he wes se neodful þet þa he hefde i Jerusalem o 
Palmsunnedei al dei ipreachet ant hit neolechede niht he lokede abuten hit 
seiþ i þe Godspel yef ei walde cleopien him to mete oþer to herbearhe ah nes 
þer nan Ant swa he wende ut of þe muchele burh into Beþanie to Marie hus ant 
to Marþen þeras he eode mid his deciples sumchearre Ha breken þe eares bi 
þe wei ant gnuddeden þe curnles ut bitweonen hare honden ant eten for hunger 
ant weren þervore swiþe icalenget Ah alre meast poverte com yet herefter 
for steortnaket he wes despuilet o þe rode þa he meande him of þurst weater 
ne mahte he habben Yet þet meast wunder is of al þe brade eorþe ne moste he 
habben a grot forte deien upon þe rode hefde a fot oþer lute mare ant þet wes 
to his pine Hwen þe worldes Wealdent walde beo þus povre unbilevet he is þe 
luveþ to muchel ant yisceþ worldes weole ant wunne 
Ayein glutunie is his povre pitance þet he hefde o rode Twa manere men habbeþ 
neode to eote wel swinkinde ant blodletene þe dei þet he wes baþe i sar 
swinc ant ilete blod as ich nest seide nes his pitance o rode bute a spunge of 
galle Loke nu hwa gruccheþ yef ha þencheþ wel heron mistrum mel of 
unsavuree metes of povre pitance Of na mon ne of na wummon ne schule ye 
makie na man ne pleainin ow of na wone bute to sum treowe freond þet hit mei 
amendin ant godin ham oþer ow Ant þet beo priveiliche iseid as under seel of 
schrift þet ye ne beon iblamet Yef ye of ei þing habbeþ wone ant sum freond 
yeorne freini ow yef ye ei wone habbeþ yef ye hopieþ god of him ondswerieþ 
þis wise Laverd Godd foryelde þe Ich drede mare ich habbe þen ich were 
wurþe ant leasse wone ich þolie þen me neod were Yef he easkeþ yeornluker 
þonkiþ him yeorne ant seggeþ Ich ne dear nawt lihen o meseolven wone ich 
habbe ase riht is Hwuch ancre kimeþ into ancrehus to habben hire eise Ah 
nu þu wult hit alles witen Ure Laverd te foryelde þis is nu an þing þet ich 
hefde neode to Ant þus bid ure riwle þet we schawin to gode freond as oþre 
Godes povre doþ hare meoseise wiþ milde eadmodnesse Ne nawt ne schule we 
forsaken þe grace of Godes sonde ah þonkin him yeorne leste he wreaþe him 
wiþ us ant wiþdrahe his large hond ant þe refter wiþ to muche wone abeate ure 
prude Ant nis hit muchel hofles hwen Godd beot his hond forþ puttinde hire 
ayein segge Ne kepe ich hit nawt have þeseolf Ich wulle fondin yef ich 
mei libben herbuten þurh þis ich habbe iherd of swuch þet nom uvel ende 
Ayein leccherie is his iborenesse of þet cleane meiden ant al his cleane lif þet 
he leadde on eorþe ant alle þe hine fuleden þus lo þe articles þet beoþ 
as þah me seide þe liþes of ure bileave onont Godes monhead hwase 
inwardliche bihalt ham fehteþ toyein þe feond þe fondeþ us wiþ þeose deadliche 
sunnen Forþi seiþ Seinte Peter Armiþ ow he seiþ wiþ þoht upo Jesu Crist þe in 
ure flesch wes ipinet Ant Seinte Pawel þencheþ þencheþ seiþ 
Seinte Pawel hwen ye wergiþ i feht ayeines þe deovel hu ure Laverd seolf 
wiþseide his fleschliche wil ant wiþseggeþ ower Yet nabbe ye nawt wiþstonden aþet te schedunge 
of ower blod as he dude of his for ow ayeines himseolven anont he 
mon wes of ure cunde Yet ye habbeþ þet ilke blod þet ilke blisfule bodi 
þet com of þe meiden ant deide o þe rode niht ant dei bi ow nis bute a 
wah bitweonen Ant euche dei he kimeþ forþ ant schaweþ him to ow 
fleschliche ant licomliche inwiþ þe measse biwrixlet þah on oþres 
lite under breades furme For in his ahne ure ehnen ne mahten nawt þe brihte 
sihþe þolien Ah swa he schaweþ him ow as þah he seide Lowr ich her 
Hwet wulle ye Seggeþ me hwet were ow leof Hwerto neodeþ ow Meaneþ 
ower neode Yef þe feondes ferd þet beoþ his temptatiuns asailiþ 
ow swiþe ondswerieþ him ant seggeþ Ye Laverd wunder is we beoþ 
iloget her bi þe þet art stan of help tur of treowe sucurs castel of strengþe ant 
te deofles ferd is woddre upon us þen upon eani oþre þis ich neome of 
for þer hit teleþ al þus þet Israel Godes folc com ant logede him bi þe stan of 
help ant te Philistews comen into Afech Philistews beoþ unwihtes Afech 
on Ebreisch spealeþ neowe wodschipe Swa hit is witerliche hwen mon logeþ 
him bi ure Laverd þenne on earst biginneþ þe deovel to weden Ah þer hit 
teleþ þet Israel wende sone þe rug ant weren fowr þusent i þe fluht sariliche i
sleine Ne wende ye nawt te rug mine leove sustren ah wiþstondeþ þe feondes 
ferd amidde þe forheaved as is iseid þe ruppe wiþ stronge bileave Ant 
wiþ þe gode Josaphaþ sendeþ beode sondesmon sone efter sucurs to þe prince 
of heovene þis is þet Englisch In us nis nawt deorewurþe Laverd swa 
muchel strengþe þet we mahen wiþstonden þe deofles ferd þe is se strong 
upon us Ah hwen we swa beoþ bisteaþet swa stronge bistonden þet we mid 
alle na read ne cunnen bi usseolven þis an we mahe don heoven ehnen up to þe 
mildfule Laverd þu send us sucurs þu todreaf ure fan for to þe we lokiþ 
þus wiþ þe gode Josaphaþ hwen Godd kimeþ bivoren ow ant freineþ hwet 
ye wulleþ ant in euch time hwen ye neode habbeþ schawiþ hit swa sweteliche 
to his swote earen Yef he sone ne hereþ ow yeieþ luddre ant meadlesluker ant 
þreatiþ þet ye wulleþ yelden up þe castel bute he sende ow sonre help ant hihi 
þe swiþere Ah wite ye hu he ondswerede Josaphaþ þe gode þus o þisse 
wise þus he onswereþ ow hwen ye help cleopieþ 
 Ne beo ye nawt offearede ne drede ye ham nawiht þah ha beon stronge ant 
monie þe feht is min nawt ower Sulement stondeþ sikerliche ant ye schulen 
seon mi sucurs habbeþ ane to me trusti bileave ant ye beoþ al sikere Lokiþ 
nu hwuch help is hardi bileave for al þet help þe Godd bihat þe strengþe to 
stonde wel al is in hire ane Hardi bileave makeþ stonden upriht ant te unwiht 
nis nawt laþre Forþi þis is his word in Ysaie Buh 
þe he seiþ duneward þet ich mahe over þe þeo buheþ hire þe to hise 
fondunges buheþ hire heorte for hwil ha stont upriht ne mei he nowþer upon 
hire rukin ne riden Lo þe treitre hu he seiþ Buh 
þe let me leapen up nule ich þe nawt longe riden ah ich chulle wenden 
over He liheþ seiþ Sein Beornard ne lef þu nawt þen traitre Nule he nawt wenden over ah wule ful feaste sitten Sum 
wes þet lefde him þohte he schulde sone adun as he bihat eaver Do he seiþ 
 þis enchearre ant schrif þe þe rof tomarhen Buh þin heorte let me up 
Schec me wiþ schrift adun yef ich alles walde ride þe longe Sum as ich seide 
lefde him ant beah him ant he leop up ant rad hire baþe dei ant niht twenti yer 
fulle þet is ha dude a sunne i þe ilke niht þurh his procunge ant þohte þet 
ha walde hire schriven ine marhen ant dude hit eft ant eft ant fealh swa i uvel 
wune þet ha lei ant rotede þe rin swa longe as ich seide Ant yef a miracle nere 
þe pufte adun þen deovel þe set on hire se feaste ha hefde iturplet wiþ him 
baþe hors ant lade dun into helle grunde Forþi mine leove sustren haldeþ ow 
efne upriht i treowe bileave Hardiliche ileveþ þet al þe deofles strengþe 
mealteþ þurh þe grace of þet hali sacrement hest over oþre þet ye seoþ as 
ofte as þe preost measseþ þe meidene bearn Jesu Godd Godes sune þe 
licomliche lihteþ oþerhwiles to ower in ant inwiþ ow eadmodliche nimeþ his 
herbearhe Deuleset ha beoþ to wake ant to unwreaste iheortet þe wiþ swilli 
gest hardiliche ne fehteþ Ye schulen bileave habben þet al Hali Chirche deþ 
red oþer singeþ ant alle hire sacremenz strengeþ ow gasteliche ah nan ase 
forþ ase þis for hit bringeþ to noht al þes deofles wiheles nawt ane his 
strengþes ant his stronge turnes ah deþ his wiltfule crokes his wrenchfule 
wicchecreftes ant alle his yulunges ase lease swefnes false schawunges dredfule 
offearunges fikele ant sweokele reades as þah hit were o Godes half ant god for
te donne For þet is his unwrench as ich ear seide þet hali men meast dredeþ 
þet haveþ moni hali mon grimliche biyulet Hwen he ne mei nawt bringen to nan 
open uvel he sput to a þing þet þuncheþ god þu schuldest he seiþ beo 
mildre ant leoten iwurþe þi chast nawt trubli þin heorte ant sturien into 
wreaþþe þis he seiþ forþi þet tu ne schuldest nawt chastien for hire gult ne 
tuhte wel þi meiden ant bringe þe into yemeles i stude of eadmodnesse Eft riht 
þertoyeines Ne let tu hire na gult toyeves he seiþ Yef þu wult þet ha 
drede þe hald hire nearowe Rihtwisnesse he seiþ mot beo nede sturne 
ant þus he liteþ cruelte wiþ heow of rihtwisnesse Me mei beon al to rihtwis Betere is wis liste þen luþer strengþe 
Hwen þu havest longe iwaket ant schuldest gan to slepen nu is vertu he 
seiþ wakien hwen hit greveþ þe Sei yet a nocturne Forhwi deþ he swa 
For þet tu schuldest slepen eft hwen time were to wakien Eft riht þertoyeines 
yef þet tu maht wakien wel he leiþ on þe an hevinesse oþer deþ i þi þoht 
 Wisdom is þinge best Ich chulle ga nu to slepen ant arise nunan ant don 
cwicluker þene nu þet ich don nuþe schulde ant swa ofte inohreaþe ne 
dest tu hit i nowþer time Of þis ilke materie ich spec muchel þe ruppe I þulliche 
temptatiuns nis nan se wis ne se war bute Godd him warni þet nis bigilet 
ofte Ah þis hehe sacrement in hardi bileave over alle oþre þing unwriþ hise 
wrenches ant brekeþ hise strengþes Iwis leove sustren hwen ye neh ow feleþ 
him forhwon þet ye habben hardi bileave nulle ye bute lahhen him lude to 
bismere þet he is se muchel ald cang þe kimeþ his pine to echen ant breiden 
ow crune Sone se he siþ ow hardi ant bald i Godes grace his mihte mealteþ ant 
he fliþ sone Ah yef he mei underyeoten þet ower bileave falsi swa þet ow 
þunche þet ye mahten beon allunge ilead forþ over yef ye weren swiþe i þe 
ilke stude itemptet þerwiþ ye unstrengeþ ant his mihte waxeþ 
We redeþ i þet Ysboset lei ant slepte ant sette a wummon yeteward 
þe windwede hweate ant comen Recabes sunen Remon ant Banaa ant funden 
þe wummon istunt of hire windwunge ant ifolen o slepe ant wenden in ant 
slohen Ysboset þe unseli þet lokede him se uvele þe bitacnunge herof is 
muche neod to understonden Ysboset on Ebrew is mon bimeaset on Englisch 
 ant nis he witerliche ameaset ant ut of his witte þe amidden his unwines leiþ 
him to slepen þe yeteward is wittes skile þet ah to windwin hweate schaden 
þe eilen ant te chef from þe cleane cornes þet is þurh bisi warschipe sundri 
god from uvel don þe hweate i gerner ant puffen eaver awei þe deofles chef 
þet nis noht bute to helle smorþre Ah þe bimeasede Ysboset lo hu measeliche 
he dude Sette a wummon to yeteward þet is feble warde Weila as feole 
doþ þus Wummon is þe reisun þet is wittes skile hwen hit unstrengeþ 
þe schulde beo monlich stealewurþe ant kene in treowe bileave þis yete
ward liþ to slepen sone se me biginneþ consenti to sunne leoten lust gan in
ward ant te delit waxen Hwen Recabes sunen þet beoþ helle bearnes i
findeþ swa unwaker ant swa nesche yeteward ha gaþ in ant sleaþ Ysboset 
þet is þe bimeasede gast þe in a slepi yemeles foryemeþ himseolven þet nis 
nawt to foryeoten þet as Hali Writ seiþ ha þurhstichden him dun into þe 
schere Her seiþ Sein Gregoire þe feond þurhsticheþ þe schere hwen delit of 
leccherie þurleþ þe heorte ant þis nis bute i slep of yemeles ant of slawþe 
as Sein Gregoire witneþ þis is þet Englisch Hwen 
þe alde unwine siþ slepi ure skile he draheþ him anan toward hire ant feleþ 
wiþ hire i speche þenchest tu he seiþ hu þe spec oþer þeo of 
flesches galnesse Ant spekeþ þus þe alde sweoke toward hire heorte wordes 
þet ha yare herde fulliche iseide oþer sihþe þet ha seh oþer hire ahne fulþen 
þet ha sumhwile wrahte Al þis he put forþ bivore þe heorte ehnen forte 
bifulen hire wiþ þoht of alde sunnen hwen he ne mei wiþ neowe ant swa he 
bringeþ ofte ayein into þe adotede sawle þurh licunge þe ilke sunnen þe þurh 
reowþful sar weren ibet yare swa þet heo mei wepen ant meanen sari man wiþ 
þe Salmwruhte Weilawei mine wunden þe weren 
feire ihealet gederiþ neowe wursum ant foþ on eft to rotien Ihealet wunde 
þenne biginneþ to rotien hwen sunne þe wes ibet kimeþ eft wiþ licunge into 
munegunge ant sleaþ þe unwarre sawle Al þis unlimp iwarþ þurh þe yetewardes slep þet 
nes war ant waker ne nes nawt monlich ah wes wummonlich eþ to overkeasten 
Beo hit wummon beo hit mon þenne is al þe strengþe efter þe bileave ant 
efter þet me haveþ trust to Godes help þet is neh bute bileave trukie as ich 
ear buven seide Heo unstrengeþ þe unwiht ant deþ him fleon ananriht Forþi 
beoþ eaver ayein him hardi ase liun i treowe bileave nomeliche i þe fondunge 
þet Ysboset deide on þet is galnesse Lo hu ye mahe cnawen þet he is earh 
ant unwreast hwen he smit þiderward Nis he earh champiun þe skirmeþ to
ward te vet þe secheþ se lahe on his kempeifere Flesches lust is fotes wunde 
 as wes feor iseid þe ruppe ant þis is þe reisun As ure fet beoreþ us alswa 
ure lustes beoreþ us ofte to þing þet us luste efter Nu þenne þah þi va hurte 
þe o þe vet þet is to seggen fondeþ wiþ flesches lustes for se lah wunde 
ne dred tu nawt to sare bute hit to swiþe swelle þurh skiles yettunge wiþ to 
muchel delit up toward te heorte ah drinc þenne atterlaþe ant drif þet swealm 
ayeinward frommard te heorte þet is to seggen þench o þe attri pine þet 
Godd dronc o þe rode ant te swealm schal setten Prude ant onde ant wreaþþe 
heorte sar for worltlich þing dreori oflongunge ant yisceunge of ahte þeose 
beoþ heorte wunden ant al þet of ham floweþ ant yeoveþ deaþes dunt anan 
buten ha beon isalvet Hwen þe feond smit þiderward þenne is iwis to dreden 
 ant nawt for fotwunden 
Prude salve is eadmodnesse ondes feolahlich luve wreaþþes þolemodnesse 
accidies redunge misliche werkes gastelich frovre yisceunges overhohe of 
eorþliche þinges festschipes freo heorte þet is to seggen nu of þe earste on 
alre earst yef þu wult beon eadmod þench eaver hwet te wonteþ of halinesse 
ant of gasteliche þeawes þench hwet tu havest of þeseolf þu art of twa 
dalen of licome ant of sawle In eiþer beoþ twa þinges þe mahen muchel meokin 
þe yef þu ham wel bihaldest I þe licome is fulþe ant unstrengþe Ne kimeþ of 
þet vetles swuch þing as þer is in Of þi flesches fetles kimeþ þer smeal of 
aromaz oþer of swote basme Deale Drue spritlen beoreþ winberien Breres 
rose blostmen þi flesch hwet frut bereþ hit in all his openunges Amid te 
menske of þi neb þet is þe fehereste deal bitweonen muþes smech ant 
neases smeal ne berest tu as twa prive þurles Nart tu icumen of ful slim Nart 
tu fulþe fette Ne bist tu wurme fode Nu a flehe mei eili þe makie þe to blenchen 
eaþe maht tu pruden Bihald hali men þe weren sumhwile hu ha feasten hu ha 
wakeden i hwuch passiun i hwuch swinc ha weren ant swa þu maht icnawen 
þin ahne wake unstrengþe Ah wast tu hwet awildgeþ monnes feble ehnen þet 
is hehe iclumben þet he bihalt duneward Alswa hwase bihalt to þeo þe 
beoþ of lah lif þet makeþ him þunchen þet he is of heh lif Ah bihald aa uppart 
toward heovenliche men þe clumben se hehe ant þenne schalt tu seon hu lahe 
þu stondest Feasten a seoveniht to weater 
ant to breade þreo niht togederes wakien hu walde hit unstrengen þi fleschliche 
strenge þus þeos twa þinges bihald i þi licome fulþe ant unstrengþe i þi 
sawle oþer twa sunne ant ignorance þet is unwisdom ant unweotenesse For 
ofte þet tu wenest god is uvel ant sawle morþre Bihald wiþ wet ehe þine scheome 
sunnen Dred yet þi wake cunde þet is eþwarpe ant sei wiþ þe hali mon þe 
bigon to wepen ant seide þa me talde him þet an of his feren wes wiþ a wummon 
i flesches fulþe ifallen þet is he todei ant ich to
marhen as þah he seide Of as unstrong cunde ich am as he wes ant al swuch 
mei me ilimpen bute yef Godd me halde þus lo þe hali mon nefde he of 
þe oþres fal na wunderlich overhohe ant biweop his unhap ant dredde þet him a 
swuch mahte bitiden O þis wise eadmodieþ ant meokiþ owseolven 
 þet is Alswa as prude is wilnunge of wurþschipe riht alswa þertoyeines 
eadmodnesse is forkeastunge of wurþschipe ant luve of lutel hereword ant of 
lahnesse þis þeaw is alre þeawene moder ant streoneþ ham alle þe is umben 
wiþuten hire to gederin gode þeawes he bereþ dust i þe wind as Sein Gregoire 
seiþ þeos ane biþ iborhen þeos ane wiþbuheþ þe deofles grunen of helle 
as ure Laverd schawde to Seint Antonie þe seh al þe world ful of þe deofles 
tildunge A Laverd quoþ he hwa mei wiþ þeose witen him þet he ne beo 
wiþ sum ilaht Ane þe þolemode quoþ he ure Laverd Swa sutil þing is 
eadmodnesse ant swa gentilliche smeal ant se smuhel þet na grune ne mei hire 
edhalden ant lo muche wunder þah ha hire makie swa smeal ant se meoke 
ha is þinge strengest swa þet of hire is euch gastelich strengþe Seint Cassiodre 
hit witneþ Ah Salomon seiþ þe reisun hwi þeras eadmodnesse is þer he seiþ is Jesu 
Crist þet is his feader wisdom ant his feader strengþe Nis na wunder þenne 
þah strengþe beo þeras he is þurh his inwuniende grace þurh þe strengþe 
of eadmodnesse he weorp þe þurs of helle þe yape wreastlere nimeþ yeme 
hwet turn his fere ne kunne nawt þet he wiþ wreastleþ for wiþ þet turn he mei 
him unmundlunge warpen Alswa dude ure Laverd ant seh hu feole þe grimme 
wreastlere of helle breid upon his hupe ant weorp wiþ þe hancheturn into galnesse 
 þe rixleþ i þe lenden hef on heh monie ant wende abuten wiþ ham ant 
swong ham þurh prude dun into helle grunde þohte ure Laverd þe biheold al 
þis Ich schal do þe a turn þet tu ne cuþest neaver ne ne maht neaver cunnen 
þe turn of eadmodnesse þet is þe fallinde turn ant feol from heovene to 
eorþe ant strahte him swa bi þe eorþe þet te feond wende þet he were al 
eorþlich ant wes bilurd wiþ þet turn ant is yet euche dei of eadmode men ant 
wummen þe hine wel cunnen On oþer half as Job seiþ he ne mei for prude 
yet bute bihalden hehe Hali men þe haldeþ 
ham lutle ant of lah lif beoþ ut of his sihþe þe wilde bar ne mei nawt buhen 
him to smiten hwase falleþ adun ant þurh meoke eadmodnesse strecheþ him bi 
þer eorþe he is carles of his tuskes þis nis nawt toyeines þet þet ich habbe i
seid ear þet me schal stonden eaver toyeines þe deovel for þet stondinge 
is treowe trust of hardi bileave upo Godes strengþe þis fallunge is eadmod 
cnawunge of þin ahne wacnesse ant of þin unstrengþe Ne nan ne mei stonde 
swa bute he þus falle þet is leote lutel tale ant unwurþ ant eþelich eaver of 
himseolven bihalde his blac ant nawt his hwit for hwit awilgeþ þe ehe 
Eadmodnesse ne mei beon neaver ful preiset for þet wes þe lesceun þet ure 
Laverd inwardlukest learde his icorene wiþ werc ba ant wiþ worde In hire he healdeþ nawt ane dropemel ah 
flowinde yeotteþ weallen of his graces as seiþ þe Salmiste I þe dealen þu makest he seiþ weallen to springen 
Heorte tobollen ant ihoven ase hul ne edhalt na wete of grace A bleddre ibollen 
of wind ne deveþ nawt into þeose halwende weattres Ah a nelde prichunge 
warpeþ al þe wind ut an eþelich stiche oþer eche makeþ to understonden hu 
lutel prude is wurþ hu egede is orhel 
Ondes salve ich seide wes feolahlich luve ant god unnunge ant god wil þer 
mihte of dede wonteþ Swa muchel strengþe haveþ luve ant god wil þet hit 
makeþ oþres god ure god ase wel as his þet hit wurcheþ Sulement luve his 
god beo wilcweme ant glead þe rof þus þu turnest hit to þe ant makest hit 
þin ahne Sein Gregoire hit witneþ Yef þu 
havest onde of oþres god þu attrest te wiþ healewi ant wundest te wiþ salve 
þi salve hit is yef þu hit luvest ayein sawle hurtes Ant ti strengþe ayein 
þe feond is al þe god þet oþer deþ yef þu hit wel unnest Witerliche ich leve 
ne schulen flesches fondunges namare þen gasteliche meistrin þe neavere yef 
þu art swote iheortet eadmod ant milde ant luvest se inwardliche alle men ant 
wummen ant nomeliche ancres þine leove sustren þet tu art sari of hare uvel 
ant of hare god glead as of þin ahne Unnen þet al þe luveþ þe luvede ham ase 
þe ant dude ham frovre as þe Yef þu havest cnif oþer claþ oþer mete oþer 
drunch scrowe oþer cwaer hali monne frovre oþer ei oþer þing þet ham walde 
freamien unnen þet tu hefdest wonte þeseolf þe rof wiþ þon þet heo hit hefden 
Yef eani is þe naveþ nawt þe heorte þus afeitet wiþ sorhfule sikes ba bi dei 
ant bi niht grede on ure Laverd ne neaver griþ ne yeove him aþet he þurh his 
grace habbe hire swuch aturnet 
Salve of wreaþþe ich seide is þolemodnesse þet haveþ þreo steiren heh 
ant herre ant alre hest ant nest te hehe heovene Heh is þe steire yef þu þolest for 
þi gult herre yef þu navest gult alre hest yef þu þolest for þi goddede Nai 
seiþ sum ameaset þing yef ich hefde gult þerto nalde ich neaver meanen 
Art tu þet swa seist ut of þeseolven Is þe leovere to beon Judase feolahe þen 
Jesu Cristes fere Ba weren ahonget ah Judas for his gult Jesu wiþute gult for 
his muchele godlec wes ahon o rode Hweþeres fere wult tu beon Wiþ hweþer 
wult tu þolien Of þis is þe ruppe iwriten muchel hu he is þi file þe misseiþ 
oþer misdeþ þe Lime is þe Frensch of file Nis hit or acurset þe iwurþeþ 
swartre ant ruhre se hit is ifilet mare ant rusteþ þe swiþere þet me hit scureþ 
hearde Gold seolver stel irn al is or Gold ant seolver cleansiþ ham of hare 
dros i þe fur yef þu gederest dros þe rin þet is ayein cunde þe chaliz þe wes 
þerin imealt ant strongliche iweallet ant seoþþen þurh se moni dunt ant 
frotunge to Godes nep se swiþe feire afeitet walde he yef he cuþe speoken 
awearien his cleansing fur ant his wruhte honden 
Al þis world is Godes smiþ to smeoþien his icorene Wult tu þet Godd nabbe 
na fur in his smiþþe ne bealies ne homeres Fur is scheome ant pine þine 
bealies beoþ þe þe misseggeþ þine homeres þe þe hearmiþ þench of þis 
essample Hwen dei of riht is iset ne deþ he scheome þe deme þe a þis half 
þe isette dei brekeþ þe triws ant wrekeþ him o þe oþer on himseolven 
Ant hwa nat þet Domesdei nis þe dei iset to don riht alle men Hald þe triws 
þe hwiles hwet woh se me deþ þe þe richtwise deme haveþ iset te dei to loki 
richt bitwenen ow  Ne do þu nawt him scheome forhohie wrake of his dom ant 
neomen to þin ahne Twa þinges beoþ þet Godd haveþ edhalden to himseolven 
þet beoþ wurþschipe ant wrake as Hali Writ witneþ Hwase eaver on himseolf 
takeþ owþer of þeos twa he robbeþ Godd ant reaveþ Deale Art tu se wraþ 
wiþ mon oþer wiþ wummon þet tu wult forte wreoke þe reavin Godd mid 
strengþe 
Accidies salve is gastelich gleadschipe ant frovre of gleadful hope þurh redunge 
þurh hali þoht oþer of monnes muþe Ofte leove sustren ye schulen uri leasse 
forte reden mare Redunge is god bone Redunge teacheþ hu ant hwet me bidde 
ant beode biyet hit efter Amidde þe redunge hwen þe heorte likeþ kimeþ up a 
devotiun þet is wurþ monie benen Forþi seiþ Sein Jerome Hali redunge beo eaver i þine honden 
Slep ga upo þe as þu lokest þe ron ant te hali pagne ikepe þi fallinde neb 
swa þu schalt reden yeornliche ant longe Euch þing þah me mei overdon best 
is eaver mete 
Ayeines yisceunge ich walde þet oþre schuneden as ye doþ gederunge To 
muche freolec cundleþ hire ofte Freo iheortet ye schule beon Ancre of oþer 
freolec haveþ ibeon oþerhwiles to freo of hireseolven 
Galnesse kimeþ of yivernesse ant of flesches eise for as Sein Gregoire seiþ 
 Mete ant drunch over riht temeþ þreo teames lihte wordes lihte werkes ant 
leccheries lustes Ure Laverd beo iþonket þe haveþ of yivernesse ihealet ow 
mid alle Ah galnesse ne biþ neaver allunge cleane acwenct of flesches fondunge 
Ah þet understondeþ wel þet þreo degrez beoþ þe rin as Seint Beornard witneþ 
þe forme is cogitatiun þe oþer is affectiun þe þridde is cunsence Cogitatiuns 
beoþ fleonninde þohtes þe ne leasteþ nawt ant teo as Sein Beornard seiþ ne 
hurteþ nawt te sawle Ah þah ha bispottiþ hire wiþ hare blake speckes swa þet 
nis ha nawt wurþe þet Jesu hire leofmon þet is al feier bicluppe hire ne cusse 
hire ear ha beo iwesschen Swuch fulþe as hit kimeþ lihtliche lihtliche geaþ 
awei wiþ wiþ wiþ alle goddeden Affectiun is hwen þe 
þoht geaþ inward ant delit kimeþ up ant te lust waxeþ þenne as wes spot 
ear upo þe hwite hude þer waxeþ wunde ant deopeþ in toward te sawle efter 
þet te lust geaþ ant te delit þe rin forþre Ant forþre þenne is neod to yeiyen A Laverd heal me for ich am iwundet Ruben þu reade þoht þu blodi delit ne waxe 
þu neaver Cunsense þet is skiles yettunge hwen þe delit i þe lust is igan se 
overforþ þet ter nere nan wiþseggunge yef þer were eise to fulle þe dede þis 
is hwen þe heorte draheþ to hire unlust as þing þe were amainet ant feþ on as 
to winkin to leote þe feond iwurþen ant leiþ hireseolf duneward buheþ him 
as he bit ant yeieþ Cravant Cravant ase softe swohninde þenne is he kene 
þe wes ear curre þenne leapeþ he to þe stod ear feorren to ant bit deaþes bite 
Godes deore spuse iwiss deaþes bite for his teþ beoþ attrie as of a wed 
dogge Daviþ i þe Sawter cleopeþ hine dogge 
Forþi mi leove suster sone se þu eaver underyetest þet tes dogge of helle 
cume snakerinde wiþ his blodi flehen of stinkinde þohtes ne li þu nawt stille 
ne ne site nowþer to lokin hwet he wule don ne hu feor he wule gan ne sei þu 
nawt slepinde Ame dogge Ga her ut Hwet wult tu nu her inne þis tolleþ 
him inward Ah nim anan þe rodesteaf mid nempnunge i þi muþ mid te mearke 
i þin hond mid þoht i þin heorte ant hat him ut heterliche þe fule curdogge 
ant liþere to him luþerliche mid te hali rodesteaf stronge bacduntes þet is 
rung up sture þe hald up ehnen on heh ant honden toward heovene Gred efter 
sucurs Yef 
þe ne kimeþ sone help gred luddre wiþ hat heorte ant swa al 
þe Salm over wiþ halsinde bonen o þin ahne 
ledene Smit smeortliche adun þe cneon to þer eorþe ant breid up þe rode
steaf ant sweng him o fowr half ayein helle dogge þet nis nawt elles bute 
blesce þe al abuten wiþ þe eadi rodetaken Spite him amid te beard to hoker ant 
to scarne þe flikereþ swa wiþ þe ant fikeþ dogge fahenunge Hwen he for se 
liht wurþ for þe licunge of a lust ane hwile stucche chapeþ þi sawle 
Godes deore bune þet he bohte mid his blod ant mid his deorewurþe deaþ o 
þe deore rode aa bihald hire wurþ þet he paide for hire ant dem þe refter hire 
pris ant beo on hire þe deorre Ne sule þu neaver se eþeliche his fa ant þin 
eiþer his deorewurþe spuse þet costnede him se deore Makie deofles hore of 
hire is reowþe over reowþe To unwreast mid alle ha is þe mei wiþ toheoven 
up hire þreo fingres overcumen hire fa ant ne luste for slawþe Hef forþi wiþ 
treowe ant hardi bileave up þine þreo fingres ant wiþ þe hali rodesteaf þet 
him is laþest cuggel lei o þe doggedeovel nempne ofte Jesu cleope his passiunes 
help halse bi his pine bi his deorewurþe blod bi his deaþ o rode flih to his 
wunden Muchel he luvede us þe lette makien swucche þurles in him forte huden 
us in Creop in ham wiþ þi þoht ne beoþ ha al opene Ant wiþ his deore
wurþe blod biblodge þin heorte 
 Ga into þe stan seiþ þe prophete ant hud te i þe dolven eorþe þet is 
i þe wunden of ure Laverdes flesch þe wes as idolven wiþ þe dulle neiles as 
he i þe Sawter longe vore seide þet 
is ha dulven me baþe þe vet ant te honden Ne seide he nawt þurleden for 
efter þis leattre as ure meistres seggeþ swa weren þe neiles dulle þet ha 
dulven his flesch ant tobreken þe ban mare þen þurleden to pinin him sarre He 
himseolf cleopeþ þe toward teose wunden Mi culvre he seiþ cum hud te i mine limen þurles i 
þe hole of mi side Muche luve he cudde to his leove culvre þet he swuch 
hudles makede Loke nu þet tu þe he cleopeþ culvre habbe culvre cunde 
þet is wiþute galle ant cum to him baldeliche ant make scheld of his passiun 
ant sei wiþ Jeremie þet is þu schalt 
yeove me Laverd heorte scheld ayein þe feond þi swincfule pine þet hit 
swincful wes he schawde hit witerliche inoh þa he sweatte ase blodes swat 
dropen þe runnen to þer eorþe Me schal halden scheld i feht up abuven heaved 
oþer ayein þe breoste nawt ne drahen hit bihinden Al riht swa yef þu wult þet 
te rodescheld ant Godes stronge passiun falsi þe deofles wepnen ne dragse þu 
hit nawt efter þe ah hef hit on heh buve þin heorte heaved i þine breoste ehnen 
Hald hit up toyein þe feond schaw hit him witerliche þe sihþe þe rof ane 
bringeþ him o fluhte for ba him scheomeþ þerwiþ ant griseþ ut of witte efter 
þe ilke time þet ure Laverd þerwiþ brohte swa to grunde his cointe coverschipe 
ant his prude strengþe Yef þu þurh þi yemeles werest te earst wacliche ant 
yevest to þe feond inyong to forþ i þe frumþe swa þet tu ne mahe nawt reculin 
him ayeinward for þi muchele unstrengþe ah art ibroht se overforþ þet tu ne 
maht þis scheld halden o þin heorte ne wrenchen hire þerunder frommard te 
deofles earowen nim þe aleast forþ Sein Beneites salve þah ne þearf hit nawt 
beon se overstrong as his wes þe of þe walewunge rug ant side ant wombe 
ron al o gureblode Ah lanhure yef þeseolf hwen þe strongest stont a smeort 
discepline ant drif as he dude þet swete licunge into smeortunge Yef þu þus ne 
dest nawt ah slepinde werest te he wule gan to feor on þe ear þu least wene 
ant bringe þe of ful þoht into delit of ful lust ant swa he bringeþ þe al over to 
skiles yettunge þet is deadlich sunne wiþuten þe dede ant swa is ec þe delit of 
þet stinkinde lust wiþute grant of þe werc se longe hit mei leasten þenne hit least to longe hwen þe skile ne fehteþ na lengre þer
toyeines Forþi leove suster as ure Laverd leareþ totred te neddre heaved 
þet is þe biginnung of his fondunge Eadi is seiþ Daviþ þe wiþhalt hire on earst ant tobrekeþ 
to þe stan þe earste sturunges hwen þe flesch ariseþ hwil þet ha beoþ yunge 
Ure Laverd is icleopet stan for his treownesse Nim ant keche us leofmon anan þe 
yunge foxes he seiþ ure Laverd þe strueþ þe winyardes þet beoþ 
þe earste procunges þe strueþ ure sawlen þe mot muche tilunge to to beoren 
winberien þe deovel is beore cunnes ant haveþ asse cunde for he is bihinden 
strong ant i þe heaved feble swa is beore ant asse þet is i þe frumþe Ne 
yef þu him neaver inyong ah tep him o þe sculle for he is earh as beore þe ron 
ant hihe him swa þeoneward ant askur him se scheomeliche sone se þu 
underyetest him þet him grise wiþ þe stude þet tu wunest inne For he is þinge 
prudest ant him is scheome laþest 
Alswa leove suster sone se þu eaver felest þet tin heorte wiþ luve falle to 
eani þing eawt over mete ananrihtes beo war of þe neddre atter ant totred his 
heaved þe cwene seide ful soþ þe wiþ a strea ontende alle hire wanes þet 
muchel kimeþ of lutel Ant nim nu yeme hu hit feareþ þe sperke þe wint up ne 
bringeþ nawt ananriht þe hus al o leie ah liþ ant kecheþ mare fur ant fostreþ 
forþ ant waxeþ from leasse to mare aþet al þe hus bleasie forþ ear me least 
wene Ant te deovel blaweþ to from þet hit earst cundleþ ant mutleþ his beali
bleas eaver as hit waxeþ Understond tis bi þeseolf a sihþe þet tu sist oþer 
anlepi word þet tu misherest yef hit eawt stureþ þe cwench hit wiþ teares 
weater ant mid Jesu Cristes blod hwil hit nis bute a sperke ear þen hit waxe ant 
ontende þe swa þet tu hit ne mahe cwenchen For swa hit timeþ ofte ant hit is 
riht Godes dom þet hwa ne deþ hwen ha mei ne schal ha hwen ha walde 
Moni cunnes fondunge is i þis feorþe dale misliche frovren ant monifalde 
salven Ure Laverd yeove ow grace þet ha ow moten helpen Of alle þe oþre 
þenne is schrift þe biheveste Of hit schal beon þe fifte dale as ich bihet þe ruppe 
Ant neomeþ yeme hu euchan dale falleþ into oþer as ich þear seide

Twa þinges neomeþ yeme of schrift i þe biginnunge þe earre of hwuch 
mihte hit beo þe oþer hwuch hit schule beon þis beoþ nu as twa limen 
ant eiþer is todealet þe earre o sixe þe oþer o sixtene stucchen Nu is þis 
of þe earre 
Schrift haveþ monie mihtes ah nulle ich of alle seggen bute sixe þreo ayein þe 
deovel ant þreo on usseolven Schrift schent þen deovel hackeþ of his heaved ant 
todreaveþ his ferd Schrift wescheþ us of alle ure fulþen yelt us alle ure luren 
makeþ us Godes children Eiþer haveþ hise þreo Pruvie we nu alle þe earste 
þreo beoþ alle ischawde i Judiþe deden Judiþ þet is schrift as wes yare iseid 
 sloh Oloferne þet is þe feond of helle Turn þe ruppe þer we speken of 
fuhelene cunde þe beoþ ievenet to ancre Ha hackede of his heaved ant seoþþen 
com ant schawde hit to þe burhpreostes þenne is þe feond ischend hwen me 
schaweþ alle hise cweadschipes his heaved is ihacket of ant he islein i þe mon 
sone se he eaver is riht sari for his sunnen ant haveþ schrift on heorte Ah he nis nawt 
þe yet ischend hwil his heaved is ihulet as dude on earst Judiþ ear hit beo i
schawet þet is ear þe muþ i schrift do ut þe heaved sunne nawt te sunne ane 
ah al þe biginnunge þe rof ant te foreridles þe brohten in þe sunne þet is þe 
deofles heaved þet me schal totreoden anan as ich ear seide þenne flith his ferd 
anan as dude Olofernes his wiheles ant his wrenches þet he us wiþ asaileþ doþ ham 
alle o fluhte ant te burh is arud þet ha hefden biset þet is to seggen þe sunfule is 
delifret Judas Macabeu hwa stod ayein him Alswa i þet folc þa hit 
easkede efter Josues deaþ hwa schulde beon hare dug ant leaden ham i ferde Ure Laverd ham ondswerede Judas schal gan bivoren ow ant ich 
chulle ower faes lond biteachen in his honden Lokiþ nu ful yeorne hwet tis beo to 
seggen Josue spealeþ heale ant Judas schrift as Judiþ þenne is Josue dead 
hwen sawle heale is forloren þurh eani deadlich sunne þe sunfule seolf is þe unwihtes 
lond þe is ure deadliche fa ah þis lond ure Laverd bihat to biteachen i Judase honden 
forhwon þet he ga bivoren Schrift lo is gunfanuner ant bereþ þe banere bivoren al 
Godes ferd þet beoþ gode þeawes Schrift reaveþ þe feond his lond þet is 
þe sunfule mon ant al todriveþ Chanaan þe feondes ferd of helle Judas hit dude 
licomliche ant schrift þet hit bitacneþ deþ gasteliche þet ilke þis beoþ nuþe þreo

þet beoþ þeose herefter 
Schrift wescheþ us of alle ure fulþen for swa hit is iwriten Ant þet wes bitacnet 
þa Judiþ wesch hire ant despulede hire of widewene schrud þet wes merke of sorhe 
 ant sorhe nis bute of sunne Schrift eft al þet god þet we hefden forloren þurh heavedsunne bringeþ 
al ayein ant yelt al togederes þis wes bitacnet þurh þet Judiþ schrudde hire mid hali
dahne weden ant feahede hire utewiþ as schrift deþ us inwiþ wiþ alle þe feire 
urnemenz þe blisse bitacniþ Ant ure Laverd seiþ þurh Zacharie þet is schrift schal makie þe mon alswuch as he wes 
bivore þet he sunegede ase cleane ant ase feier ant ase riche of alle god þe limpeþ 
to sawle þe þridde þing is þet schrift deþ usseolven þe frut of þes oþre twa ant 
endeþ ham baþe þet is makeþ us Godes children þis is bitacnet þerbi þet 
Judas i Genesy biwon of Jacob Benjamin Benjamin seiþ ase muchel ase sune of riht 
half Judas þet is schrift alswa as is Judiþ for ba ha spealieþ an on Ebreische 
ledene þes gasteliche Judas biyet of Jacob his feader þet is ure Laverd to 
beon his rihthondes sune ant bruken buten ende þe eritage of heovene Nu we habbeþ 
iseid of hwuch mihte schrift is hwucch efficaces hit haveþ ant inempnet sixe Loki 
we nu yeornliche hwuch schrift schule beon þe beo of swuch strengþe Ant forte 
schawin hit bet deale we nu þis lim o sixtene stucchen 
Schrift schal beo wreiful bitter mid sorhe ihal naket ofte imaket hihful eadmod 
scheomeful dredful hopeful wis soþ ant willes ahne ant studevest biþoht 
bivore longe Her beoþ nu as þah hit weren sixtene stuchen þe beoþ ifeiet to schrift 
ant we schulen of euchan sum word sunderliche seggen 
Schrift schal beo wreiful Mon schal wreien him i schrift nawt werien him ne 
seggen Ich hit dude þurh oþre Ich wes ined þerto þe feond hit makede me 
don þus Eve ant Adam wereden ham Adam þurh Eve ant Eve þurh þe neddre 
þe feond ne mei neden namon to na sunne þah he eggi þerto ah ful wel he let of 
hwen ei seiþ þet he makede him to sunegin as þah he hefde strengþe þe naveþ nan 
mid alle bute of usseolven Ah me ah to seggen Min ahne unwrestlec hit dude ant 
willes ant waldes ich beah to þe deovel Yef þu witest ei þing þi sunne bute þe
seolven þu ne schrivest te nawt yef þu seist þet tin unstrengþe ne mahte nawt elles 
þu wrenchest þi sunne upo Godd þe makede þe swuch þet tu bi þin tale wiþstonde 
ne mahtest Wreie we þenne usseolven for lo hwet Seinte Pawel seiþ þet is yef we wreieþ wel her ant 
demeþ her usseolven we schule beo cwite of wreiunge ed te muchele dome þear 
as Seint Anselme seiþ þeos dredfule wordes O þe an half o Domesdei schulen ure swarte sunnen 
strongliche bicleopien us of ure sawle morþre O þe oþer half stont rihtwisnesse 
þet na reowþe nis wiþ dredful ant grislich ant grureful to bihalden buven us þe 
eorre deme for ase softe as he is her ase heard he biþ þer ase milde as he is nu 
ase sturne þenne lomb her liun þer as þe prophete witneþ þe liun schal greden he seiþ Hwa ne mei beon offearet Her we 
cleopieþ him lomb as ofte as we singeþ Nu 
as ich seide schule we seon buven us þe ilke eorre deme þet is ec witnesse ant wat 
alle ure gultes bineoþen us yeoniende þe wide þrote of helle inwiþ usseolven ure 
ahne conscience þet is ure inwit forculiende hireseolven wiþ þe fur of 
sunne wiþuten us al þe world leitinde o swart lei up into þe skiwes þe sari sunfule 
þus biset hu schal him stonde þenne To hwuch of þes fowre mei he him biwenden

Jeremie witneþ þet 
is al þet him luvede yeieþ spi him on ant heatieþ him alle Yet mare his children 
sone se he sunegede deadliche deiden alle clane þet beoþ his gode werkes þe 
beoþ forloren alle Yet upon al þis ilke he is himseolf biwrixlet ant bicumen of Godes 
child þe deofles bearn of helle eatelich to seonne as Godd seolf i þe Godspel seiþ þenche euch of his estat þet he is oþer wes in ant he 
mei seon hwervore he ah to siken sare Forþi seiþ Jeremie Make bitter man as wif deþ for hire child þe nefde bute 
him ane ant siþ hit bivoren hire fearliche asteorven Nu þe oþer þet ich bihet A mon 
þe were idemet for a luþer morþre to beo forbearnd al cwic oþer scheomeliche 
ahonget hu walde his heorte stonden Me þu unseli sunful þa þu þurh deadlich

beon ahonget o bearninde wearitre i þe eche lei of helle

forlorene þet

feondes chaffere he yeove þe sunne ant tu him þi sawle ant ti bodi mid al to weane 
ant to wontreaþe world abuten ende Nu þe þridde scheortliche þench a mon 
þe hefde al þe world o walde ant hefde for his cweadschipe forloren al on a stunde 
 hu he walde murnin ant sari iwurþen þenne ahest tu to beon hundret siþe 
sarure þe þurh an heaved sunne forlure þe riche of heovene forlure ure Laverd 
þet is hundret siþen ye þusent þusent siþen betere þen is al þe world eorþe ba 
ant heovene Nu yet þe feorþe yef þe king 
hefde bitaht his deore sune to his an cniht to lokin ant unþeode leadde forþ þis child 
in his warde swa þet tet child seolf weorrede upon his feader wiþ þet unþeode nalde 
þe cniht beo sari ant scheomien ful sare We beoþ alle Godes sunen þe kinges of 
heovene þe haveþ bitaht ure euch an engel i warde Sari is he on his wise hwen 
unþeode leat us forþ hwen we ure gode feader wreaþeþ wiþ sunne Beo we sari 
þet we eaver schulen wreaþen swuch feader ant sweamen swuch wardein þe wit 
ant wereþ us eaver wiþ þe unseli gastes for elles uvele us stode Ah we schuhteþ 
him awei hwen we doþ deadlich sunne ant heo leapeþ þenne to sone se he us 
firseþ Halde we him neh us wiþ smeal of gode werkes ant us in his warde Wat 
Crist ure euchan to se gentil wardein bereþ to lutel menske ant kunnen him to lutel 
þonc of his servise þeos ant monie reisuns beoþ hwi mon mei beo bitterliche sari 
for his sunnen ant wepen ful sare Ant wel is him þe swa mei for wop is sawle heale 
Ure Laverd deþ toward us as me deþ to uvel deattur nimeþ leasse þen we ahen him 
ant is þah wel ipaiet We ahen him blod for blod ant ure blod þah ayein his blod þet 
he schedde for us were ful unefne change Ah wast tu hu me yeddeþ me nimeþ ed 
uvel dettur aten for hweate ant ure Laverd nimeþ ed us teares ayein his blod ant is 
wilcweme He weop o þe rode o Lazre o Jerusalem for oþer monne sunnen Yef 
we wepeþ for ure ahne nis na muche wunder Wepe we quoþ þe hali mon i þa me hefde longe on him iyeiet efter sarmun Leote we quoþ he teares 
leste ure ahne teares forseoþen us in helle 
Schrift schal beon ihal þet is iseid al to a mon ut of childhade þe povre 
widewe hwen ha wule hire hus cleansin ha gedereþ al þe greaste on an heap on alre 
earst ant schuveþ hit ut þenne þe refter kimeþ eft ayein ant heapeþ eft togederes 
þet wes ear ileavet ant schuveþ hit ut efter þe refter o þe smeale dust yef hit 
dusteþ swiþe ha flaskeþ weater ant swopeþ ut efter al þet oþer Alswa schal þe 
schriveþ him efter þe greate schuven ut þe smealre Yef dust of lihte þohtes windeþ 
to swiþe up flaski teares on ham ne schulen ha nawt þenne ablende þe heorte 
ehnen Hwase heleþ eawiht he naveþ iseid nawiht forhwon he beo þe skerre ah 
is ilich þe mon þe haveþ on him monie deadliche wunden ant schaweþ þe leche alle 
ant let healen buten an þet he deieþ upon as he schulde on alle He is ase men in a 
schip þe haveþ monie þurles þer þe weater þreasteþ in ant heo dutteþ alle buten 
an þurh hwam ha druncniþ alle clane Me teleþ of þe hali mon þe lei on his deaþ
uvel ant wes laþ to seggen a sunne of his childhad ant his abbat bed him allegate 
seggen Ant he ondswerede þet hit nere na neod forþi þet he wes lute child þa he 
hit wrahte O least þah unneaþe þurh þe abbates ropunge þet he hit seide ant deide 
þ refter sone Efter his deaþ com a niht ant schawde him to his abbat i snawhwite 
schrudes as þe þet was iborhen ant seide þet sikerliche yef he nefde þet ilke þing 
þet he dude i childhad i schrift utterliche iseid he were idemet bimong þe forlorene 
Alswa of anoþer þet wes for neh fordemet forþi þet he hefde enchearre ined a 
mon to drinken ant deide þe rof unschriven Alswa of þe leafdi forþi þet ha hefde i
leanet to a wake a wummon an of hire weden Ah hwase haveþ yeorne isoht alle þe 
hurnen of his heorte ne ne con rungi mare ut yef þer eawiht edluteþ hit is ich 
hopie i þe schrift ischuven ut mid tet oþer hwen þer ne liþ na yemeles ant he 
walde fein mare yef he cuþe seggen 
Schrift schal beo naket þet is naketliche imaket nawt bisamplet feire ne 
hendeliche ismaket ah schulen þe wordes beon ischawet efter þe werkes þet is 
tacne of heatunge þet me tukeþ to wundre þing þet me heateþ swiþe Yef þu 
heatest ti sunne hwi spekest tu menskeliche þe rof Hwi hudest tu his fulþe Spec hit 
scheome schendfulliche ant tuk hit al to wundre alswa as þu wel wult schende þen 
schucke Sire ha seiþ þe wummon ich habbe ihaved leofmon oþer ich habbe

Do awei þe totagges Unwrih þe ant sei Sire Godes are ich am a ful stod
meare a stinkinde hore Yef þi fa a ful nome ant cleope þi sunne fule Make hit i

mare þen of a wepmon for hit bicom me wurse Ich am an ancre a nunne a wif

wes wiþ swuch mon ant nempni þenne munek preost oþer clearc ant

i chirchyard biheold hit oþer wreastlunge ant oþre fol gomenes spec þus 
oþer pleide bivoren worltliche men bivoren recluse in ancrehus ed oþer þurl þen

meseolven I chirche ich þohte þus biheold him ed te weovede Of þe time 
alswa Sire ich wes of swuch ealde þet ich ahte wel to habben wisluker iwite me 
 Sire ich hit dude in lenten i feasten dahes in hali dahes hwen oþre weren ed chirche 
 Sire ich wes sone overcumen ant is þe sunne mare þen yef ich hefde ibeon akeast 
wiþ strengþe ant feole swenges Sire ich wes þe biginnunge hwi swuch þing

ful wel ear þen ich hit eaver dude hu uvele hit were idon ant dude hit noþeleatere 
þe manere alswa seggen þet is þe feorþe totagge Sire þis sunne ich dude þus 
ant o þisse wise þus ich leornede hit earst þus ich com earst þe rin þus 
ich dude hit forþward o þus feole wisen þus fulliche þus scheomeliche þus 
ich sohte delit hu ich meast mahte paien mi lustes brune ant seggen al þe wise Tale

iwonet for to speoke þus hercni þullich speche þenchen hwiche þochtes foryeme

 Ich habbe ibeon þus ofte wraþ seoþþen ich wes ischriven nest ant for þulli

Schrift schal beon ofte imaket forþi is i þe Sawter Ant ure Laverd seolf seiþ to his deciples 
 Ga we eft seide he into Judee Judee spealeþ schrift ant swa we ifindeþ 
þet he wende ofte ut of Galilee into Judee Galilee spealeþ hweol forte learen us 
þet we of þe worldes turpelnesse ant of sunne hweol ofte gan to schrifte For þis is 
þe sacrement efter þe weofdes sacrement ant efter fulluht þet te feond is laþest as

Yef hit timeþ bi dei ear þen me slepe Hwa durste slepen hwil his deadliche fa heolde
