amead yef he liþ biþencheþ him hwenne he wule arisen A wummon þe haveþ i
losed hire nelde oþer a sutere his eal secheþ hit ananriht ant towent euch strea aþet 
hit beo ifunden ant Godd þurh sunne forloren schal liggen unsoht seove dahes 
fulle Nihe þinges beoþ þet ahten hihin to schrift þe pine þet okereþ for sunne is 
þe deofles feh þet he yeveþ to okere ant to gavel of pine ant eaver se mon liþ lengre 
in his sunne se þe gavel waxeþ of pine i purgatoire oþer her oþer in helle þe oþer þing is þe muchele ant te reowþfule lure þet he 
leoseþ þet na þing þet he deþ nis Gode licwurþe þe þridde is deaþ þet he nat hweþer he schule þet ilke dei ferliche asteorven þe feorþe is secnesse þet he ne mei þenche wel bute 
ane of his uvel ne speoken as he schulde bute granin for his eche ant grunte mare 
for his stiche þen for his sunne þe fifte þing is 
muche scheome þet hit is efter val to liggen se longe ant hure under þe schucke þe 
seste is þe wunde þet eaver wurseþ on hond ant strengre is to healen þe seoveþe þing is uvel 
wune þet Lazre bitacneþ þe stonc se longe he hefde ilein i þer eorþe o 
hwam ure Laverd weop as þe Godspel teleþ ant risede ant mengde himseolven ant 
yeide lude upon him ear he him arearde forte schawin hu strong hit is to arisen of uvel 
wune þe roteþ in his sunne Seinte Marie Lazre stonc of fowr dahes Hu stinkeþ þe 
sunfule of fowr yer oþer of five O seiþ Seint Austin hu earmliche he ariseþ þe under 
wune of sunne haveþ ilein longe Monie 
hundes seiþ Daviþ habbeþ biset me Hwen gredi hundes stondeþ bivore þe 
bord nis hit neod yerde As ofte as eani lecheþ toward te ant reaveþ þe of þi mete 
nult tu as ofte smiten Elles ha walden kecchen of þe al þet tu hefdest Ant tu alswa 
þenne nim þe yerde of þi tunge ant as ofte as þe dogge of helle kecheþ ei god from 
þe smit him ananriht mid te yerde of þi tunge i schrift ant smit him se luþerliche 
þet him laþi ant drede to snecchen eft toward te þet dunt of alle duntes is him 
dunte laþest þe hund þe fret leþer oþer awurieþ ahte me hit beat ananriht 
þet he understonde forhwi he is ibeaten þenne ne dear he nawt eft do þet ilke Beat 
alswa mid ti tunge i schrift þe hund of helle ananriht ant he wule beon ofdred to do 
þe eft swuch þucke Hwa is se fol þet he seiþ bi þe hund þet fret leþer Abid aþet 
tomarhen Ne beat tu him nawt yetten Ah ananriht beat Beat beat ananriht 
Nis þing i þe world þet smeorteþ him sarre þen deþ swuch beatunge Se me 
deoppre wadeþ i þe feondes leiven se me kimeþ up leatere þe eahtuþe þing is 
þet Seint Gregoire seiþ þet is sunne þet nis sone ibet draheþ anan anoþer 
ant þet eft þe þridde ant swa euchan cundleþ mare ant wurse cundel þen þe 
seolve moder þe niheþe reisun is se he ear biginneþ her to don his penitence se 
he haveþ to beten leasse i pine of purgatoire þis beoþ nu nihe reisuns ant monie ma 
þer beoþ hwi schrift ah to beon imaket aa on hihþe 
Schrift ah to beon eadmod as þe puplicanes wes nawt as þe phariseus wes þe 
talde his goddeden ant schawde þet hale forþ þa he schulde habben unwrihen hise 
wunden Forþi he wende unhealet as ure Laverd seolf teleþ ut of þe temple 
Eadmodnesse is ilich þeose cointe hearloz hare gutefeastre hare flowinde cweise 
þet ha putteþ eaver forþ Ant yef hit is eatelich ha schawiþ hit yet eateluker i riche 
monnes ehnen þet ha habben reowþe of ham ant yeoven ham god þe reaþere 
Hudeþ hare hale claþ ant doþ on alre uvemest fiterokes al totorene O þis ilke wise 
eadmodnesse eadmodliche bigileþ ure Laverd ant biyet of his god wiþ seli truandise 
hudeþ eaver hire god schaweþ forþ hire poverte put forþ hire cancre wepinde ant 
graninde bivore Godes ehnen halseþ meadlesliche on his derve passiun on his deore
wurþe blod on his fif wunden on his moder teares o þe ilke tittes þet he seac þe 
milc þet hine fedde on alle his halhene luve o þe deore druerie þet he haveþ to his 
deore spuse þet is to cleane sawle oþer to Hali Chirche on his deaþ o rode for 
hire to biyeotene Wiþ þus anewil ropunge halseþ efter sum help to þe wrecche 
meoseise to lechni wiþ þe seke to healen hire cancre Ant ure Laverd ihalset swa 
ne mei for reowþe wearnen hire ne sweamen hire wiþ warne nomeliche swa as he 
is se unimete large þet him nis na þing leovere þen þet he mahe ifinden acheisun 
forte yeovene Ah hwase yelpeþ of his god as doþ i schrift þeos prude hwet neod 
is ham to helpe Moni haveþ a swuch manere to seggen hire sunnen þet hit is wurþ 
a dearne yelp ant hunteþ efter hereword of mare halinesse 
Schrift ah to beon scheomeful bi þet te folc of Israel wende ut þurh þe Reade Sea 
þet wes read ant bitter is bitacnet þet we moten þurh rudi scheome þet is i soþ 
schrift ant þurh bitter penitence passin to heovene God riht is wat Crist þet us 
scheomie bivore mon þe foryeten scheome þa we duden þe sunne bivore Godes 
sihþe For al 
þet is al is naket seiþ Seinte Pawel ant open to his ehnen wiþ hwam we schulen 
rikenin alle ure deden Scheome is þe measte deal as Seint Austin seiþ of ure 
penitence Ant Sein Bernard seiþ þet na 
deorewurþe yimstan ne deliteþ swa muchel mon to bihalden as deþ Godes ehe þe 
rude of monnes neb þe riht seiþ hise sunnen Understond wel þis word Schrift is a 
sacrement ant euch sacrament haveþ an ilicnesse utewiþ of þet hit wurcheþ in
wiþ as hit is i fulluht þe wesschunge wiþuten bitacneþ þe wesschunge of sawle 
wiþinnen Alswa i schrift þe cwike rude of þe neb deþ to understonden þet te 
sawle þe wes bla ant nefde bute dead heow haveþ icaht cwic heow ant is irudet 
feire 
Schrift schal beo dredful þet tu segge wiþ Jerome As ofte as ich am ischriven eaver me þuncheþ 
me unschriven for eaver is sum foryeten of þe totagges Forþi seiþ Seint Austin þet is þe 
beste mon of al þe world yef ure Laverd demde him al efter rihtwisnesse ant nawt 
efter mearci wa schulde him iwurþen 
 Ah his mearci toward us weieþ eaver mare þen þe rihte nearewe 
Schrift schal beon hopeful Hwase seiþ as he con ant deþ al þet he mei Godd ne 
bit na mare Ah hope ant dred schulen aa beon imengt togederes þis forte bitacnin 
wes i þe alde lahe ihaten þet te twa grindelstanes ne schulde namon twinnin þe 
neoþere þe liþ stille ant bereþ hevi charge bitacneþ fearlac þe teieþ mon from 
sunne ant is iheveget her wiþ heard forte beo quite of heardre þe uvere stan 
bitacneþ hope þe eorneþ ant stureþ hire i gode werkes eaver wiþ trust of muche 
mede þeos twa namon ne parti from oþer for as Sein Gregoire seiþ 
 Dred wiþuten hope makeþ mon untrusten ant hope wiþute dred makeþ over
trusten þeos twa unþeawes untrust ant overtrust beoþ þe deofles tristen þer 
þet wrecche beast seldene edstearteþ Triste is þer me sit mid te greahunz forte 
kepe þe heare oþer tildeþ þe nettes ayein him Toward an of þeos twa is al þet he 
sleateþ for þer beoþ his greahunz þer beoþ his nettes Untrust ant overtrust 
beoþ of alle sunnen nest te yete of helle Wiþ dred wiþuten hope þet is wiþ 
untrust wes Caymes schrift ant Judasen forhwi ha forferden Wiþ hope wiþute 
dred þet is wiþ overtrust is þe unselies sahe þe seiþ i þe Sawter Nis nawt Godd quoþ ha se grim as ye 
him fore makieþ Na he seiþ Daviþ Yeoi he ant seiþ þenne On alre earst he 
cleopeþ þe overtrusti unbilevet þe unbilevet wiþ hwon gremeþ he Godd almihti 
Wiþ þon þet he seiþ Nule he nawt se nearowliche demen as ye seggeþ Yeoi 
siker ah he wule þus þeos twa unþeawes beoþ to grimme robberes ievenet For 
þe an þet is overtrust reaveþ Godd his rihte dom ant his rihtwisnesse þe 
oþer þet is untrust reaveþ him his milce Ant swa ha beoþ umben to fordon 
Godd seolf for Godd ne muhte nawt beon wiþuten rihtwisnesse ne wiþuten milce 
Nu þenne hwucche unþeawes beoþ evening to þeose þe wulleþ Godd acwellen on 
hare fule wise Yef þu art to trusti ant haldest Godd to nessche forte wreoke sunne 
sunne likeþ him bi þin tale Ah bihald hu he wrec in his heh engel þe þohte of a 
prude hu he wrec in Adam þe bite of an eappel hu he bisencte Sodome ant Gommorre 
were ant wif ant wenchel þe nomecuþe burhes al a muche schire dun into helle 
grunde þeras is nu þe Deade Sea þet nawiht cwikes nis inne hu he i Noes 
flod al þe world adrencte bute eahte i þe arche hu he in his ahne folc Israel his 
deorling grimliche awrec him ase ofte as ha gulten Daþan ant Abyron Chore ant his 
feren þe oþre alswa þe he sloh bi feole þusendes ofte for hare gruchunge ane On 
oþer half loke yef þu havest untrust of his unimete milce hu lihtliche ant hu sone 
Seinte Peter efter þet he hefde forsaken him ant þet for a cwene word wes wiþ him 
isahtnet hu þe þeof o rode þe hefde aa ilived uvele in a sterthwile hefde ed him 
milce wiþ a feier speche Forþi bitweone þeos twa untrust ant overtrust hope ant 
dred beon aa ifeiet togederes 
Schrift yet schal beo wis ant to wis mon imaket of uncuþe sunnen nawt to 
yunge preostes yunge ich segge of wit ne to sotte alde Bigin earst ed prude ant 
sech alle þe bohes þe rof as ha beoþ þe ruppe iwritene hwuch falle to þe þe refter 
alswa of onde ant ga we swa duneward rawe bi rawe aþet to þe leaste Ant drah 
togedere al þe team under þe moder 
Schrift ah to beo soþ ne lih þu nawt o þeseolf For as Seint Austin seiþ 
 þe seiþ leas on himseolf þurh to muchel eadmodnesse he is imaket sunful þah 
he ear nere Sein Gregoire seiþ þah Cunde of god heorte is to beon offearet of sunne þeras nan nis 
ofte oþer weie swiþre his sunne sumchearre þen he þurfte Weien hit to lutel is 
ase uvel oþer wurse þe middel wei of meosure is eaver guldene Drede we us eavre 
for ofte we weneþ forte don a lutel uvel ant doþ a great sunne ofte wel to donne ant 
doþ al to cweade Segge we eaver þenne wiþ Seinte Anselme Na god in us nis 
of us ure god is Godes Ah sunne is of us ant ure ahne Godes god hwen ich hit do 
quoþ he Seint Anselme swa o summe wise min uvel hit forgneaieþ oþer ich hit do 
ungleadliche oþer to ear oþer to leate oþer leote wel þe rof þah namon hit nute 
oþer walde þet ei hit wiste oþer yemelesliche do hit oþer to unwisliche to muchel 
oþer to lutel þus eaver sum uvel mongleþ him wiþ mi god þet Godes grace yeveþ 
me þet hit mei lutel likin Godd ant mislikin ofte Seinte Marie Hwen þe hali mon 
seide þus bi himseolf hu mahe we hit witerliche seggen bi us wrecches 
Schrift ah to beon willes þet is willeliche unfreinet nawt idrahen of þe as þin 
unþonkes Hwil þu const seggen eawt sei al uneasket Me ne schal easki nan but for 
neode ane for of þe easkunge mei uvel fallen bute hit beo þe wisre On oþer half 
moni mon abit forte schriven him aþet te nede tippe Ah ofte him liheþ þe wrench 
þet he ne mei hwen he wule þe nalde þa he mahte Na mare cangschipe nis þen 
setten Godd tearme as þah grace were his as he bere hire in his purs to neomen upo 
grace þe rin i þe tearme as he himseolf sette Nai beal ami nai þe tearme is i Godes 
hond nawt i þi bandun Hwen Godd beot hit te reach to ba þe honden for wiþdrahe 
he his hond þu maht þe refter lokin Yef uvel oþer oþerhwet ned te to schrifte lo 
hwet seiþ Seint Austin Servises inedde ne 
cwemeþ nawt ure Laverd þah noþeleatere betere is o þene no Nis neaver to leate penitence þet is soþliche imaket he 
seiþ eft himseolven Ah betere is as Daviþ seiþ þet is mi flesch is ifluret bicumen al neowe for ich chulle 
schrive me ant herie Godd willes Wel seiþ he ifluret to bitacnin wilschrift for 
þe eorþe al unnet ant te treon alswa openiþ ham ant bringeþ forþ misliche flures Eadmodnesse abstinence culvres 
unlaþnesse ant oþre swucche vertuz beoþ feire i Godes ehnen ant swote i Godes 
nease smeallinde flures Of ham make his herbearhe inwiþ þeseolven for his delices 
he seiþ beoþ þer forte wunien 
Schrift ah to beon ahne Namon ne schal i schrift wreien bute himseolven ase 
forþ as he mei þis ich segge forþi þet swuch aventure bitimeþ to sum mon oþer 
to sum wummon þet ha ne mei nawt fulleliche wreien hireseolven bute ha wreie 
oþre Ah bi nome noþeleatere ne nempni ha nawt þe ilke þah þe schriftfeader 
wite wel toward hwam hit turne ah a munk oþer a preost nawt Wilyam ne 
 Water þah þer ne beo nan oþer 
Schrift schal beo studevest to halde þe penitence ant leave þe sunne þet tu segge 
to þe preost Ich habbe studefestliche i þonc ant in heorte þis sunne to forleten ant 
do þe penitence þe preost ne schal nawt easki þe yef þu wult þeonnevorþ 
forhate þi sunne inoh is þet tu segge þet tu hit havest on heorte treoweliche to donne 
þurh Godes grace ant yef þu fallest eft þe rin þet tu wult ananriht arisen þurh 
Godes help ant cumen ayein to schrifte Ga quoþ 
ure Laverd to a sunful wummon ant have wil þet tu nult sungi na mare þus ne 
easkede he nan oþer sikernesse 
Schrift ah to beon biþoht bivore longe Of fif þinges wiþ þi wit gedere þine 
sunnen of alle þine ealdes of childhad of yuheþehad gedere al togederes þe refter 
gedere þe studen þet tu in wunedest ant þench yeorne hwet tu dudest in euch stude 
sunderliche ant in euch ealde þe refter sech al ut ant trude þine sunnen bi þine fif 
wittes þe refter bi alle þine limen i hwuch þu havest isuneget meast oþer oftest 
Aleast sunderliche bi dahes ant bi tiden 
Nu ye habbeþ alle ihaved as ich understonde þe sixtene stucchen þe ich bihet to 
dealen ant alle ich habbe tobroken ham ow mine leove sustren as me deþ to children 
þe mahten wiþ unbroke bread deien on hunger Ah me is þet wite ye moni 
crome edfallen Secheþ ham ant gederiþ for ha beoþ sawle fode 
þulli schrift þet haveþ þus þes sixtene stucchen haveþ þe ilke muchele mihten 
þet ich earst seide þreo ayein þe deovel þreo on usseolven ant þreo ayeines þe 
world deorewurþe over gold or ant yimmes of Ynde 
Mine leove sustren þis fifte dale þe is of schrift limpeþ to alle men iliche forþi 
ne wundri ye ow nawt þet ich toward ow nomeliche nabbe nawt ispeken i þis dale 
Habbeþ þah to ower bihove þis lutle leaste ende Of alle cuþe sunnen as of prude of 
great oþer of heh heorte of onde of wreaþþe of slawþe of yemeles of idel word 
of untohene þohtes of sum idel herunge of sum fals gleadunge oþer of hevi murnunge 
of ypocresie of mete of drunch to muchel oþer to lutel of gruchunge of grim chere 
of silences ibrokene of sitten longe ed þurl of ures mis iseide wiþute yeme of 
heorte oþer in untime of sum fals word of sware of plohe of ischake lahtre of 
schede cromen oþer ale of leote þinges muhelin rustin oþer rotien claþes unseowet 
bireinet unwesschen breoke nep oþer disch oþer biseo yemelesliche ei þing þet me 
wiþ feareþ oþer ahte to yemen of keorfunge of hurtunge þurh unbisehenesse 
of alle þe þinges þe beoþ i þis riwle þe beoþ misnumene of alle þulliche þing 
schrive hire euche wike eanes ed te leaste for nan se lutel nis of þeos þet te deovel 
naveþ enbrevet on his rolle Ah schrift hit schrapeþ of ant makeþ him to leosen 
muchel of his hwile Ah al þet schrift ne schrapeþ of al he wule o Domesdei rede ful 
witerliche forte bicleopie þe wiþ a word ne schal þer wontin Nu þenne ich reade 
yeoveþ him to writen þet leaste þet ye eaver mahen for na meoster nis him leovere 
ant hwetse he writ beoþ umben to schrapien hit of cleanliche Wiþ na þing ne mahe 
ye matin him betere To euch preost mei ancre schriven hire of swucche utterliche 
sunnen þe to alle bifalleþ Ah ful trusti ha schal beon o þe preostes godlec þet ha 
allunge schaweþ to hu hire stonde abute flesches temptatiuns yef ha is swa ifondet 
 bute i deaþes dute þus þah me þuncheþ þet ha mei seggen Sire flesches 
fondunge þet ich habbe oþer habbe ihaved geaþ to vorþ upo me þurh mi 
þeafunge Ich am ofdred leste ich ga drivinde oþerhwiles to swiþe forþward mine 
fol þohtes ant fule umbestunde as þah ich huntede efter licunge Ich mihte þurh 
Godes strengþe schaken ham ofte of me yef ich were cwicliche ant stealewurþliche 
umben Ich am offearet sare þet te delit i þe þoht leaste to longe ofte swa þet hit 
cume neh skiles yettunge Ne dear ich þet ha deopluker ne witerluker schrive hire to 
yung preost herabuten ant yet of þis inohreaþe him walde þunche wunder Ah to 
hire ahne schriftfeader oþer to sum lifhali mon yef ha mei him habben culle al þe 
pot ut þer speowe ut al þet wunder þer wiþ fule wordes þet fulþe efter þet hit 
is tuki al to wundre swa þet ha drede þet ha hurte his earen þet hercneþ hire 
sunnen Yef ei ancre nat nawt of þulliche þinges þonki yeorne Jesu Crist ant halde 
hire i drede þe deovel nis nawt dead þet wite ha þah he slepe 
Lihte gultes beteþ þus anan bi owseolven ant þah seggeþ ham i schrift hwen ye 
þencheþ ham on as ye speokeþ mid preoste For þe leaste of alle sone se ye 
underyeoteþ hit falleþ bivoren ower weoved o cros to þer eorþe ant seggeþ Ich gulte Mearci Laverd þe preost ne þearf for na gult bute hit beo þe 
greattre leggen oþer schrift on ow þen þet lif þet ye leadeþ efter þeos riwle Ah 
efter þe absolutiun he schal þus seggen Al þet god þet tu eaver dest ant al þet 
uvel þet tu eaver þolest for þe luve of Jesu Crist inwiþ þine ancrewahes al ich 
engoini þe al ich legge upo þe i remissiun of þeose ant foryevenesse of alle þine 
sunnen Ant þenne sum lutles ihweat he mei leggen upon ow as a Salm oþer twa tene oþer tweolve Disceplines echi to yef him swa þuncheþ 
Efter þe totagges þe beoþ iwriten þe ruppe he schal þe sunne demen mare oþer 
leasse A sunne ful foryevelich mei wurþe ful deadlich þurh sum uvel totagge þe liþ 
þerbisiden Efter schrift falleþ to speoken of penitence þet is deadbote ant 
swa we habbeþ inyong ut of þis fifte dale into þe seste

Al is penitence ant strong penitence þet ye eaver dreheþ mine leove 
sustren Al þet ye eaver doþ of god al þet ye þolieþ is ow martirdom 
i se derf ordre For ye beoþ niht ant dei upo Godes rode bliþe mahe 
ye beon þe rof For as Seinte Pawel seiþ As 
ye scottiþ wiþ him of his pine on eorþe ye schule scotti wiþ him of his blisse in 
heovene Forþi seiþ Seinte Pawel Ant Hali Chirche singeþ Al ure blisse mot beon i Jesu Cristes rode þis 
word nomeliche limpeþ to recluses hwas blisse ah to beon allunge i Godes rode 
Ich chulle biginnen herre ant lihten swa herto Neomeþ nu gode yeme for al 
meast is Sein Beornardes sentence 
þreo manere men of Godes icorene livieþ on eorþe þe ane mahe beon to 
gode pilegrimes ievenet þe oþre to deade þe þridde to ihongede wiþ hare 
gode wil o Jesuse rode þe forme beoþ gode þe oþre beoþ betere þe þridde 
best of alle 
To þe forme gredeþ Seinte Peter inwardliche Ich halsi ow he seiþ as elþeodie ant pilegrimes þet ye 
wiþhalden ow from fleschliche lustes þe weorriþ ayein þe sawle þe gode 
pilegrim halt eaver his rihte wei forþward þah he seo oþer here idele gomenes 
ant wundres bi þe weie he ne edstont nawt as foles doþ ah halt forþ his rute ant 
hiheþ toward his giste He ne bereþ na gersum bute his speonse gnedeliche ne 
claþes bute ane þeo þet him to neodeþ þis beoþ hali men þe þah ha beon i 
þe world ha beoþ þe rin as pilegrimes ant gaþ wiþ god liflade toward te riche 
of heovene ant seggeþ wiþ þe Apostle þet is nabbe we na wununge her ah we secheþ 
oþer Beoþ bi þe leaste þet ha mahen ne ne haldeþ na tale of na worltlich 
frovre þah ha beon i worltlich wei as ich seide of pilegrim ah habbeþ hare 
heorte eaver toward heovene Ant ahen wel to habben for oþer pilegrimes gaþ 
i muche swinc to sechen ane sontes banes as Sein James oþer Sein Giles Ah 
þeo pilegrimes þe gaþ toward heovene ha gaþ to beon isontet ant to finden 
Godd seolf ant alle his hali halhen liviende i blisse ant schulen livien wiþ him i 
wunne buten ende Ha ifindeþ iwis Sein Julienes in þe weifearinde men 
yeornliche bisecheþ 
Nu beoþ þeose gode ah yet beoþ þe oþre betere for allegate pilegrimes as 
ich ear seide al gan ha eaver forþward ne bicumen burhmen i þe worldes 
burh ham þuncheþ sumchearre god of þet ha seoþ bi weie ant edstuteþ sum
deal þah ha ne don mid alle ant moni þing ham falleþ to hwerþurh ha beoþ i
lette swa þet mare hearm is sum kimeþ leate ham sum neaver mare Hwa 
is þenne skerre ant mare ut of þe world þen pilegrimes þet is to seggen 
þen þeo men þe habbeþ worltlich þing ant ne luvieþ hit nawt ah yeoveþ hit 
as hit kimeþ ham ant gaþ untrusset lihte as pilegrimes doþ toward heovene 
Hwa beoþ betere þene þeos Godd wat þeo beoþ betere þe þe Apostle spekeþ 
to ant seiþ in his epistle Ye beoþ deade ant ower lif is ihud mid Criste Hwen he þet is ower 
lif eadeaweþ ant springeþ as þe dahunge efter nihtes þeosternesse ant ye schulen 
wiþ him springen schenre þen þe sunne into eche blisse þe nu beoþ þus 
deade hare liflade is herre for pilegrim eileþ monihwet þe deade nis noht of 
þah he ligge unburiet ant rotie buven eorþe Preise him laste him do him scheome 
sei him scheome al him is iliche leof þis is a seli deaþ þet makeþ cwic 
mon þus oþer cwic wummon ut of þe worlde Ah sikerliche hwase is þus 
dead in hireseolven Godd liveþ in hire heorte For þis is þet te Apostle seiþ Ich livie nawt ich ah 
Crist liveþ in me þurh his inwuniende grace ant is as þah he seide worltlich 
speche worltlich sihþe ant euch worltlich þing ifindeþ me deade Ah þet te 
limpeþ to Crist þet ich seo ant here ant wurche i cwicnesse þus riht is euch 
religius dead to þe worlde ant cwic þah to Criste þis is an heh steire ah yet is 
þah an herre Ant hwa stod eaver þe rin Godd wat þe þe seide þis is þet ich seide þe ruppe Crist me schilde 
forte habben eani blisse i þis world bute i Jesu Cristes rode mi Laverd þurh 
hwam þe world is me unwurþ ant ich am unwurþ hire as weari þe is ahonget 
A Laverd hehe stod he þe spec o þisse wise Ant þis is ancre steire þet ha þus 
segge I na þing ne blissi ich me bute i 
Godes rode þet ich þolie nu wa ant am itald unwurþ as Godd wes o rode 
Lokiþ leove sustren hu þis steire is herre þen eani beo of þe oþre þe pilegrim 
i þe worldes wei þah he ga forþward toward te ham of heovene he siþ ant 
hereþ unnet ant spekeþ umbehwile wreaþeþ him for weohes ant moni þing 
mei letten him of his jurnee þe deade nis na mare of scheome þen of menske of 
heard þen of nesche for he ne feleþ nowþer ant forþi ne ofearneþ he nowþer 
wa ne wunne Ah þe þe is o rode ant haveþ blisse þe rof he wendeþ scheome to 
menske ant wa into wunne ant ofearneþ forþi hure over hure þis beoþ þeo 
þe neaver ne beoþ gleade iheortet bute hwen ha þolieþ sum wa oþer sum 
scheome wiþ Jesu on his rode For þis is þe selhþe on eorþe hwase mei for 
Godes luve habben scheome ant teone þus lo rihte ancres ne beoþ nawt ane 
pilegrimes ne yet nawt ane deade ah beoþ of þeos þridde For al hare blisse is 
forte beon ahonget sariliche ant scheomeliche wiþ Jesu on his rode þeos mahe 
bliþe wiþ Hali Chirche singen þet is as ich 
seide ear Hwetse beo of oþre þe habbeþ hare blisse summe i flesches licunge 
summe i worldes dweole summe in oþres uvel we mote nede blissin us i Jesu 
Cristes rode þet is i scheome ant i wa þet he droh o rode Moni walde summes 
weis þolien flesches heardschipe ah beon itald unwurþ ne scheome ne mahte 
he þolien Ah he nis bute halflunge upo Godes rode yef he nis igreiþet to 
þolien ham baþe vilte ant asprete þeos twa scheome ant pine as Sein 
Beornard seiþ beoþ þe twa leaddresteolen þe beoþ up iriht to heovene Ant 
bitweone þeose steolen beoþ of alle gode þeawes þe tindes ifestnet bi hwucche 
me climbeþ to þe blisse of heovene Forþi þet Daviþ hefde þe twa steolen of 
þis leaddre þah he king were he clomb uppard ant seide baldeliche to ure Laverd 
 Bihald quoþ he ant sih min eadmodnesse ant mi swinc ant foryef me mine 
sunnen alle togederes Notiþ wel þes twa word þe Daviþ feieþ somet swinc 
ant eadmodnesse swinc i pine ant i wa i sar ant i sorhe eadmodnesse ayein 
woh of scheome þet mon dreheþ þe is itald unwurþ Ba þeos bihald in me 
quoþ Daviþ Godes deorling Ich habbe þeos twa leaddresteolen Leaf quoþ he bihinde me ant warp awei from me alle 
mine gultes þet ich ilihtet of hare hevinesse lihtliche stihe up to heovene bi 
þeos leaddre 
þeose twa þinges þet is wa ant scheome ifeiet togederes beoþ Helyes 
hweoles þe weren furene hit teleþ ant beren him up to parais þer he liveþ 
yetten Fur is hat ant read I þe heate is understonden euch wa þet eileþ flesch 
scheome bi þe reade Ah wel mei duhen ha beoþ her hweolinde ase hweoles 
overturneþ sone ne leasteþ nane hwile þis ilke is ec bitacnet bi cherubines 
sweord bivore paraise yeten þe wes of lei ant hweolinde ant turninde abuten Ne 
kimeþ nan into parais bute þurh þis leitinde sweord þe wes hat ant read ant in 
Helyes furene hweoles þet is þurh sar ant þurh scheome þe overturneþ 
tidliche ant agaþ sone Ant nes Godes rode wiþ his deorewurþe blod irudet 
ant ireadet forte schawin on himseolf þet pine ant sorhe ant sar schulden 
wiþ scheome beon iheowet Nis hit iwriten bi him þet is he wes buhsum his feader 
nawt ane to deaþ ah to deaþ o rode þurh þet he seide earst deaþ is pine 
understonden þurh þet he þe refter seiþ deaþ o þe rode is schendlac bitacnet 
for swuch wes Godes deaþ o þe deore rode pinful ant schentful over alle oþre 
Hwase eaver deieþ ine Godd ant o Godes rode þeos twa ha mot þolien scheome 
for him ant pine Scheome ich cleopie eaver her beon itald unwurþ ant beggin 
as an hearlot yef neod is hire liveneþ ant beon oþres beodesmon as ye 
beoþ leove sustren ant þolieþ ofte danger of swuch oþerhwile þe mahte 
beon ower þreal þis is þet eadi scheome þet ich of talie Pine ne trukeþ ow 
nawt I þeos ilke twa þing þet al penitence is in blissiþ ow ant gleadieþ for 
ayein þeos twa ow beoþ twafald blissen iyarket ayein scheome menske ayein 
pine delit ant reste buten ende Ha schulen seiþ Ysaie in hare ahne lond wealden twavald 
blisse ayein twavald wa þet ha her dreheþ In hare ahne lond seiþ Ysaie 
for alswa as þe uvele nabbeþ na lot in heovene ne þe gode nabbeþ na lot in 
eorþe In hare ahne lond ha schulen wealden blisse twafald cunne mede ayein 
twavald sorhe as þah he seide Ne þunche ham na feorlich þah ha her þolien 
as in uncuþ lond ant in uncuþ eard bituhhen unþeode scheome ba ant sorhe 
for swa deþ moni gentil mon þe is uncuþ in uncuþþe Me mot ute swinken ed 
hame me schal resten ant nis he a cang cniht þe secheþ reste i þe feht ant eise i 
þe place Al þis lif is a feht as Job 
witneþ Ah efter þis feht her yef we wel fehteþ menske ant reste abit us ed 
hame in ure ahne lond þet is heoveriche Lokiþ nu hu witerliche ure Laverd 
seolf hit witneþ Hwen ich sitte forte demen seiþ 
ure Laverd ye schulen sitten wiþ me ant deme wiþ me al þe world þet schal 
beon idemet kinges ant keisers cnihtes ant clearkes I þe sete is reste ant eise 
bitacnet ayein þe swinc þet her is I þe menske of þe dom þet ha schulen 
demen is hehschipe menskeful over alle understonden ayein scheome ant lahschipe 
þet ha her for Godes luve mildeliche þoleden 
Nis þer nu þenne bute þolien gleadliche for bi Godd seolf is iwriten þet 
is þurh schentful pine he com to gloire of blisful ariste Nis na selcuþ þenne 
yef we wrecche sunfule þolien her pine yef we wulleþ o Domesdei blisfule 
arisen Ant þet we mahen þurh his grace yef we usseolf wulleþ 
 Seinte Paweles sahe þe seiþ se wel eaver yef we beoþ iimpet to þe i
licnesse of Godes deaþ we schulen of his ariste þet is to seggen yef we 
libbeþ i scheome ant i pine for his luve i hwucche twa he deide we schulen 
beon iliche his blisful ariste ure bodi briht as his is world buten ende as Seinte 
Pawel witneþ Let oþre acemin hare bodi þe eorneþ 
bivorenhond Abide we ure Healent þe schal acemin ure efter his ahne Yef we þolieþ wiþ him we schule blissin wiþ 
him Nis þis god foreward Wat Crist nis he nawt god feolahe ne treowe þe 
nule scottin i þe lure as eft i þe biyete Godd schedde his blod for alle ah 
heom ane hit is wurþ þe fleoþ flesches licunge ant piniþ hamseolven Ant is 
þet eani wunder Nis Godd ure heaved ant we his limen alle Ah nis euch lim sar 
wiþ sorhe of þe heaved His lim þenne nis he nawt þe naveþ eche under se sar 
akinde heaved Hwen þe heaved sweat wel þet lim þe ne swet nawt nis hit 
uvel tacne He þe is ure heaved sweatte blodes swat for ure secnesse to turnen us 
of þet londuvel þet alle londes leien on ant liggeþ yette monie þe lim þe ne 
sweat nawt i swincful pine for his luve deuleset hit leaveþ in his secnesse ant 
nis þer bute forkeorven hit þah hit þunche sar Godd For betere is finger offe 
þen he ake eaver Cwemeþ he nu wel Godd þe þus bilimeþ him of himseolf 
þurh þet he nule sweaten Seinte Marie mearci Hit moste swa beon hit seiþ Crist þolie pine 
ant passiun ant swa habben inyong into his riche Lo deale hwet he seiþ swa 
habben inyong into his riche swa ant nan oþerweis Ant we wrecches sunfule 
wulleþ wiþ eise stihen to heovene þet is se hehe buven us ant se swiþe muchel 
wurþ Ant me ne mei nawt wiþuten swinc a lutel cote arearen ne twa þwongede 
scheos habbe wiþute bune Oþer þeo beoþ canges þe weneþ wiþ liht leapes 
buggen eche blisse oþer þe hali halhen þe bohten hit se deore Nes Seinte Peter 
ant Seinte Andrew þerevore istraht o rode Sein Lorenz o þe gridil ant laþlese 
meidnes þe tittes itoren of tohwiþeret o hweoles heafdes bicorven Ah ure 
sotschipe is sutel Ant heo weren ilich þeose yape children þe habbeþ riche 
feaderes þe willes ant waldes toteoreþ hare claþes forte habbe neowe Ure 
alde curtel is þe flesch þet we of Adam ure alde feader habbeþ þe neowe we 
schulen undervon of Godd ure riche feader i þe ariste of Domesdei hwen ure 
flesch schal blikien schenre þen þe sunne yef hit is totoren her wiþ wontreaþe 
ant wiþ weane Of þeo þe hare curtles toteoreþ o þisse wise seiþ Ysaie A folc tolaimet ant totoren a folc he seiþ fearlich schal makien to 
ure Laverd present of himseolven Folc tolaimet ant totoren wiþ strong liflade 
ant wiþ heard he cleopeþ folc fearlich for þe feond is of swucche offruht ant 
offearet Forþi þet Job wes þullich he meande him ant seide þet is he wulle yeoven fel for fel þe alde for þe 
neowe as þah he seide Ne geineþ me nawt to asailin him he is of þet totore 
folc He tereþ his alde curtel ant torendeþ þe alde pilche of his deadliche fel 
For þe fel is undeadlich þet i þe neowe ariste schal schine seovevald brihtre 
þen þe sunne Eise ant flesches este beoþ þes deofles mearken Hwen he siþ 
þeos mearken i mon oþer i wummon he wat þe castel is his ant geaþ baldeliche 
in þer he siþ iriht up swucche baneres as me deþ i castel I þet totore folc he 
misseþ his merken ant siþ in ham iriht up Godes banere þet is heardschipe 
of lif ant haveþ muche dred þe rof as Ysaie witneþ 
 Me leove sire seiþ sum ant is hit nu wisdom to don se wa himseolven 
Ant tu yeld me ondswere of tweie men hweþer is wisre Ha beoþ ba seke þe an 
forgeaþ al þet he luveþ of metes ant of drunches ant drinkeþ bitter sabraz forte 
acovrin heale þe oþer folheþ al his wil ant forþeþ his lustes ayein his secnesse 
ant leoseþ his lif sone Hweþer is wisre of þes twa Hweþer is betere his ahne 
freond Hweþer luveþ himseolf mare Ant hwa nis sec of sunne Godd for ure 
secnesse dronc attri drunch o rode ant we nulleþ nawt bittres biten for us
seolven Nis þer nawiht þe rof Sikerliche his folhere mot wiþ pine of his flesch 
folhin his pine Ne wene nan wiþ este stihen to heovene 
 Me sire seiþ sum eft wule Godd se wracfulliche wreoken upo sunne 
Ye mon For loke nu hu he hit heateþ swiþe Hu walde nu þe mon beate þet 
þing seolf hwerse he hit ifunde þe for muchel heatunge beote þe rof þe 
schadewe ant al þet hefde þerto eani licnesse Godd feader almihti hu beot 
he bitterliche his deorewurþe sune Jesu ure Laverd þet neaver nefde sunne 
bute ane þet he ber flesch ilich ure þet is ful of sunne Ant we schulden beon i
spearet þe beoreþ on us his sune deaþ þe wepne þet sloh him þet wes ure 
sunne ant he þe nefde nawt of sunne bute schadewe ane wes i þe ilke schadewe 
se scheomeliche ituket se sorhfulliche ipinet þet ear hit come þerto for þe 
þreatunge ane þe rof swa him agras þerayein þet he bed his feader are Sare quoþ he me grulleþ ayein mi muchele pine Mi feader 
yef hit mei beon speare me ed tis time þi wil þah ant nawt min eaver beo i
vorþet His deorewurþe feader forþi ne forber him nawt ah leide on him se 
luþerliche þet he bigon to greden wiþ reowþfule stevene Mi Godd mi Godd mi deorewurþe feader havest tu al forwarpe 
me þin anlepi sune þe beatest me se hearde For al þis ne lette he nawt ah 
beot se swiþe longe ant se swiþe grimliche þet he stearf o rode seiþ Ysaie þus ure beatunge feol on him for he dude 
himseolven bitweonen us ant his feader þe þreatte us forte smiten ase moder 
þet is reowþful deþ hire bitweonen hire child ant te wraþe sturne feader hwen 
he hit wule beaten þus dude ure Laverd Jesu Crist ikepte on him deaþes dunt 
forte schilden us þerwiþ Igracet beo his milce Hwerse muchel dunt is hit 
bulteþ ayein upo þeo þe þer neh stondeþ Soþliche hwase is neh him þe i
kepte se hevi dunt hit wule bulten on him ne nule he him neaver meanen for þet 
is þe preove þet he stont neh him Ant liht is þe bultunge to þolien for his luve 
þe underveng se hevi dunt us forte burhen from þe deofles botte i þe pine of 
helle 
 Yet seiþ moni mon hweat is Godd þe betere þah ich pini me for his luve 
Leove mon ant wummon Godd þuncheþ god of ure god Ure god is yef we doþ 
þet tet we ahen Nim yeme of þis essample A mon þe were feor ifearen ant me 
come ant talde him þet his deore spuse se swiþe murnede efter him þet heo 
wiþuten him delit nefde i na þing ah were for þoht of his luve leane ant el
heowet nalde him betere likin þen þet me seide him þet ha gleowde ant 
gomnede ant wedde wiþ oþre men ant livede i delices Alswa ure Laverd þet 
is þe sawle spus þet siþ al þet ha deþ þah he hehe sitte he is ful wel ipaiet 
þet ha murneþ efter him ant wule hihin toward hire mucheles þe swiþere wiþ 
yeove of his grace oþer fecchen hire allunge to him to gloire ant to blisse þurh
wuniende 
Ne grapi hire nan to softeliche hireseolven to bichearren Ne schal ha for hire 
lif witen hire al cleane ne halden riht hire chastete wiþuten twa þinges as Seint 
Ailred þe abbat wrat to his suster þet an is pinsunge i flesch wiþ feasten wiþ 
wecchen wiþ disceplines wiþ heard werunge heard leohe wiþ uvel wiþ 
muchele swinkes þe oþer is heorte þeawes devotiun reowfulnesse riht luve 
eadmodnesse ant vertuz oþre swucche Me sire þu ondswerest me suleþ 
Godd his grace Nis grace wilyeove Mine leove sustren þah cleannesse of 
chastete ne beo nawt bune ed Godd ah beo yeove of grace ungraciuse stondeþ 
þertoyeines ant makieþ ham unwurþe to halden se heh þing þe nulleþ swinc 
þervore bliþeliche þolien Bitweonen delices ant eise ant flesches este hwa 
wes eaver chaste Hwa bredde eaver inwiþ hire fur þet ha ne bearnde Pot þe 
walleþ swiþe nule he beon overleden oþer cald weater iwarpe þe rin ant 
brondes wiþdrahene þe wombepot þe walleþ of metes ant of drunches is se 
neh nehbur to þet fulitohe lim þet ha dealeþ þerwiþ þe brune of hire heate 
Ah monie mare hearm is beoþ se fleschwise ant swa overswiþe ofdred 
leste hare heaved ake leste hare licome febli to swiþe ant witeþ swa hare heale 
þet te gast unstrengeþ ant secleþ i sunne Ant þeo þe schulden ane lechnin hare 
sawle wiþ heorte bireowsunge ant flesches pinsunge forwurþeþ fisitiens ant 
licomes leche Dude swa Seinte Agace þe ondswerede ant seide to ure Laverdes 
sonde þe brohte salve o Godes half to healen hire tittes þet is fleschlich medecine ne dude ich me 
neavre Nabbe ye iherd tellen of þe þreo hali men Bute þe an wes iwunet 
for his calde mahe to nutten hate speces ant wes ornre of mete ant of drunch þen 
þe tweien oþre þe þah ha weren seke ne nomen neaver yeme hweat wes hal 
hwet unhal to eoten ne to drinken ah nomen eaver forþriht hwetse Godd ham 
sende ne makeden neaver strengþe of gingivre ne of zedual ne of clowes de 
gilofre A dei as ha þreo weren ifolen o slepe ant lei bitweone þes twa þe 
þridde þet ich seide com þe cwen of heovene ant twa meidnes wiþ hire þe 
an as þah hit were ber a letuaire þe oþer of gold a sticcke Ure Leafdi wiþ þe 
sticke nom ant dude i þe anes muþ of þe letuaire ant te meidnes eoden forþre to 
þe midleste Nai quoþ ure Leafdi he is his ahne leche Ga over to þe þridde 
Stod an hali mon of feor biheold al þis ilke Hwen sec mon haveþ ed hond þing 
þet wule don him god he hit mei wel notien Ah beon þe refter se ancreful 
nomeliche religius nis nawt Godd icweme Godd ant his desciples speken of 
sawle lechecreft Ypocras ant Galien of licomes heale þe an þe wes best i
learet of Jesu Cristes lechecreft seiþ flesches wisdom is deaþ to þe sawle as Job seiþ Swa we dredeþ 
flesches uvel ofte ear þen hit cume þet sawle uvel kimeþ up Ant we þolieþ 
sawle uvel forte edstearten flesches uvel as þah hit were betere to þolien 
galnesses brune þen heavedeche oþer grucchunge of a mistohe wombe Ant 
hweþer is betere i secnesse to beo Godes freo child þen i flesches heale to beo 
þreal under sunne Ant þis ne segge ich nawt swa þet wisdom ant meosure ne 
beon overal iloket þe moder is ant nurrice of alle gode þeawes Ah we cleopieþ 
ofte wisdom þet nis nan For soþ wisdom is don eaver sawle heale bivore flesches 
heale Ant hwen he ne mei nawt ba somet halden cheose ear licomes hurt þen 
þurh to strong fondunge sawle þrowunge Nichodemus brohte to smirien ure 
Laverd an hundret weies hit seiþ of mirre ant of aloes þet beoþ bittre 
speces ant bitacniþ bittre swinkes ant flesches pinsunges Hundret is ful tale ant 
noteþ perfectiun þet is ful dede forte schawin þet me schal ful do flesches 
pine ase forþ as eaver evene mei þolien I þe weie is bitacnet meosure ant wis
dom þet euch mon wiþ wisdom weie hwet he mahe don ne beo nawt se over
swiþe i gast þet he foryeme þe bodi ne eft se tendre of his flesch þet hit i
wurþe untohen ant makie þe gast þeowe Nu is al þis meast iseid of bitternesse 
utewiþ Of bitternesse inwiþ segge we nu sumhweat for of þes twa bitternesses 
awakeneþ swetnesse her yet i þis world nawt ane in heovene 
As ich seide riht nu þet Nichodemus brohte smirles to ure Laverd alswa þe 
þreo Maries bohten deorewurþe aromaz his bodi forte smirien Neomeþ nu 
gode yeme mine leove sustren þeos þreo Maries bitacniþ þreo bitternesses 
for þis nome Marie as Meraht ant Merariht þet ich spec þe ruppe of 
spealeþ bitternesse þe earste bitternesse is i sunne bireowsunge ant i deadbote 
hwen þe sunfule is iturnd earst to ure Laverd Ant þeos is understonden bi þe 
earste Marie Marie Magdaleine ant bi god rihte for ha wiþ muche bireowsunge 
ant bitternesse of heorte leafde hire sunnen ant turnde to ure Laverd Ah forþi 
þet sum mahte þurh to muche bitternesse fallen into unhope Magdaleine þe 
spealeþ tures hehnesse is to Marie ifeiet þurh hwet is bitacnet hope of heh 
mearci ant of heovene blisse þe oþer bitternesse is i wreastlunge ant i wragelunge 
ayeines fondunges Ant þeos is bitacnet bi þe oþer Marie Marie Jacobi for 
 Jacob spealeþ wreastlere þis wreastlunge is ful bitter to monie þe beoþ 
ful forþ i þe wei toward heovene for þeo yet i fondunges þet beoþ þe 
deofles swenges waggiþ oþerhwiles ant moten wreastlin ayein wiþ strong 
wraglunge For as Seint Austin seiþ 
Hwil eaver Israeles folc wes in Egypte under Pharones hond ne leadde he neaver 
ferd þe ron ah þa hit fleah from him þa wiþ al his strengþe wende he þe refter 
Forþi is eaver bitter feht neod ayein Pharaon þet is ayein þe deovel For ase 
seiþ Ezechiel Flih sunne ant 
sunne wule folhin eaver efter Inoh is iseid þe ruppe hwi þe gode nis neaver 
sker of alle fondunges Sone se he haveþ þe an overcumen ikepe anan anoþer 
þe þridde bitternesse is i longunge toward heovene ant i þe ennu of þis world 
hwen ei is se hehe þet he haveþ heorte reste onont unþeawes weorre ant is as in 
heovene yeten ant þuncheþ bitter alle worltliche þinges Ant tis þridde 
bitternesse is understonden bi Marie Salomee þe þridde Marie for Salome 
spealeþ pes Ant þeo yet þe habbeþ pes ant reste of cleane inwit habbeþ in 
hare heorte bitternesse of þis lif þet edhalt ham from blisse þet ham longeþ to 
from Godd þet ha luvieþ þus lo in euch stat rixleþ bitternesse earst i þe 
biginnunge hwen me sahtneþ wiþ Godd i þe forþyong of god lif ant i þe 
leaste ende Hwa is þenne o Godes half þe wilneþ i þis world eise oþer este 
Ah neomeþ nu yeme mine leove sustren hu efter bitternesse kimeþ swetnesse 
bitternesse buþ hit For as þet Godspel teleþ þeose þreo Maries bohten swote 
smeallinde aromaz to smirien ure Laverd þurh aromaz þe beoþ swote is 
understonden swotnesse of devot heorte þeos Maries hit buggeþ þet is 
þurh bitternesse me kimeþ to swotnesse Bi þis nome Marie nim eaver 
 bitternesse þurh Maries bone wes ed te neoces weater iwent to wine þet 
is to understonden þurh bone of bitternesse þet me dreheþ for Godd þe heorte 
þe wes weattri smechles ne ne felde na savur of Godd namare þen i weater 
schal beon iwent to wine þet is ifinden smech in him swete over alle wines 
Forþi seiþ þe wise þe þolemode þolie bitter ane hwile he schal sone þe refter habben 
yeld of blisse Ant Anna i Tobie seiþ bi ure Laverd 
þet is iblescet beo þu Laverd þe makest stille efter storm ant efter wopi 
weattres yeldest bliþe murhþes yef þu art ofhungret efter þet swete þu most earst witerliche biten o 
þe bittre Ich 
chulle ha seiþ Godes deore spuse gan to rechleses hul bi þe dun of myrre 
Lo hwuch is þe wei to rechleses swotnesse bi myrre of bitternesse Ant eft i þet 
ilke luveboc Aromaz me makeþ of myrre ant of rechles ah 
myrre he set bivoren ant rechles kimeþ efter 
Nu meaneþ hire sum þet ha ne mei habben na swotnesse of Godd ne swetnesse 
wiþinnen Ne wundri ha hire nawiht yef ha nis Marie for ha hit mot buggen 
wiþ bitternesse wiþuten nawt wiþ euch bitternesse for sum geaþ frommard 
Godd as euch worltlich sar þet nis for sawle heale Forþi i þe Godspel of þe 
þreo Maries is iwriten þisses weis þeos Maries hit seiþ þeose biternesses weren cuminde to 
smirien ure Laverd þeo beoþ cuminde to smirien ure Laverd þe me þoleþ 
for his luve þe strecheþ him toward us as þing þet ismired is ant makeþ him 
nesche ant softe to hondlin Ant nes he himseolf reclus i Maries wombe þeos 
twa þing limpeþ to ancre nearowþe ant bitternesse for wombe is nearow 
wununge þer ure Laverd wes reclus ant tis word Marie as ich ofte habbe i
seid spealeþ bitternesse Yef ye þenne i nearow stude þolieþ bitternesse ye 
beoþ his feolahes reclus as he wes i Marie wombe Beo ye ibunden inwiþ fowr 
large wahes ant he in a nearow cader ineilet o rode i stanene þruh bicluset 
hetefeste Marie wombe ant þis þruh weren his ancrehuses I nowþer nes he 
worltlich mon ah wes as ut of þe world forte schawin ancren þet ha ne schulen 
wiþ þe world na þing habben imeane Ye þu ondswerest me ah he wende 
ut of ba Ye went tu alswa of ba þine ancrehuses as he dude wiþute bruche 
ant leaf ham ba ihale þet schal beon hwen þe gast went ut on ende wiþuten 
bruche ant wem of his twa huses þet an is þe licome þet oþer is þe uttre hus 
þet is as þe uttre wah abute þe castel 
Al þet ich habbe iseid of flesches pinsunge nis nawt for ow mine leove sustren 
 þe oþerhwile þolieþ mare þen ich walde ah is for sum þet schal rede 
þis inohreaþe þe grapeþ hire to softe Noþeles yunge impen me bigurd 
wiþ þornes leste beastes freoten ham hwil ha beoþ mearewe Ye beoþ yunge 
impen iset i Godes orchard þornes beoþ þe heardschipes þet ich habbe ispeken 
of Ant ow is neod þet ye beon biset wiþ ham abuten þet te beast of helle hwen 
he snakereþ toward ow forte biten on ow hurte him o þe scharpschipe ant 
schunche ayeinwardes Wiþ alle þeose heardschipes beoþ gleade ant wel i
paiet yef lutel word is of ow yef ye beoþ unwurþe for þorn is scharp ant unwurþ 
Wiþ þeose twa beoþ bigurde Ye ne ahen nawt to unnen þet uvel word beo of 
ow Scandle is heavedsunne þet is þing swa iseid oþer idon þet me mei 
rihtliche turnen hit to uvele ant sunegin þe refter þerþurh wiþ misþoht wiþ 
uvel word on hire on oþre ant sungin ec wiþ dede Ah ye ahen unnen þet na 
word ne beo of ow na mare þen of deade ant beon bliþe iheortet yef ye þolieþ 
danger of Sluri þe cokes cneave þe wescheþ ant wipeþ disches i cuchene 
þenne beo ye dunes ihehet toward heovene For lo hu spekeþ þe leafdi i þet 
swete luveboc Mi 
leof kimeþ leapinde ha seiþ o þe dunes overleapinde hulles Dunes bitacneþ
þeo þe leadeþ hechhest lif hulles beoþ þe lachhere Nu seiþ ha þet hire leof
leapeþ o þe dunes þet is totret ham tofuleþ ham þoleþ þet me totreode
ham tuki ham al to wundre schaweþ in ham his ahne troden þet me trudde him
in ham ifinde hu he wes totreden as his trode schaweþ þis beoþ þe hehe
dunes as munt of Muntgiw dunes of Armenie þe hulles þe beoþ lahre þeo
 as þe leafdi seiþ hireseolf he overleapeþ ne trust nawt se wel on ham for
hare feblesce ne mahte nawt þolien swuch totreodunge ant he leapeþ over ham 
forbereþ ham ant forbuheþ aþet ha waxen herre from hulles to dunes His
schadewe lanhure overgeaþ ant wriþ ham hwil he leapeþ over ham þat is 
sum ilicnesse he leiþ on ham of his lif on eorþe as þah hit were his schadewe 
Ah þe dunes undervoþ þe troden of himseolven ant schaweþ in hare lif hwuch
his liflade wes hu ant hwer he eode i hwuch vilte i hwuch wa he leadde his lif
on eorþe þulliche dunes þe gode Pawel spek of ant eadmodliche seide 
 Alle wa 
quoþ he ant alle scheome we þolieþ ah þet is ure selhþe þet we beoren on 
ure bodi Jesu Cristes deadlicnesse þet hit suteli in us hwuch wes his lif on eorþe 
Godd hit wat þe þus doþ ha pruvieþ us hare luve toward ure Laverd Luvest 
tu me Cuþ hit For luve wule schawin him wiþ uttre werkes Ne beo neaver þing se heard soþ luve 
lihteþ hit ant softeþ ant sweteþ Hweat þolieþ 
men ant wummen for fals luve ant for ful luve ant mare walden þolien Ant 
hweat is mare wunder þet siker luve ant treowe ant over alle oþre swete ne 
mei meistrin us se forþ as deþ þe luve of sunne Nawt forþi ich wat swuch 
þet bereþ ba togederes hevi brunie ant here ibunden hearde wiþ irn middel 
þeh ant earmes mid brade þicke bondes swa þet tet swat þe rof is passiun to 
þolien Feasteþ wakeþ swinkeþ ant Crist hit wat meaneþ him þet hit ne 
greveþ him nawt ant bit me ofte teachen him sumhwet wiþ hwet he mahte his 
licome derven Al þet is bitter for ure Laverdes luve al him þuncheþ swete 
Deuleset yet he wepeþ to me as wivene sarest ant seiþ Godd foryet him 
forþi þet he ne sent him na muchel secnesse Godd hit wat þet makeþ luve 
For as he seiþ me ofte for na þing þet Godd mahte don uvele bi him þah he 
wiþ þe forlorene wurpe him into helle ne mahte he neaver him þuncheþ luvien 
him þe leasse Yef ei mon eani swuch þing ortrowi bi him he is mare mat þen 
þeof inume wiþ þeofþe Ich wat ec swuch wummon þet þoleþ lutel leasse 
ah nis þer bute þoncki Godd i strengþe þet he yeveþ ham ant icnawen 
eadmodliche ure wacnesse Luvie we hare god ant swa hit is ure ahne For as 
Sein Gregoire seiþ of swa muchel strengþe is luve þet hit makeþ oþres god 
wiþute swinc ure ahne as is iseid þe ruppe Nu me þuncheþ we beoþ icumen 
into þe seoveþe dale þet is al of luve þe makeþ schir heorte

<td align=left valign=top>
Seinte Pawel witneþ þet alle uttre heardschipes alle flesches pinsunges 
ant licomliche swinkes al is ase nawt ayeines luve þe schireþ ant 
brihteþ þe heorte þet is licomlich bisischipe is to lutel wurþ ah swote ant schir 
heorte is god to alle þinges þah ich cuþe he seiþ monne ledene ant englene þah ich dude o 
mi bodi alle pine ant passiun þet bodi mahte þolien þah ich yeve povre al þet 
ich hefde yef ich nefde luve þerwiþ to Godd ant to alle men in him ant for him 
al were ispillet For as þe hali abbat Moyses seide al þet wa ant al þet heard 
þet we þolieþ o flesch ant al þet god þet we eaver doþ alle swucche þinges 
ne beoþ nawt bute as lomen to tilie wiþ þe heorte Yef þe axe ne kurve ne 
spitelsteaf ne dulve ne þe sulh ne erede hwa kepte ham to halden Alswa as na 
mon ne luveþ lomen for hamseolf ah deþ for þe þinges þet me wurcheþ wiþ 
ham alswa na flesches derf nis to luvien bute forþi þet Godd te reaþere þider
ward loki mid his grace ant makie þe heorte schir ant of briht sihþe þet nan ne 
mei habben wiþ monglunge of unþeawes ne wiþ eorþlich luve of worltliche 
þinges For þis mong woreþ swa þe ehnen of þe heorte þet ha ne mei cnawen 
Godd ne gleadien of his sihþe Schir heorte as Seint Bernard seiþ makieþ twa 
þinges þet tu al þet tu dest do hit oþer for luve ane of Godd oþer for oþres 
god ant for his biheve Have in al þet tu dest an of þes twa ententes oþer ba 
togederes for þe leatere falleþ into þe earre Have eaver schir heorte þus ant 
do al þet tu wult have wori heorte al þe sit uvele Forþi mine 
leove sustren over alle þing beoþ bisie to habben schir heorte Hwet is schir 
heorte Ich hit habbe iseid ear þet is þet ye na þing ne wilnin ne ne luvien 
bute Godd ane ant te ilke þinges for Godd þe helpeþ ow toward him for 
Godd ich segge luvien ham ant nawt for hamseolven as is mete oþer claþ 
mon oþer wummon þe ye beoþ of igodet For ase seiþ Seint Austin ant spekeþ 
þus to ure Laverd þet is Laverd leasse ha luvieþ þe þe luvieþ eawt bute þe bute ha 
luvien hit for þe Schirnesse of heorte is Godes luve ane I þis is al þe strengþe 
of alle religiuns þe ende of alle ordres Luve fulleþ 
þe lahe seiþ Seinte Pawel 
 Alle Godes heastes as Sein Gregoire seiþ beoþ i luve irotet Luve ane 
schal beon ileid i Seinte Mihales weie þeo þe meast luvieþ schulen beo meast 
iblisset nawt þeo þe leadeþ heardest lif for luve hit overweieþ Luve is heovene 
stiward for hire muchele freolec for heo ne edhalt na þing ah yeveþ al þet ha 
haveþ ant ec hireseolven elles ne kepte Godd nawt of þet hiren were 
Godd haveþ ofgan ure luve on alle cunne wise He haveþ muchel idon us ant 
mare bihaten Muchel yeove ofdraheþ luve Me al þe world he yef us in Adam 
ure alde feader ant al þet is i þe world he weorp under ure fet beastes ant fuheles 
ear we weren forgulte Ant yet al þet is as is þe ruppe iseid serveþ þe 
gode to sawle biheve yet te uvele serviþ eorþe sea ant sunne He dude yet 
mare yef us nawt ane of his ah dude al himseolven Se heh yeove nes neaver i
yeven to se lahe wrecches Crist seiþ Seinte Pawel luvede swa his leofmon þet he yef 
for hire þe pris of himseolven Neomeþ nu gode yeme mine leove sustren for
hwi me ah him to luvien Earst as a mon þe woheþ as a king þet luvede a gentil 
povre leafdi of feorrene londe he sende his sonden bivoren þet weren þe 
patriarches ant te prophetes of þe alde testament wiþ leattres isealet On ende he 
com himseolven ant brohte þe Godspel as leattres iopenet ant wrat wiþ his 
ahne blod saluz to his leofmon luvegretunge forte wohin hire wiþ ant hire 
luve wealden Herto falleþ a tale a wrihe forbisne 
A leafdi wes mid hire fan biset al abuten hire lond al destruet ant heo al povre 
inwiþ an eorþene castel A mihti kinges luve wes þah biturnd upon hire swa 
unimete swiþe þet he for wohlech sende hire his sonden an efter oþer ofte 
somet monie sende hire beawbelez baþe feole ant feire sucurs of liveneþ help 
of his hehe hird to halden hire castel Heo underfeng al as on unrecheles ant swa 
wes heard iheortet þet hire luve ne mahte he neaver beo þe neorre Hwet wult 
tu mare He com himseolf on ende schawde hire his feire neb as þe þe wes of 
alle men feherest to bihalden spec se swiþe swoteliche ant wordes se murie 
þet ha mahten deade arearen to live wrahte feole wundres ant dude muchele 
meistries bivoren hire ehsihþe schawde hire his mihte talde hire of his kinedom 
bead to makien hire cwen of al þet he ahte Al þis ne heold nawt nes þis 
hoker wunder For heo nes neaver wurþe forte beon his þuften ah swa þurh 
his deboneirte luve hefde overcumen him þet he seide on ende Dame þu art i
weorret ant þine van beoþ se stronge þet tu ne maht nanesweis wiþute mi 
sucurs edfleon hare honden þet ha ne don þe to scheome deaþ efter al þi weane 
Ich chulle for þe luve of þe neome þet feht upo me ant arudde þe of ham þe þi 
deaþ secheþ Ich wat þah to soþe þet ich schal bituhen ham neomen deaþes 
wunde ant ich hit wulle heorteliche forte ofgan þin heorte Nu þenne biseche 
ich þe for þe luve þet ich cuþe þe þet tu luvie me lanhure efter þe ilke dede 
dead hwen þu naldest lives þes king dude al þus arudde hire of alle hire van 
ant wes himseolf to wundre ituket ant islein on ende þurh miracle aras þah 
from deaþe to live Nere þeos ilke leafdi of uveles cunnes cunde yef ha over alle 
þing ne luvede him herefter 
þes king is Jesu Godes sune þet al o þisse wise wohede ure sawle þe deoflen 
hefden biset Ant he as noble wohere efter monie messagers ant feole goddeden 
com to pruvien his luve ant schawde þurh cnihtschipe þet he wes luvewurþe as 
weren sumhwile cnihtes iwunet to donne dude him i turneiment ant hefde for 
his leoves luve his scheld i feht as kene cniht on euche half iþurlet His scheld 
þe wreah his Goddhead wes his leove licome þet wes ispread o rode brad as 
scheld buven in his istrahte earmes nearow bineoþen as þe an fot efter mon
ies wene set upo þe oþer þet þis scheld naveþ siden is for bitacnunge þet 
his deciples þe schulden stonden bi him ant habben ibeon his siden fluhen alle 
from him ant leafden him as fremede as þe Godspel seiþ þis scheld is iyeven us ayein alle temptatiuns as Jeremie witneþ Nawt ane þis scheld ne schilt us from alle 
uveles ah deþ yet mare cruneþ us in heovene Laverd 
he seiþ Daviþ wiþ þe scheld of þi gode wil þu havest us icrunet Scheld 
he seiþ of god wil for willes he þolede al þet he þolede 
 Me Laverd þu seist hwerto ne mahte he wiþ leasse gref habben arud 
us Yeoi iwiss ful lihtliche ah he nalde Forhwi Forte bineomen us euch 
bitellunge ayein him of ure luve þet he se deore bohte Me buþ lihtliche þing 
þet me luveþ lutel He bohte us wiþ his heorte blod deorre pris nes neaver 
forte ofdrahen of us ure luve toward him þet costnede him se sare I scheld 
beoþ þreo þinges þe treo ant te leþer ant te litunge Alswa wes i þis scheld 
þe treo of þe rode þet leþer of Godes licome þe litunge of þe reade blod þet 
heowede hire se feire Eft þe þridde reisun efter kene cnihtes deaþ me hongeþ 
hehe i chirche his scheld on his mungunge Alswa is þis scheld þet is þe 
crucifix i chirche iset i swuch stude þer me hit sonest seo forte þenchen 
þerbi o Jesu Cristes cnihtschipe þet he dude o rode His leofmon bihalde þe ron 
hu he bohte hire luve lette þurlin his scheld openin his side to schawin hire his 
heorte to schawin hire openliche hu inwardliche he luvede hire ant to ofdrahen 
hire heorte 
Fowr heaved luven me ifind i þis world bitweone gode iferen bitweone mon 
ant wummon bitweone wif ant hire child bitweone licome ant sawle þe luve 
þet Jesu Crist haveþ to his deore leofmon overgeaþ þeos fowre passeþ ham 
alle Ne teleþ me him god fere þe leiþ his wed i Giwerie to acwitin ut his fere 
Godd almihti leide himseolf for us i Giwerie ant dude his deorewurþe bodi to 
acwitin ut his leofmon of Giwene honden Neaver fere ne dude swuch fordede for 
his fere 
Muche luve is ofte bitweone mon ant wummon ah þah ha were iweddet him 
ha mahte iwurþen se unwreast ant swa longe ha mahte forhorin hire wiþ oþre 
men þet þah ha walde ayein cumen he ne kepte hire nawt Forþi Crist luveþ 
mare for þah þe sawle his spuse forhori hire wiþ þe feond under heavedsunne 
feole yeres ant dahes his mearci is hire eaver yarow hwen ha wule cumen ham ant 
leten þen deovel Al þis he seiþ himseolf þurh Jeremie Yet he yeiyeþ al dei þu þet havest se 
unwreaste idon biturn þe ant cum ayein welcume schalt tu beo me Yet he eorneþ hit seiþ ayein hire yeincume ant 
warpeþ earmes anan abuten hire swire Hweat is mare milce Yet her gleadfulre 
wunder ne beo neaver his leof forhoret mid se monie deadliche sunnen sone se 
ha kimeþ to him ayein he makeþ hire neowe meiden For as Seint Austin seiþ 
swa muchel is bitweonen Godes neoleachunge ant monnes to wummon þet monnes 
neoleachunge makeþ of meiden wif ant Godd makeþ of wif meiden Gode werkes ant treowe bileave þeose twa þinges 
beoþ meiþhad i sawle 
Nu of þe þridde luve Child þet hefde swuch uvel þet him bihofde beaþ of 
blod ear hit were ihealet muchel þe moder luvede hit þe walde þis beaþ him 
makien þis dude ure Laverd us þe weren se seke of sunne ant swa isulet þer
wiþ þet na þing ne mahte healen us ne cleansin us bute his blod ane for swa he 
hit walde His luve makeþ us beaþ þe rof Iblescet beo he eavre þreo beaþes 
he greiþede to his deore leofmon forte weschen hire in ham se hwit ant se feier 
þet ha were wurþe to his cleane cluppunges þe earste beaþ is fulluht þe 
oþer beoþ teares inre oþer uttre efter þe forme beaþ yef ha hire suleþ þe 
þridde is Jesu Cristes blod þet halheþ ba þe oþre as Sein Juhan seiþ i þe 
Apocalipse þet he luveþ us mare 
þen eani moder hire child he hit seiþ himseolven þurh Ysaie 
 Mei moder he seiþ foryeoten hire child Ant þah heo do ich ne mei þe 
foryeoten neaver ant seiþ þe resun efter Ich 
habbe he seiþ depeint te i mine honden swa he dude mid read blod upo 
þe rode Me cnut his gurdel to habben þoht of a þing ah ure Laverd for he 
nalde neaver foryeoten us dude mearke of þurlunge in ure munegunge i ba twa 
his honden 
Nu þe feorþe luve þe sawle luveþ þe licome swiþe mid alle ant þet is 
etscene i þe twinnunge for leove freond beoþ sari hwen ha schulen twinnin 
ah ure Laverd willeliche totweamde his sawle from his bodi forte veien ure baþe 
togederes world buten ende i þe blisse of heovene þus lo Jesu Cristes luve 
toward his deore spuse þet is Hali Chirche oþer cleane sawle passeþ alle 
ant overkimeþ þe fowr measte luven þet me ifind on eorþe Wiþ al þis luve 
yetten he woheþ hire o þis wise 
 þi luve he seiþ oþer hit is forte yeoven allunge oþer hit is to sullen 
oþer hit is to reavin ant to neomen wiþ strengþe Yef hit is forte yeoven hwer 
maht tu biteon hit betere þen upo me Nam ich þinge feherest Nam ich kinge 
richest Nam ich hest icunnet Nam ich weolie wisest Nam ich monne hendest 
Nam ich þinge freoest For swa me seiþ bi large mon þe ne con nawt edhalden 
þet he haveþ þe honden as mine beoþ iþurlet Nam ich alre þinge swotest 
ant swetest þus alle þe reisuns hwi me ah to yeove luve þu maht ifinden in 
me nomeliche yef þu luvest chaste cleannesse For nan ne mei luvie me bute ha 
hire halde Ah ha is þreovald i widewehad i spushad i meidenhad þe heste 
Yef þi luve nis nawt to yeovene ah wult þet me bugge hire buggen hire 
Hu  Oþer wiþ oþer luve oþer wiþ sumhweat elles Me suleþ wel luve for 
luve ant swa me ah to sulle luve ant for na þing elles Yef þin is swa to sullen 
ich habbe iboht hire wiþ luve over alle oþre For of þe fowr measte luven ich 
habbe icud toward te þe measte of ham alle Yef þu seist þu nult nawt leote 
þ ron se liht chap ah wult yette mare nempne hweat hit schule beon Sete feor o 
þi luve þu ne schalt seggen se muchel þet ich nule yeove mare Wult tu castles 
kinedomes Wult tu wealden al þe world Ich chulle do þe betere makie þe 
wiþ al þis cwen of heoveriche þu schalt teseolf beo seovevald brihtre þen 
þe sunne Nan uvel ne schal nahhi þe Na wunne ne schal wonti þe Al þi wil 
schal beon iwraht in heovene ant ec in eorþe ye ant yet in helle Ne schal 
neaver heorte þenchen hwuch selhþe þet ich nule yeoven for þi luve unmeteliche 
unevenliche unendeliche mare Al Creasuse weole þe wes kinge richest 
Absalones schene wlite þe as ofte as me evesede him salde his evesunge þe her 
þet he kearf of for twa hundret sicles of seolver iweiet Asaeles swiftschipe þe 
straf wiþ heortes of urn Samsones strengþe þe sloh a þusent of his fan al ed a 
time ant ane bute fere Cesares freolec Alixandres hereword Moysese heale 
Nalde a mon for an of þeos yeoven al þet he ahte Ant alle somet ayein mi bodi 
ne beoþ nawt wurþ a nelde Yef þu art se swiþe anewil ant swa ut of þi wit 
þet tu þurh nawt to leosen forsakest swuch biyete wiþ alles cunnes selhþe lo 
ich halde her heatel sweord upo þin heaved to dealen lif ant sawle ant bisenchen 
ham ba into þe fur of helle to beon deofles hore schentfulliche ant sorhfulliche 
world abuten ende Ondswere nu ant were þe yef þu const ayein me oþer yette 
me þi luve þe ich yirne se swiþe nawt for min ah for þin ahne muchele 
biheve 
Lo þus ure Laverd woheþ Nis ha to heard iheortet þet a þulli wohere ne 
mei to his luve turnen yef ha wel þencheþ þeose þreo þinges hwet he is ant 
hwet heo is ant hu muchel is þe luve of se heh as he is toward se lah as heo is 
Forþi seiþ þe Salmwruhte Nis nan 
þet mahe edlutien þet ha ne mot him luvien þe soþe sunne i þe undertid wes 
forþi istihen on heh o þe hehe rode forte spreaden overal hate luvegleames 
þus neodful he wes ant is aþet tes dei to ontenden his luve i his leoves heorte 
ant seiþ i þe Godspel 
 Ich com to bringen he seiþ fur into eorþe þet is bearninde luve into 
eorþlich heorte ant hwet yirne ich elles bute þet hit bleasie Wlech luve is 
him laþ as he seiþ þurh Sein Juhan i þe Apocalipse Ich walde he 
seiþ to his leofmon þet tu were i mi luve oþer allunge cald oþer hat mid alle 
ah forþi þet tu art ase wlech bitweone twa nowþer hat ne cald þu makest me 
to wleatien ant ich wulle speowe þe ut bute þu wurþe hattre 
Nu ye habbeþ iherd mine leove sustren hu ant forhwi Godd is swiþe to 
luvien Forte ontenden ow wel gederiþ wude þerto wiþ þe povre wummon of 
Sarepte þe burh þe spealeþ ontendunge Laverd quoþ ha to Helye þe hali prophete lo ich gederi twa treon 
þeos twa treon bitacniþ þet a treo þet stod upriht ant þet oþer þe eode 
þwertover o þe deore rode Of þeos twa treon ye schulen ontende fur of 
luve inwiþ ower heorte Biseoþ ofte towart ham þencheþ yef ye ne ahen 
eaþe to luvien þe king of blisse þe tospreat swa his earmes toward ow ant 
buheþ as to beoden cos duneward his heaved Sikerliche ich segge hit yef þe 
soþe Helye þet is Godd almihti ifint ow þeose twa treon bisiliche gederin 
he wule gestnin wiþ ow ant monifalden in ow his deorewurþe grace as Helie 
dude hire liveneþ ant gestnede wiþ hire þet he ifond þe twa treon gederin i 
Sarepte 
Grickisch fur is imaket of reades monnes blod ant þet ne mei na þing bute 
migge ant sond ant eisil as me seiþ acwenchen þis Grickisch fur is þe 
luve of Jesu ure Laverd ant ye hit schule makien of reade monnes blod þet is 
Jesu Crist ireadet wiþ his ahne blod o þe deore rode ant wes inread cundeliche 
alswa as me weneþ þis blod for ow isched upo þe earre twa treon schal 
makien ow Sareptiens þet is ontende mid tis Grickisch fur þet as Salomon 
seiþ nane weattres þet beoþ worldliche tribulatiuns nane temptatiuns nowþer 
inre ne uttre ne mahen þis luve acwenchen Nu nis þenne on ende bute witen 
ow warliche wiþ al þet hit acwencheþ þet beoþ migge ant sond ant eisil as 
ich ear seide Migge is stench of sunne O sond ne groweþ na god ant bitacneþ 
idel Idel akeldeþ ant acwencheþ þis fur Sturieþ ow cwicliche aa i gode werkes 
ant þet schal heaten ow ant ontenden þis fur ayein þe brune of sunne For alswa 
as þe an neil driveþ ut þen oþer alswa þe brune of Godes luve driveþ brune of 
ful luve ut of þe heorte þe þridde þing is eisil þet is sur heorte of niþ 
oþer of onde Understondeþ þis word þa þe niþfule Giws offreden ure Laverd 
þis sure present upo þe rode þa seide he þet reowþfule word Neaver quoþ he ear nu nes ich ful pinet nawt þurh þet eisil ah þurh 
hare ondfule niþ þet tet eisil bitacnede þet heo him duden drinken ant is ilich 
as þah a mon þet hefde longe iswunken ant failede efter long swinc on ende of 
his hure Alswa ure Laverd mare þen twa ant þritti yer tilede efter hare luve ant 
for al his sare swinc ne wilnede na þing bute luve to hure Ah i þe ende of his lif 
þet wes as i þe eventid hwen me yelt wercmen hare deies hure loke hu ha 
yulden him for piment of huni luve eisil of sur niþ ant galle of bitter onde O 
quoþ ure Laverd þa Al mi swinc on eorþe al mi pine o 
rode ne sweameþ ne ne derveþ me nawiht ayein þis þet ich þus biteo al þet 
ich idon habbe þis eisil þet ye beodeþ me þis sure hure þurhfulleþ mi pine 
þis eisil of sur heorte ant of bitter þonc over alle oþre þing acwencheþ Grickisch 
fur þet is þe luve of ure Laverd ant hwase hit bereþ i breoste toward 
wummon oþer mon ha is Giwes make Ha offreþ Godd þis eisil ant þurhfulleþ 
onont hire Jesues pine o rode Me warpeþ Grickisch fur upon his famen ant swa 
me overkimeþ ham Ye schule don alswa hwen Godd areareþ ow of ei va eani 
weorre Hu ye hit schule warpen Salomon teacheþ þet is yef þi fa hungreþ fed him To his þurst yef him 
drunch þet is to understonden yef he efter þin hearm haveþ hunger oþer 
þurst yef him fode of þine beoden þet Godd do him are Yef him drunch of 
teares Wep for his sunnen þus þu schalt seiþ Salomon rukelin on his 
heaved bearninde gleden þet is to seggen þus þu schalt ontenden his heorte 
forte luvie þe For heorte is in Hali Writ bi heaved understonden O þulli wise 
wule Godd seggen ed te dome Hwi luvedest tu þe mon oþer þe wummon 
 Sire ha luveden me Ye he wule seggen þu yulde þet tu ahtest Her nabbe 
ich þe nawt muches to yelden Yef þu maht ondswerien alle wa ha duden me 
ne na luve ne ahte ich ham ah sire ich luvede ham for þi luve þet luve he ah 
þe for hit wes iyeven him ant he hit wule þe yelden 
Migge as ich seide þet acwencheþ Grickisch fur is stinkinde flesches 
luve þe acwencheþ gastelich luve þet Grickisch fur bitacneþ Hweat flesch 
wes on eorþe se swete ant se hali as wes Jesu Cristes flesch Ant þah he seide 
himseolf to his deore deciples 
þet is Bute ich parti from ow þe Hali Gast þet is min ant mines feaderes 
luve ne mei nawt cumen to ow Ah hwen ich beo from ow ich chulle senden 
him ow Hwen Jesu Cristes ahne deciples hwil þet ha fleschliche luveden him 
neh ham foreoden þe swetnesse of þe Hali Gast ne ne mahte nawt habben baþe 
togederes Demeþ owseolven nis he wod oþer heo þe luveþ to swiþe hire 
ahne flesch oþer eani mon fleschliche swa þet ha yirne to swiþe his sihþe oþer 
his speche Ne þunche hire neaver wunder yef hire wonti þe Hali Gastes frovre 
Cheose nu euchan of þes twa eorþlich elne ant heovenlich to hweþer ha 
wule halden for þet oþer ha mot leten For i þe tweire monglunge ne mei ha 
habben neaver mare schirnesse of heorte þet is as we seiden ear þet god ant 
te strengþe of alle religiuns ant in euch ordre Luve makeþ hire schir griþful ant 
cleane Luve haveþ a meistrie bivoren alle oþre for al þet ha rineþ al ha turneþ 
to hire ant makeþ al hire ahne Deore walde moni mon buggen a swuch þing 
þet al þet he rine to al were his ahne Ant ne seide hit þe ruppe feor ane þurh 
þet tu luvest þet god þet is in anoþer wiþ þe rinunge of þi luve þu makest 
wiþuten oþer swinc his god þin ahne god as Sein Gregoire witneþ Lokiþ nu 
hu muchel god þe ontfule leoseþ Streche þi luve to Jesu Crist þu havest him i
wunnen Rin him wiþ ase muche luve as þu havest sum mon sumchearre he is 
þin to don wiþ al þet tu wilnest Ah hwa luveþ þing þet leaveþ hit for leasse 
þen hit is wurþ Nis Godd betere unevenlich þen al þet is i þe world Chearite 
is cherte of leof þing ant of deore Undeore he makeþ Godd ant to unwurþ mid 
alle þet for ei worltlich þing of his luve leaskeþ for na þing ne con luvien riht 
bute he ane Swa overswiþe he luveþ luve þet he makeþ hire his evening Yet 
ich dear segge mare he makeþ hire his meistre ant deþ al þet ha hat as þah he 
moste nede Mei ich pruvien þis Ye witerliche ich bi his ahne wordes for þus 
he spekeþ to Moyses þe monne meast him luvede Ich hefde quoþ he imunt to wreoke mine 
wreaþþe i þis folc Ah þu seist I ne schal nawt þi word beo iforþet Me 
seiþ þet luve bindeþ witerliche luve bint swa ure Laverd þet he ne mei na þing 
don bute þurh luves leave Nu preove herof for hit þuncheþ wunder Laverd þu wult smiten seiþ 
Ysaie Weilawei þu maht wel nis nan þet te halde as þah he seide yef 
ei luvede þe riht he mahte halden þe ant wearnen þe to smiten þet is þa ure Laverd walde bisenchen Sodome þer Lot his freond wes 
inne hihe þe quoþ he utward For hwil þu art bimong ham ne mei ich 
nawt don ham Nes þes wiþ luve ibunden Hwet wult tu mare Luve is his 
chamberleng his conseiler his spuse þet he ne mei nawt heole wiþ ah teleþ al 
þet he þencheþ 
 Mei ich quoþ ure Laverd heolen Abraham þing þet ich þenche to donne 
Nai o nane wise Nu con þes luvien þe þus spekeþ ant þus deþ to alle þe 
him inwardliche leveþ ant luvieþ þe blisse þet he yarkeþ ham as ha is 
unevenlich to alle worldes blissen alswa ha is untalelich to worldliche tungen Ye habbeþ of þeos 
blissen iwriten elleshwer mine leove sustren þis luve is þe riwle þe riwleþ 
þe heorte þis is þe leafdi 
riwle alle þe oþre serviþ hire Ant ane for hire sake me hat ham to luvien 
Lutel strengþe ich do of ham forhwon þet þeos beo deorewurþliche ihalden 
Habbeþ ham þah scheortliche i þe eahtuþe dale
