Bivoren on earst ich seide þet ye ne schulden nawiht as i vu bihaten for
te halden nan of þe uttre riwlen þet ilke ich segge yetten ne nane ne 
write ich ham buten ow ane Ich segge þis forþi þet oþre ancren ne 
seggen nawt þet ich þurh mi meistrie makie ham neowe riwle Ne bidde ich nawt 
þet ha halden ham Ah ye yet moten changin hwense ye eaver wulleþ þeose for 
betere Ayein þinges þe beoþ bivoren of ham is lutel strengþe 
Of sihþe ant of speche ant of þe oþre wittes is inoh iseid Nu is þis leaste 
dale as ich bihet on earst todealet ant isundret o lutle seove stucchen 
Me let leasse of þe þing þet me haveþ ofte Forþi ne schule ye beon bute 
as ure breþren beoþ ihuslet inwiþ tweolfmoneþ fiftene siþen i Mid
winter Dei ii Tweofte Dei iii Condelmeasse Dei iiii a Sunnedei midwei 
bitweonen þet ant Easter oþer Ure Leafdi Dei yef he is neh þe Sunnedei for 
þe hehnesse v Easter Dei vi þe þridde Sunnedei þe refter vii Hali þursdei 
 viii Witsunne Dei ix Midsumer Dei x Seinte Marie Dei Magdaleine xi 
þe Assumptiun xii þe Nativite xiii Seinte Mihales Dei xiii Alle Halhene 
Dei xv Seint Andrews Dei Ayein alle þeose beoþ cleanliche ischrivene ant 
neomeþ disceplines neaver þah of namon bute of owseolven ant forgaþ an 
dei ower pitance Yef ewt ilimpeþ misliche þet ye ne beon nawt ihuslet i þeose 
sette tearmes beoþ hit þe neste Sunnedei oþer yef þe oþer terme is neh 
abideþ aþet tenne 
Ye schulen eoten from Easter aþet te Hali Rode Dei þe leatere þe is in 
hervest euche dei twien bute þe Fridahes oþer Umbridayes Yongdayes 
vigilies I þeose dayes ne i þe Advent ne schule ye nawt eoten hwit bute neode 
hit makie þe oþer half yer feasten al bute Sunnedahes ane hwen ye beoþ in 
heale ant i ful strengþe ah riwle ne tweast nawt seke ne blodletene 
Ye ne schulen nawt eoten flesch ne seim bute for muche secnesse oþer hwa
se is overfeble Potage eoteþ bliþeliche ant wunieþ ow to lutel drunch No
þeles leove sustren ower mete ant ower drunch haveþ iþuht me ofte leasse 
þen ich walde Ne feaste ye na dei to bread ne to weattre bute ye habben leave 
Sum ancre makeþ hire bord wiþ hire gest utewiþ þet is to muche 
freondschipe for of alle ordres þenne is hit uncundelukest ant meast ayein ancre 
ordre þe is al dead to þe world Me haveþ iherd ofte þet deade speken wiþ 
cwike ah þet ha eten wiþ cwike ne fond ich yet neaver 
Ne makie ye nane gestnunges ne ne tulle ye to þe yete nane uncuþe hearloz 
þah þer nere nw uvel bute hare meadlese nurþ hit walde letten oþerhwile 
heovenliche þohtes Ne limpeþ nawt to ancre of oþer monnes ealmesse to makien 
hire large Nalde me lahhen a beggere lude to bismere þe leaþede men to feaste 
Marie ant Marþe ba weren sustren ah hare lif sundrede ye ancren beoþ inumen 
ow to Marie dale þe ure Laverd seolf herede 
 Marþe Marþe quoþ he þu art in muche baret Marie haveþ icore bet 
ant ne schal hire na þing reavin hire dale Husewifschipe is Marþe dale Marie 
dale is stilnesse ant reste of alle worldes noise þet na þing ne lette hire to heren 
Godes stevene Ant lokiþ hwet Godd seiþ þet na þing ne schal ow reavin þis 
dale Marþe haveþ hire meoster leoteþ hire iwurþen Ye sitten wiþ Marie 
stanstille ed Godes fet ant hercniþ him ane Marþe meoster is to feden povre ant 
schruden as husleafdi Marie ne ah nawt to entremeatin þe rof Yef ei blameþ 
hire Godd seolf ihwer wereþ hire as Hali Writ witneþ On oþer half nan ancre ne ah to neomen bute meaþfulliche þet hire to 
neodeþ Hwerof þenne mei ha makien hire large Ha schal libben bi ealmesse 
ase meaþfulliche as ha eaver mei ant nawt gederin forte yeoven Ha nis nawt 
husewif ah is a chirchancre Yef ha mei spearien eani povre schraden sende 
ham al dearnliche ut of hire wanes Under semblant of god is ofte ihulet sunne 
Ant hu schulen þeose riche ancres þe tilieþ oþer habbeþ rentes isette don to 
povre nehburs dearnliche hare ealmesse Ne wilni ha nawt to habbe word of a 
large ancre ne forte yeoven muchel ne beo nan þe grediure forte habben 
mare Forhwon þet gredinesse beo rote of þet gederunge of hire bitternesse al 
beoþ þe bohes bittre þe of hire spruteþ Bidden hit forte yeoven hit nis nawt 
ancre rihte Of ancre curteisie of ancre largesce is icumen ofte sunne ant scheome 
on ende 
Wummen ant children ant nomeliche ancre meidnes þe cumeþ iswenchet for 
ow þah ye spearien hit on ow oþer borhin oþer bidden hit makieþ ham to 
eotene wiþ chearitable chere ant leaþieþ to herbarhin 
Na mon ne eote bivoren ow bute bi ower meistres leave general oþer spetial 
general as of freres preachurs ant meonurs spetial of alle oþre Ne leaþie ye 
nane oþre to eoten ne to drinken bute alswa þurh his leave Liht is me seiþ 
leave Nawiht ne yirne ich þet me for swucche boden telle ow hende ancren I
hwear þah ant eaver yemeþ ow þet nan from ow þurh ower untuhtle ne parti 
wiþ scandle 
Ed gode men neomeþ al þet ow to nedeþ Ah þet lokiþ ow wel þet ye ne 
kecchen þe nome of gederinde ancren Of mon þet ye misleveþ þurh his fol 
semblant oþer bi his wake wordes nowþer ne neome ye ne leasse ne mare Neode 
schal driven ow forte bidden ei þing þah eadmodliche schawiþ to gode men 
ant wummen ower meoseise 
Ye mine leove sustren bute yef neod ow drive ant ower meistre hit reade ne 
schulen habbe na beast bute cat ane Ancre þe haveþ ahte þuncheþ bet huse
wif ase Marþe wes ne lihtliche ne mei ha nawt beo Marie Marþe suster wiþ 
griþfullnesse of heorte For þenne mot ha þenchen of þe kues foddre of heorde
monne hure olhnin þe heiward wearien hwen he punt hire ant yelden þah þe 
hearmes Ladlich þing is hit wat Crist hwen me makeþ i tune man of ancre 
ahte Nu þenne yef eani mot nedlunge habben hit loki þet hit namon ne eili ne ne 
hearmi ne þet hire þoht ne beo nawiht þe ron ifestnet Ancre ne ah to habben 
na þing þet utward drahe hire heorte 
Na chaffere ne drive ye Ancre þet is chepilt þet is buþ forte sullen efter 
biyete ha chepeþ hire sawle þe chapmon of helle þing þah þet ha wurcheþ 
ha mei þurh hire meistres read for hire neode sullen Hali men sumhwile liveden 
bi hare honden 
Nawt deore dehtren ne wite ye in ower hus of oþer monne þinges ne ahte ne 
claþes ne boistes ne chartres scoren ne cyrograffes ne þe chirch vestemenz 
ne þe calices bute neode oþer strengþe hit makie oþer muchel eie Of swuch 
witunge is muchel uvel ilumpen ofte siþen 
Inwiþ ower wanes ne leote ye namon slepen Yef muchel neod mid alle makeþ 
breoken ower hus hwil hit eaver is ibroken habbeþ þe rinne wiþ ow a wummon 
of cleane lif deies ant nihtes 
Forþi þet wepmen ne seoþ ow ne ye ham wel mei don of ower claþ beo hit 
hwit beo hit blac bute hit beo unorne warm ant wel iwraht felles wel itawet 
ant habbeþ ase monie as ow to neodeþ to bedde ant to rugge 
Nest flesch ne schal nan werien linnene claþ bute hit beo of hearde ant of 
greate heorden Stamin habbe hwase wule hwase wule beo buten 
Ye schulen in an hetter ant igurd liggen swa leoþeliche þah þet ye mahen 
honden putten þerunder Nest lich nan ne gurde hire wiþ na cunne gurdles bute 
þurh schriftes leave ne beore nan irn ne here ne ilespiles felles ne ne beate hire 
þerwiþ ne wiþ scurge ileadet wiþ holin ne wiþ breres ne biblodgi hire
seolf wiþute schriftes leave nohwer ne binetli hire ne ne beate bivoren ne na 
keorvunge ne keorve ne ne neome ed eanes to luþere disceplines temptatiuns 
forte acwenchen Ne for na bote ayein cundeliche secnesses nan uncundelich 
lechecreft ne leve ye ne ne fondin wiþuten ower meistres read leste ow stonde 
wurse 
Ower schon i winter beon meoke greate ant warme I sumer ye habbeþ leave 
bearvot gan ant sitten ant lihte scheos werien 
Hosen wiþute vampez ligge in hwase likeþ Ischeoed ne slepe ye nawt ne 
nohwer bute i bedde Sum wummon inohreaþe wereþ þe brech of here ful wel 
icnottet þe streapeles dun to þe vet ilacet ful feaste ah eaver is best þe swete 
ant te swote heorte me is leovere þet ye þolien wel an heard word þen an 
heard here 
Yef ye muhen beo wimpelles ant ye wel wullen beoþ bi warme cappen ant 
þeruppon hwite oþer blake veiles Ancren summe sungiþ in hare wimplunge 
na leasse þen leafdis Ah þah seiþ sum þet hit limpeþ to euch wummon 
cundeliche forte werien wimpel Nai Wimpel ne heavedclaþ nowþer ne 
nempneþ Hali Writ ah wriheles ane 
 Wummon seiþ þe Apostle schal wreon hire heaved Wrihen he seiþ 
nawt wimplin Wrihen ha schal hire scheome as Eve sunfule dohter i mungunge 
of þe sunne þet schende us on earst alle ant nawt drahe þe wriheles to tiffunge 
ant to prude Eft wule þe Apostle þet wummon wreo i chirche hire neb yetten 
leste uvel þoht arise þurh hire onsihþe Hwi þenne 
þu chirchancre iwimplet openest þi neb to wepmonnes ehe Toyeines þe 
þe sist men spekeþ þe Apostle yef þu þe ne hudest Ah yef þet ei þing wriheþ 
þi neb from monnes ehe beo hit wah beo hit claþ i wel itund windowe wel mei 
duhen ancre of oþer wimplunge Toyeines þe þe þus ne dest spekeþ þe Apostle 
nawt toyeines oþre þet hare ahne wah wriheþ wiþ euch monnes sihþe þer 
awakeniþ ofte wake þohtes of ant werkes oþerhwiles Hwase wule beon i
sehen þah ha atiffi hire nis nawt muche wunder Ah to Godes ehnen ha is lufsumre 
þe is for þe luve of him untiffet wiþuten 
Ring ne broche ne habbe ye ne gurdel imembret ne gloven ne nan swuch 
þing þet ow ne deh to habben A meoke surpliz ye mahen in hat sumer werien 
Eaver me is leovere se ye doþ greattre werkes 
Ne makie ye nane purses forte freondin ow wiþ bute to þeo þet ower meistre 
yeveþ ow his leave ne huve ne blodbinde of seolc ne laz buten leave Ah 
schapieþ ant seowiþ ant mendiþ chirche claþes ant povre monne hettren Na 
swuch þing ne schule ye yeoven wiþuten schriftes leave namare þen neomen 
þet ye ne seggen him fore as of oþre þinges kun oþer cuþþe hu ofte ye 
undervengen hu longe ye edheolden Tendre of cun ne limpeþ nawt ancre beonne 
A mon wes of religiun ant com to him efter help his fleschliche broþer ant he 
tahte him to his þridde breþer þe wes dead biburiet þe ondswerede wundrinde 
 Nai quoþ he nis he dead Ant ich quoþ þe hali mon am dead gasteliche 
Na fleschlich freond ne easki me fleschlich frovre Amites ant parures worldliche 
leafdis mahen inoh wurchen Ant yef ye ham makieþ ne makie ye þe rof na 
mustreisun Veinegloire attreþ alle gode þeawes ant alle gode werkes Criblin 
ne schal nan of ow for luve ne for hure Taveles ne forbeode ich nawt yef sum 
riveþ surpliz oþer meassekemese Oþre rivunges ne rive ha nawt nomeliche 
overegede bute for muche neode 
Helpeþ ow wiþ ower ahne swinc se forþ se ye eaver mahen to schruden ow
seolven ant feden yef neod is ant þeo þe ow serviþ 
As Sein Jerome leareþ ne beo ye neaver longe ne lihtliche of sum þing allunges 
idel for ananrihtes þe feond beot hire his werc þe i Godes werc ne swinkeþ 
ant tuteleþ anan toward hire for hwil he siþ hire bisi he þencheþ þus For 
nawt ich schulde nu cume neh hire ne mei ha nawt iyemen to lustni mi lare Of 
idelnesse awakeneþ muchel flesches fondunge þet is Sodomes cwedschipe com of idelnesse ant of ful wombe 
Irn þet liþ stille gedereþ sone rust Weater þe ne stureþ nawt readliche stinkeþ 
Ancre ne schal nawt forwurþe scolmeistre ne turnen ancrehus to childrene 
scole Hire meiden mei learen sum oþer meiden þet were pliht of to leornin among 
wepmen oþer bimong gromes ah ancre ne ah to yemen bute Godd ane þah bi 
hire meistres read ha mei sum rihten ant helpen to learen 
Ye ne schulen senden leattres ne undervon leattres ne writen bute leave 
Ye schulen beon idoddet oþer yef ye wulleþ ischaven fowr siþen i þe yer 
to lihtin ower heaved beo bi þe her ieveset hwase swa is leovere ant as 
ofte ileten blod ant yef neod is oftre þe mei beo þerbuten ich hit mei wel 
þolien Hwen ye beoþ al greiþe ilete blod ye ne schule don na þing þe þreo 
dahes þet ow greveþ ah talkiþ to ower meidnes ant wiþ þeawfule talen schurteþ 
ow togederes Ye mahen swa don ofte hwen ow þuncheþ hevie oþer beoþ for 
sum worltlich þing sare oþer seke þah euch worltlich frovre is unwurþe to 
ancre 
Swa wisliche witeþ ow in ower blodletunge ant haldeþ ow i swuch reste þet 
ye longe þe refter mahen i Godes servise þe monluker swinken ant alswa hwen 
ye feleþ eani secnesse Muchel sotschipe hit is leosen for an dei tene oþer tweolve 
Wesscheþ ow hwerse neod is as ofte as ye wulleþ ant ower oþre þinges 
nes neaver fulþe Godd leof þah poverte ant unorneschipe beon him licwurþe 
Understondeþ eaver of alle þeose þinges þet nan nis heast ne forbod þet 
beoþ of þe uttre riwle þet is lute strengþe of forhwon þet te inre beo wel i
wist as ich seide i þe frumþe þeos mei beon ichanget hwerse eani neod oþer 
eani skile hit easkeþ efter þet ha best mei þe leafdi riwle servin as hire eadmode 
þuften Ah sikerliche wiþuten hire þe leafdi feareþ to wundre 
Ancre þe naveþ nawt neh honde hire fode beoþ bisie twa wummen an eaver 
þe leave ed hame an oþer þe wende ut hwenne driveþ neod ant þeo beo ful 
unorne wiþuten euch tiffunge oþer a lutel þuftene oþer of feier ealde Bi þe 
wei as ha geaþ ga singinde hire beoden ne ne halde na tale wiþ mon ne wiþ 
wummon ne sitte ne ne stonde bute þet leaste þet ha eaver mei ear þen ha ham 
cume Nohwider elles ne ga heo bute þider as me send hire Wiþute leave ne 
ne eote ha ne ne drinke ute þe oþer beo eaver inne ne wiþute þe yeten ne ga 
wiþute leave Ba beon obedient to hare dame in alle þing bute i sunne ane Na 
þing nabben þet heo hit nute ne undervo na þing ne ne yeove nowþer wiþuten 
hire leave Na mon ne leoten in ne þe yungre ne speoke wiþ namon bute leave 
ne ga ha nawt ut of tune wiþuten siker fere Yef hit swa mei beon ne ne ligge 
ute Yef heo ne con o boke segge bi ant bi hire ures ant 
wurche þet me hat hire wiþute gruchunge Habbe eaver hire earen opene toward 
hire dame Nowþer of þe wummen ne beore from hare dame ne ne bringe to 
hire nane idele talen ne neowe tidinges ne bitweonen hamseolf ne singen ne ne 
speoken nane worldliche spechen ne lahhen swa ne pleien þet ei mon þet hit 
sehe mahte hit to uvel turnen 
Over alle þinges leasunges ant luþere wordes heatien Hare her beo icorven 
hare heavedclaþ sitte lahhe Eiþer ligge ane Hare cop beo hehe isticchet ant 
bute broche Na mon ne seo ham unleppet ne openheaved Lah locunge habben 
Heo ne schulen cussen na mon ne cuþmon ne cunnesmon ne for na cuþþe 
cluppen ne weschen hare heaved ne lokin feaste o na mon ne toggin wiþ ne 
pleien Hare weden beon of swuch schape ant al hare aturn swuch þet hit beo 
edscene hwerto ha beoþ iturnde Hare lates lokin warliche þet nan ne mahe 
edwiten ham in hus ne ut of hus On alle wise forbeoren to wreaþen hare dame 
ant as ofte as heo hit doþ ear ha drinken oþer eoten makien hare o cneon 
dun bivoren hire ant seggen ant undervon þe penitence þet ha leiþ 
upon hire lutinde hire lahe þe ancre þe refter neaver mare þet ilke gult ne 
upbreide for na wreaþþe bute yef ha eft sone falle i þet ilke ah do hit allunge ut 
of hire heorte Yef ei strif ariseþ bitweone þe wummen þe ancre makie eiþer to 
makien oþer o cneon to þer eorþe ant eiþer rihte up oþer ant cussen on 
ende ant te ancre legge on eiþer sum penitence mare upo þe ilke þe greatluker 
gulte þis is a þing witen ha wel þet is Gode leovest sahtnesse ant some 
 ant te feond laþest Forþi he is eaver umben to arearen sum leaþþe Nu siþ 
þe sweoke wel þet hwen fur is wel o brune ant me wule þet hit aga me sundreþ 
þe brondes ant he deþ on hond þet ilke Luve is Jesu Cristes fur þet he wule 
þet bleasie aa i þin heorte ant te deovel blaweþ forte puffen hit ut Hwen his 
blawunge ne geineþ nawt he bringeþ up sum uvel word oþer sum oþer 
nohtunge hwerþurh ha tohurten eiþer frommard oþer ant te Hali Gastes fur 
cwencheþ hwen þe brondes þurh wreaþþe beoþ isundret Forþi halden ham 
i luve feaste togederes Ant ne beo ham nawt of hwen þe feond blawe nomeliche 
yef monie beon iveiet somet ant wel wiþ luve ontende þah þe ancre on hire 
meidnes for openliche gultes legge penitence to þe preost noþeleater schriven 
ham hwen neod is ah eaver þah wiþ leave 
Yef ha ne cunnen nawt þe metegraces seggen in hare stude 
bivoren ant ant efter mete alswa ant a mare ant segge þus 
on ende Feader Sune Hali Gast an almihti Godd yeove ure dame his grace 
se lengre se mare ant leve hire ant us ba neomen god ende Foryelde alle þe us 
god doþ ant milci hare sawle þe us god idon habbeþ hare sawle ant alle 
Cristene sawles 
Bitweone mel ne gruseli nawt nowþer frut ne oþerhwet ne drinken bute leave 
ant te leave beo liht in al þet nis sunne Ed te mete na word oþer lut ant teo 
stille Alswa efter þe ancre Complie aþet Prime ne don na þing ne seggen 
hwerþurh hire silence mahe beon isturbet 
Nan ancre servant ne ahte bi rihte to easkin iset hure bute mete ant claþ þet 
ha mei flutte bi ant Godes milce Ne misleve nan Godd hwetse tide of þe 
ancre þet he hire trukie þe meidnes wiþuten yef ha serviþ þe ancre alswa 
as ha ahen hare hure schal beon þe hehe blisse of heovene Hwase haveþ ehe of 
hope toward se heh hure gleadliche wule ha servin ant lihtliche alle wa ant alle 
teone þolien wiþ eise ant wiþ este ne buþ me nawt blisse 
Ye ancres ahen þis leaste stucche reden to ower wummen euche wike eanes 
aþet ha hit cunnen Ant muche neod is þet ye neomen to ham muche yeme for ye 
mahen muchel beon þurh ham igodet ant iwurset On oþer half yef þet ha 
sungiþ þurh ower yemeles ye schule beo bicleopet þe rof bivore þe hehe deme 
ant forþi as ow is muche neod ant ham yet mare yeornliche leareþ ham to 
halden hare riwle ba for ow ant for hamseolf liþeliche ant luveliche for swuch 
ah wummone lare to beonne luvelich ant liþe ant selthwenne sturne Ba is riht 
þet ha ow dreden ant luvien ant þah þet ter beo eaver mare of luve þen of 
drede þenne schal hit wel fearen Me schal healden eoli ant win ba i wunden 
efter Godes lare ah mare of softe eoli þen of bitinde win þet is mare of liþe 
wordes þen of suhinde for þerof kimeþ þinge best þet is luve eie Lihtliche 
ant sweteliche foryeoveþ ham hare gultes hwen ha ham icnaweþ ant bihateþ 
bote 
As forþ as ye mahen of mete ant of claþes ant of oþre þinges þet neode of 
flesch easkeþ beoþ large toward ham þah ye nearowe beon ant hearde to ow
seolven Swa deþ þe wel blaweþ went te nearewe of þe horn to his ahne muþ 
ant utward þet wide Ant ye don alswa as ye wulleþ þet ower beoden bemin 
wel ant dremen i Drihtines earen nawt ane to ower ahnes ah to alle folkes heale 
 as ure Laverd leve þurh þe grace of himseolf þet hit swa mote amen 
Hwen ower sustres meidnes cumeþ to ow to frovre cumeþ to ham to þe þurl 
earunder ant overunder eanes oþer twien ant gaþ ayein sone to ower note 
gastelich ne bivore Complie ne sitte ye nawt for ham over riht time swa þet hare 
cume beo na lure of ower religiun ah gastelich biyete Yef þer is eani word iseid 
þet mahte hurten heorte ne beo hit nawt iboren ut ne ibroht to oþer ancre þet 
is eþhurte To him hit schal beon iseid þe lokeþ ham alle Twa niht is inoh 
þet ei beo edhalden ant þet beo ful seldene ne for heom ne breoke silence ed te 
wmete ne for blodletunge bute yef sum muche god oþer neod hit makie 
þe ancre ne hire meiden ne plohien nane worldliche gomenes ed te þurle ne 
ne ticki togederes for ase seiþ Seint Beornard unwurþe þing is to euch gastelich 
mon ant nomeliche to ancre euch swuch fleschlich frovre ant hit binimeþ 
gastelich þet is wiþute met utnume murhþe ant þet is uvel change as is i
seid þe ruppe 
Of þis boc redeþ hwen ye beoþ eise euche dei leasse oþer mare Ich hopie 
þet hit schal beon ow yef ye hit redeþ ofte swiþe biheve þurh Godes muchele 
grace elles ich hefde uvele bitohe mi muchele hwile Me were leovere Godd hit 
wite do me toward Rome þen forte biginnen hit eft forte donne Yef ye findeþ 
þet ye doþ alswa as ye redeþ þonckiþ Godd yeorne yef ye ne doþ nawt 
biddeþ Godes are ant beoþ umben þeronuven þet ye hit bet halden efter ower 
mihte 
Feader Sune Hali Gast an almihti Godd wite ow in his warde He gleadie 
ow ant frovri ow mine leove sustren ant for al þet ye for him dreheþ ant dreaieþ 
ne yeove ow neaver leasse þen al togedere himseolven Beo he aa iheiet from 
world into world aa on ecnesse AMEN 
Ase ofte as ye habbeþ ired eawiht heron greteþ þe Leafdi wiþ an for 
him þet swonc herabuten Inoh meaþful ich am þe bidde se lutel 
Iþench on þi writere i þine beoden sumchearre ne beo hit ne se lutel hit 
turneþ þe to gode þet tu bidest for oþre
